诗篇 Psalms

不从恶人的计谋，不站罪人的道路，不坐亵慢人的座位。
Happy is the man who does not go in the company of sinners, or take his place in the way of evil-doers, or in the seat of those who do not give honour to the Lord.

惟喜爱耶和华的律法，昼夜思想，这人便为有福。
But whose delight is in the law of the Lord, and whose mind is on his law day and night.

他要像一棵树栽在溪水旁，按时候结果子，叶子也不枯干。凡他所作的，尽都顺利。
He will be like a tree planted by the rivers of water, which gives its fruit at the right time, whose leaves will ever be green; and he will do well in all his undertakings.

恶人并不是这样，乃像糠秕被风吹散。
The evil-doers are not so; but are like the dust from the grain, which the wind takes away.

因此当审判的时候，恶人必站立不住，罪人在义人的会中，也是如此。
For this cause there will be no mercy for sinners when they are judged, and the evil-doers will have no place among the upright,

因为耶和华知道义人的道路。恶人的道路，却必灭亡。
Because the Lord sees the way of the upright, but the end of the sinner is destruction.

外邦为什么争闹，万民为什么谋算虚妄的事。
Why are the nations so violently moved, and why are the thoughts of the people so foolish?

世上的君王一齐起来，臣宰一同商议，要敌挡耶和华，并他的受膏者，
The kings of the earth have taken their place, and the rulers are fixed in their purpose, against the Lord, and against the king of his selection, saying,

说，我们要挣开他们的捆绑，脱去他们的绳索。
Let their chains be broken, and their cords taken from off us.

那坐在天上的必发笑。主必嗤笑他们。
Then he whose seat is in the heavens will be laughing: the Lord will make sport of them.

那时他要在怒中责备他们，在烈怒中惊吓他们，
Then will his angry words come to their ears, and by his wrath they will be troubled:

说，我已经立我的君在锡安我的圣山上了。
But I have put my king on my holy hill of Zion.

受膏者说，我要传圣旨。耶和华曾对我说，你是我的儿子，我今日生你。
I will make clear the Lord's decision: he has said to me, You are my son, this day have I given you being.

你求我，我就将列国赐你为基业，将地极赐你为田产。
Make your request to me, and I will give you the nations for your heritage, and the farthest limits of the earth will be under your hand.

你必用铁杖打破他们。你必将他们如同窑匠的瓦器摔碎。
They will be ruled by you with a rod of iron; they will be broken like a potter's vessel.

现在你们君王应当省悟。你们世上的审判官该受管教。
So now be wise, you kings: take his teaching, you judges of the earth.

当存畏惧事奉耶和华，又当存战兢而快乐。
Give worship to the Lord with fear, kissing his feet and giving him honour,

当以嘴亲子，恐怕他发怒，你们便在道中灭亡，因为他的怒气快要发作。凡投靠他的，都是有福的。
For fear that he may be angry, causing destruction to come on you, because he is quickly moved to wrath. Happy are all those who put their faith in him.

（大卫逃避他儿子押沙龙的时候作的诗。）耶和华阿，我的敌人何其加增。有许多人起来攻击我。
<A Psalm. Of David. When he went in flight from Absalom his son.> Lord, how greatly are they increased who make attacks on me! in great numbers they come against me.

有许多人议论我说，他得不着神的帮助。（细拉）
Unnumbered are those who say of my soul, There is no help for him in God. (Selah.)

但你耶和华是我四围的盾牌。是我的荣耀，又是叫我抬起头来的。
But your strength, O Lord, is round me, you are my glory and the lifter up of my head.

我用我的声音求告耶和华，他就从他的圣山上应允我。（细拉）
I send up a cry to the Lord with my voice, and he gives me an answer from his holy hill. (Selah.)

我躺下睡觉。我醒着。耶和华都保佑我。
I took my rest in sleep, and then again I was awake; for the Lord was my support.

虽有成万的百姓来周围攻击我，我也不怕。
I will have no fear, though ten thousand have come round me, putting themselves against me.

耶和华阿，求你起来。我的神阿，求你救我。因为你打了我一切仇敌的腮骨，敲碎了恶人的牙齿。
Come to me, Lord; keep me safe, O my God; for you have given all my haters blows on their face-bones; the teeth of the evil-doers have been broken by you.

救恩属乎耶和华。愿你赐福给你的百姓。（细拉）
Salvation comes from the Lord; your blessing is on your people. (Selah.)

（大卫的诗，交与伶长。用丝弦的乐器。）显我为义的神阿，我呼吁的时候，求你应允我。我在困苦中，你曾使我宽广。现在求你怜恤我，听我的祷告。
<To the chief music-maker on corded instruments. A Psalm. Of David.> Give answer to my cry, O God of my righteousness; make me free from my troubles; have mercy on me, and give ear to my prayer.

你们这上流人哪，你们将我的尊荣变为羞辱，要到几时呢你们喜爱虚妄，寻找虚假，要到几时呢？（细拉）
O you sons of men, how long will you go on turning my glory into shame? how long will you give your love to foolish things, going after what is false? (Selah.)

你们要知道耶和华已经分别虔诚人归他自己。我求告耶和华，他必听我。
See how the Lord has made great his mercy for me; the Lord will give ear to my cry.

你们应当畏惧，不可犯罪。在床上的时候，要心里思想，并要肃静。（细拉）
Let there be fear in your hearts, and do no sin; have bitter feelings on your bed, but make no sound. (Selah.)

当献上公义的祭，又当倚靠耶和华。
Give the offerings of righteousness, and put your faith in the Lord.

有许多人说，谁能指示我们什么好处。耶和华阿，求你仰起脸来，光照我们。
There are numbers who say, Who will do us any good? the light of his face has gone from us.

你使我心里快乐，胜过那丰收五谷新酒的人。
Lord, you have put joy in my heart, more than they have when their grain and their wine are increased.

我必安然躺下睡觉，因为独有你耶和华使我安然居住。
I will take my rest on my bed in peace, because you only, Lord, keep me safe.

（大卫的诗，交与伶长。用吹的乐器。）耶和华阿，求你留心听我的言语，顾念我的心思。
<To the chief music-maker on wind instruments. A Psalm. Of David.> Give ear to my words, O Lord; give thought to my heart-searchings.

我的王我的神阿，求你垂听我呼求的声音。因为我向你祈祷。
Let the voice of my cry come to you, my King and my God; for to you will I make my prayer.

耶和华阿，早晨你必听我的声音。早晨我必向你陈明我的心意，并要儆醒。
My voice will come to you in the morning, O Lord; in the morning will I send my prayer to you, and keep watch.

因为你不是喜悦恶事的神。恶人不能与你同居。
For you are not a God who takes pleasure in wrongdoing; there is no evil with you.

狂傲人不能站在你眼前。凡作孽的，都是你所恨恶的。
The sons of pride have no place before you; you are a hater of all workers of evil.

说谎言的，你必灭绝。好流人血弄诡诈的，都为耶和华所憎恶。
You will send destruction on those whose words are false; the cruel man and the man of deceit are hated by the Lord.

至于我，我必凭你丰盛的慈爱进入你的居所。我必存敬畏你的心向你的圣殿下拜。
But as for me, I will come into your house, in the full measure of your mercy; and in your fear I will give worship, turning my eyes to your holy Temple.

耶和华阿，求你因我的仇敌，凭你的公义，引领我。使你的道路在我面前正直。
Be my guide, O Lord, in the ways of your righteousness, because of those who are against me; make your way straight before my face.

因为他们的口中没有诚实。他们的心里满有邪恶。他们的喉咙，是敞开的坟墓。他们用舌头谄媚人。
For no faith may be put in their words; their inner part is nothing but evil; their throat is like an open place for the dead; smooth are the words of their tongues.

神阿，求你定他们的罪。愿他们因自己的计谋跌倒。愿你在他们许多的过犯中，把他们逐出。因为他们背叛了你。
Send them to destruction, O Lord; let their evil designs be the cause of their fall; let them be forced out by all their sins; because they have gone against your authority.

凡投靠你的，愿他们喜乐，时常欢呼，因为你护庇他们。又愿那爱你名的人，都靠你欢欣。
But let all those who put their faith in you be glad with cries of joy at all times, and let all the lovers of your name be glad in you.

因为你必赐福与义人。耶和华阿，你必用恩惠如同盾牌四面护卫他。
For you, Lord, will send a blessing on the upright man; your grace will be round him, and you will be his strength.

（大卫的诗，交与伶长。用丝弦的乐器，调用第八。）耶和华阿，求你不要在怒中责备我，也不要在烈怒中惩罚我。
<To the chief music-maker on corded instruments, on the Sheminith. A Psalm. Of David.> O Lord, do not be bitter with me in your wrath; do not send punishment on me in the heat of your passion.

耶和华阿，求你可怜我。因为我软弱。耶和华阿，求你医治我。因为我的骨头发战。
Have mercy on me, O Lord, for I am wasted away: make me well, for even my bones are troubled.

我心也大大地惊惶。耶和华阿，你要到几时才救我呢？
My soul is in bitter trouble; and you, O Lord, how long?

耶和华阿，求你转回，搭救我。因你的慈爱拯救我。
Come back, O Lord, make my soul free; O give me salvation because of your mercy.

因为在死地无人记念你，在阴间有谁称谢你。
For in death there is no memory of you; in the underworld who will give you praise?

我因唉哼而困乏。我每夜流泪，把床榻漂起，把褥子湿透。
The voice of my sorrow is a weariness to me; all the night I make my bed wet with weeping; it is watered by the drops flowing from my eyes.

我因忧愁眼睛干瘪。又因我一切的敌人眼睛昏花。
My eyes are wasting away with trouble; they are becoming old because of all those who are against me.

你们一切作孽的人，离开我吧。因为耶和华听了我哀哭的声音。
Go from me, all you workers of evil; for the Lord has given ear to the voice of my weeping.

耶和华听了我的恳求。耶和华必收纳我的祷告。
The Lord has given ear to my request; the Lord has let my prayer come before him.

我的一切仇敌都必羞愧，大大惊惶。他们必要退后，忽然羞愧。
Let all those who are against me be shamed and deeply troubled; let them be turned back and suddenly put to shame.

（大卫指着便雅悯人古实的话，向耶和华唱的流离歌。）耶和华我的神阿，我投靠你。求你救我脱离一切追赶我的人，将我救拔出来。
<Shiggaion of David; a song which he made to the Lord, about the words of Cush the Benjamite.> O Lord my God, I put my faith in you; take me out of the hands of him who is cruel to me, and make me free;

恐怕他们像狮子撕裂我，甚至撕碎，无人搭救。
So that he may not come rushing on my soul like a lion, wounding it, while there is no one to be my saviour.

耶和华我的神阿，我若行了这事，若有罪孽在我手里，
O Lord my God, if I have done this; if my hands have done any wrong;

我若以恶报那与我交好的人，连那无故与我为敌的，我也救了他，
If I have given back evil to him who did evil to me, or have taken anything from him who was against me without cause;

就任凭仇敌追赶我，直到追上。将我的性命踏在地下，使我的荣耀归于灰尘。（细拉）
Let my hater go after my soul and take it; let my life be crushed to the earth, and my honour into the dust. (Selah.)

耶和华阿，求你在怒中起来，挺身而立，抵挡我敌人的暴怒。求你为我兴起。你已经命定施行审判。
Come up, Lord, in your wrath; be lifted up against my haters; be awake, my God, give orders for the judging.

愿众民的会环绕你。愿你从其上归于高位。
The meeting of the nations will be round you; take your seat, then, over them, on high.

耶和华向众民施行审判。耶和华阿，求你按我的公义，和我心中的纯正，判断我。
The Lord will be judge of the peoples; give a decision for me, O Lord, because of my righteousness, and let my virtue have its reward.

愿恶人的恶断绝。愿你坚立义人。因为公义的神察验人的心肠肺腑。
O let the evil of the evil-doer come to an end, but give strength to the upright: for men's minds and hearts are tested by the God of righteousness.

神是我的盾牌。他拯救心里正直的人。
God, who is the saviour of the upright in heart, is my breastplate.

神是公义的审判者，又是天天向恶人发怒的神。
God is the judge of the upright, and is angry with the evil-doers every day.

若有人不回头，他的刀必磨快。弓必上弦，预备妥当了。
If a man is not turned from his evil, he will make his sword sharp; his bow is bent and ready.

他也预备了杀人的器械。他所射的是火箭。
He has made ready for him the instruments of death; he makes his arrows flames of fire.

试看恶人因奸恶而劬劳。所怀的是毒害，所生的是虚假。
That man is a worker of evil; the seed of wrongdoing has given birth to deceit.

他掘了坑，又挖深了，竟掉在自己所挖的阱里。
He has made a hole deep in the earth, and is falling into the hole which he has made

他的毒害，必临到他自己的头上。他的强暴必落到他自己的脑袋上。
His wrongdoing will come back to him, and his violent behaviour will come down on his head.

我要照着耶和华的公义称谢他，歌颂耶和华至高者的名。
I will give praise to the Lord for his righteousness; I will make a song to the name of the Lord Most High.

（大卫的诗，交与伶长。用迦特乐器。）耶和华我们的主阿，你的名在全地何其美。你将你的荣耀彰显于天。
<To the chief music-maker on the Gittith. A Psalm. Of David.> O Lord, our Lord, whose glory is higher than the heavens, how noble is your name in all the earth!

你因敌人的缘故，从婴孩和吃奶的口中，建立了能力，使仇敌和报仇的，闭口无言。
You have made clear your strength even out of the mouths of babies at the breast, because of those who are against you; so that you may put to shame the cruel and violent man.

我观看你指头所造的天，并你所陈设的月亮星宿，
When I see your heavens, the work of your fingers, the moon and the stars, which you have put in their places;

便说，人算什么，你竟顾念他。世人算什么，你竟眷顾他。
What is man, that you keep him in mind? the son of man, that you take him into account?

你叫他比天使（或作神）微小一点，并赐他荣耀尊贵为冠冕。
For you have made him only a little lower than the gods, crowning him with glory and honour.

你派他管理你手所造的，使万物，就是一切的牛羊，田野的兽，空中的鸟，海里的鱼，凡经行海道的，都服在他的脚下。
You have made him ruler over the works of your hands; you have put all things under his feet;


All sheep and oxen, and all the beasts of the field;


The birds of the air and the fish of the sea, and whatever goes through the deep waters of the seas.

耶和华我们的主阿，你的名在全地何其美。
O Lord, our Lord, how noble is your name in all the earth!

（大卫的诗，交与伶长。调用慕拉便。）我要一心称谢耶和华。我要传扬你一切奇妙的作为。
<To the chief music-maker on Muthlabben. A Psalm. Of David.> I will give you praise, O Lord, with all my heart; I will make clear all the wonder of your works.

我要因你欢喜快乐。至高者阿，我要歌颂你的名。
I will be glad and have delight in you: I will make a song of praise to your name, O Most High.

我的仇敌转身退去的时候，他们一见你的面，就跌倒灭亡。
When my haters are turned back, they will be broken and overcome before you.

因你已经为我伸冤，为我辨屈。你坐在宝座上，按公义审判。
For you gave approval to my right and my cause; you were seated in your high place judging in righteousness.

你曾斥责外邦。你曾灭绝恶人。你曾涂抹他们的名，直到永永远远。
You have said sharp words to the nations, you have sent destruction on the sinners, you have put an end to their name for ever and ever.

仇敌到了尽头。他们被毁坏，直到永远。你拆毁他们的城邑。连他们的名号，都归于无有。
You have given their towns to destruction; the memory of them has gone; they have become waste for ever.

惟耶和华坐着为王，直到永远。他已经为审判设摆他的宝座。
But the Lord is King for ever: he has made ready his high seat for judging.

他要按公义审判世界，按正直判断万民。
And he will be the judge of the world in righteousness, giving true decisions for the peoples.

耶和华又要给受欺压的人作高台，在患难的时候作高台。
The Lord will be a high tower for those who are crushed down, a high tower in times of trouble;

耶和华阿，认识你名的人要倚靠你。因你没有离弃寻求你的人。
And those who have knowledge of your name will put their faith in you; because you, Lord, have ever given your help to those who were waiting for you.

应当歌颂居锡安的耶和华，将他所行的传扬在众民中。
Make songs of praise to the Lord, whose house is in Zion: make his doings clear to the people.

因为那追讨流人血之罪的，他记念受屈的人，不忘记困苦人的哀求。
When he makes search for blood, he has them in his memory: he is not without thought for the cry of the poor.

耶和华阿，你是从死门把我提拔起来的。求你怜恤我。看那恨我的人所加给我的苦难。
Have mercy on me, O Lord, and see how I am troubled by my haters; let me be lifted up from the doors of death;

好叫我述说你一切的美德。我必在锡安城的门（城原文作女子），因你的救恩欢乐。
So that I may make clear all your praise in the house of the daughter of Zion: I will be glad because of your salvation.

外邦人陷在自己所掘的坑中。他们的脚，在自己暗设的网罗里缠住了。
The nations have gone down into the hole which they made: in their secret net is their foot taken.

耶和华已将自己显明了，他已施行审判。恶人被自己手所作的缠住了（或作他叫恶人被自己手所作的累住了）。（细拉）
The Lord has given knowledge of himself through his judging: the evil-doer is taken in the net which his hands had made. (Higgaion. Selah.)

恶人，就是忘记神的外邦人，都必归到阴间。
The sinners and all the nations who have no memory of God will be turned into the underworld.

穷乏人必不永久被忘，困苦人的指望，必不永远落空。
For the poor will not be without help; the hopes of those in need will not be crushed for ever.

耶和华阿，求你起来，不容人得胜。愿外邦人在你面前受审判。
Up! O Lord; let not man overcome you: let the nations be judged before you.

耶和华阿，求你使外邦人恐惧。愿他们知道自己不过是人。（细拉）
Put them in fear, O Lord, so that the nations may see that they are only men. (Selah.)

耶和华阿，你为什么站在远处。在患难的时候，为什么隐藏。
Why do you keep far away, O Lord? why are you not to be seen in times of trouble?

恶人在骄横中，把困苦人追得火急。愿他们陷在自己所设的计谋里。
The evil-doer in his pride is cruel to the poor; let him be taken by the tricks of his invention.

因为恶人以心愿自夸。贪财的背弃耶和华，并且轻慢他（或作他祝福贪财的，却轻慢耶和华）。
For the evil-doer is lifted up because of the purpose of his heart, and he whose mind is fixed on wealth is turned away from the Lord, saying evil against him.

恶人面带骄傲，说，耶和华必不追究。他一切所想的，都以为没有神。
The evil-doer in his pride says, God will not make a search. All his thoughts are, There is no God.

凡他所作的，时常稳固。你的审判超过他的眼界。至于他一切的敌人，他都向他们喷气。
His ways are ever fixed; your decisions are higher than he may see: as for his haters, they are as nothing to him.

他心里说，我必不动摇，世世代代不遭灾难。
He has said in his heart, I will not be moved: through all generations I will never be in trouble.

他满口是咒骂，诡诈，欺压。舌底是毒害奸恶。
His mouth is full of cursing and deceit and false words: under his tongue are evil purposes and dark thoughts.

他在村庄埋伏等候。他在隐密处杀害无辜的人。他的眼睛窥探无倚无靠的人。
He is waiting in the dark places of the towns: in the secret places he puts to death those who have done no wrong: his eyes are secretly turned against the poor.

他埋伏在暗地，如狮子蹲在洞中。他埋伏，要掳去困苦人。他拉网，就把困苦人掳去。
He keeps himself in a secret place like a lion in his hole, waiting to put his hands on the poor man, and pulling him into his net.

他屈身蹲伏，无倚无靠的人，就倒在他爪牙之下（爪牙或作强暴人），
The upright are crushed and made low, and the feeble are overcome by his strong ones.

他心里说，神竟忘记了。他掩面，永不观看。
He says in his heart, God has no memory of me: his face is turned away; he will never see it.

耶和华阿，求你起来。神阿，求你举手。不要忘记困苦人。
Up! O Lord; let your hand be lifted: give thought to the poor.

恶人为何轻慢神，心里说，你必不追究。
Why has the evil-doer a low opinion of God, saying in his heart, You will not make search for it?

其实你已经观看。因为奸恶毒害，你都看见了，为要以手施行报应。无倚无靠的人，把自己交托你。你向来是帮助孤儿的。
You have seen it; for your eyes are on sorrow and grief, to take it into your hand: the poor man puts his faith in you; you have been the helper of the child who has no father.

愿你打断恶人的膀臂。至于坏人，愿你追究他的恶，直到净尽。
Let the arm of the sinner and the evil-doer be broken; go on searching for his sin till there is no more.

耶和华永永远远为王。外邦人从他的地已经灭绝了。
The Lord is King for ever and ever; the nations are gone from his land.

耶和华阿，谦卑人的心愿，你早已知道（原文作听见）。你必预备他们的心，也必侧耳听他们的祈求。
Lord, you have given ear to the prayer of the poor: you will make strong their hearts, you will give them a hearing:

为要给孤儿和受欺压的人伸冤，使强横的人不再威吓他们。
To give decision for the child without a father and for the broken-hearted, so that the man of the earth may no longer be feared.

（大卫的诗，交与伶长。）我是投靠耶和华。你们怎么对我说，你当像鸟飞往你的山去。
<For the chief music-maker. Of David.> In the Lord put I my faith; how will you say to my soul, Go in flight like a bird to the mountain?

看哪，恶人弯弓，把箭搭在弦上，要在暗中射那心里正直的人。
See, the bows of the evil-doers are bent, they make ready their arrows on the cord, so that they may send them secretly against the upright in heart.

根基若毁坏，义人还能作什么呢？
If the bases are broken down, what is the upright man to do?

耶和华在他的圣殿里，耶和华的宝座在天上。他的慧眼察看世人。
The Lord is in his holy Temple, the Lord's seat is in heaven; his eyes are watching and testing the children of men.

耶和华试验义人。惟有恶人和喜爱强暴的人，他心里恨恶。
The Lord puts the upright and the sinner to the test, but he has hate in his soul for the lover of violent acts.

他要向恶人密布网罗。有烈火，硫磺，热风，作他们杯中的分。
On the evil-doer he will send down fire and flames, and a burning wind; with these will their cup be full.

因为耶和华是公义的。他喜爱公义。正直人必得见他的面。
For the Lord is upright; he is a lover of righteousness: the upright will see his face.

（大卫的诗，交与伶长。调用第八。）耶和华阿，求你帮助，因虔诚人断绝了。世人中间的忠信人没有了。
<For the chief music-maker on the Sheminith. A Psalm. Of David.> Send help, Lord, for mercy has come to an end; there is no more faith among the children of men.

人人向邻舍说谎。他们说话，是嘴唇油滑，心口不一。
Everyone says false words to his neighbour: their tongues are smooth in their talk, and their hearts are full of deceit.

凡油滑的嘴唇，和夸大的舌头，耶和华必要剪除。
The smooth lips and the tongue of pride will be cut off by the Lord.

他们曾说，我们必能以舌头得胜。我们的嘴唇是我们自己的。谁能作我们的主呢？
They have said, With our tongues will we overcome; our lips are ours: who is lord over us?

耶和华说，因为困苦人的冤屈，和贫穷人的叹息，我现在要起来，把他安置在他所切慕的稳妥之地。
Because of the crushing of the poor and the weeping of those in need, now will I come to his help, says the Lord; I will give him the salvation which he is desiring.

耶和华的言语，是纯净的言语。如同银子在泥炉中炼过七次。
The words of the Lord are true words: like silver tested by fire and burned clean seven times.

耶和华阿，你必保护他们。你必保佑他们永远脱离这世代的人。
You will keep them, O Lord, you will keep them safe from this generation for ever.

下流人在世人中升高，就有恶人到处游行。
The sinners are walking on every side, and evil is honoured among the children of men.

（大卫的诗，交与伶长。）耶和华阿，你忘记我要到几时呢？要到永远吗？你掩面不顾我要到几时呢？
<To the chief music-maker. A Psalm. Of David.> Will you for ever put me out of your memory, O Lord? will your face for ever be turned away from me?

我心里筹算，终日愁苦，要到几时呢？我的仇敌升高压制我，要到几时呢？
How long is my soul to be in doubt, with sorrow in my heart all the day? how long will he who is against me be given power over me?

耶和华我的神阿，求你看顾我，应允我，使我眼目光明，免得我沉睡至死。
Let my voice come before you, and give me an answer, O Lord my God; let your light be shining on me, so that the sleep of death may not overtake me;

免得我的仇敌说，我胜了他。免得我的敌人在我摇动的时候喜乐。
And he who is against me may not say, I have overcome him; and those who are troubling me may not be glad when I am moved.

但我倚靠你的慈爱。我的心因你的救恩快乐。
But I have had faith in your mercy; my heart will be glad in your salvation.

我要向耶和华歌唱，因他用厚恩待我。
I will make a song to the Lord, because he has given me my reward.

（大卫的诗，交与伶长。）愚顽人心里说，没有神。他们都是邪恶，行了可憎恶的事。没有一个人行善。
<To the chief music-maker. Of David.> The foolish man has said in his heart, God will not do anything. They are unclean, they have done evil works; there is not one who does good.

耶和华从天上垂看世人，要看有明白的没有，有寻求神的没有。
The Lord was looking down from heaven on the children of men, to see if there were any who had wisdom, searching after God.

他们都偏离正路，一同变为污秽。并没有行善的，连一个也没有。
They have all gone out of the way together; they are unclean, there is not one who does good, no, not one.

作孽的都没有知识吗？他们吞吃我的百姓，如同吃饭一样，并不求告耶和华。
Have all the workers of evil no knowledge? they take my people for food as they would take bread; they make no prayer to the Lord.

他们在那里大大地害怕，因为神在义人的族类中。
Then were they in great fear: for God is in the generation of the upright.

你们叫困苦人的谋算，变为羞辱。然而耶和华是他的避难所。
You have put to shame the thoughts of the poor, but the Lord is his support.

但愿以色列的救恩从锡安而出。耶和华救回他被掳的子民，那时雅各要快乐，以色列要欢喜。
May the salvation of Israel come out of Zion! when the fate of his people is changed by the Lord, Jacob will have joy and Israel will be glad.

（大卫的诗。）耶和华阿，谁能寄居你的帐幕？谁能住在你的圣山？
<A Psalm. Of David.> Lord, who may have a resting-place in your tent, a living-place on your holy hill?

就是行为正直，作事公义，心里说实话的人。
He who goes on his way uprightly, doing righteousness, and saying what is true in his heart;

他不以舌头谗谤人，不恶待朋友，也不随伙毁谤邻里。
Whose tongue is not false, who does no evil to his friend, and does not take away the good name of his neighbour;

他眼中藐视匪类，却尊重那敬畏耶和华的人。他发了誓，虽然自己吃亏，也不更改。
Who gives honour to those who have the fear of the Lord, turning away from him who has not the Lord's approval. He who takes an oath against himself, and makes no change.

他不放债取利，不受贿赂以害无辜。行这些事的人，必永不动摇。
He who does not put out his money at interest, or for payment give false decisions against men who have done no wrong. He who does these things will never be moved.

（大卫的金诗。）神阿，求你保佑我，因为我投靠你。
<Michtam. Of David.> Keep me safe, O God: for in you I have put my faith.

我的心哪，你曾对耶和华说，你是我的主。我的好处不在你以外。
O my soul, you have said to the Lord, You are my Lord: I have no good but you.

论到世上的圣民，他们又美又善，是我最喜悦的。
As for the saints who are in the earth, they are the noble in whom is all my delight.

以别神代替耶和华的（或作送礼物给别神的），他们的愁苦必加增。他们所浇奠的血我不献上，我嘴唇也不提别神的名号。
Their sorrows will be increased who go after another god: I will not take drink offerings from their hands, or take their names on my lips.

耶和华是我的产业，是我杯中的分。我所得的你为我持守。
The Lord is my heritage and the wine of my cup; you are the supporter of my right.

用绳量给我的地界，坐落在佳美之处。我的产业实在美好。
Fair are the places marked out for me; I have a noble heritage.

我必称颂那指教我的耶和华。我的心肠在夜间也警戒我。
I will give praise to the Lord who has been my guide; knowledge comes to me from my thoughts in the night.

我将耶和华常摆在我面前。因他在我右边，我便不至摇动。
I have put the Lord before me at all times; because he is at my right hand, I will not be moved.

因此我的心欢喜，我的灵（原文作荣耀）快乐。我的肉身也要安然居住。
Because of this my heart is glad, and my glory is full of joy: while my flesh takes its rest in hope.

因为你必不将我的灵魂撇在阴间。也不叫你的圣者见朽坏。
For you will not let my soul be prisoned in the underworld; you will not let your loved one see the place of death.

你必将生命的道路指示我。在你面前有满足的喜乐。在你右手中有永远的福乐。
You will make clear to me the way of life; where you are joy is complete; in your right hand there are pleasures for ever and ever.

（大卫的祈祷。）耶和华阿，求你听闻公义，侧耳听我的呼吁。求你留心听我这不出于诡诈嘴唇的祈祷。
<A Prayer. Of David.> Let my cause come to your ears, O Lord, give attention to my cry; give ear to my prayer which goes not out from false lips.

愿我的判语从你面前发出。愿你的眼睛观看公正。
Be my judge; for your eyes see what is right.

你已经试验我的心。你在夜间鉴察我。你熬炼我，却找不着什么。我立志叫我口中没有过失。
You have put my heart to the test, searching me in the night; you have put me to the test and seen no evil purpose in me; I will keep my mouth from sin.

论到人的行为，我借着你嘴唇的言语，自己谨守，不行强暴人的道路。
As for the works of men, by the word of your lips I have kept myself from the ways of the violent.

我的脚踏定了你的路径，我的两脚未曾滑跌。
I have kept my feet in your ways, my steps have not been turned away.

神阿，我曾求告你，因为你必应允我。求你向我侧耳，听我的言语。
My cry has gone up to you, for you will give me an answer, O God: let your ear be turned to me, and give attention to my words.

求你显出你奇妙的慈爱来。你是那用右手拯救投靠你的，脱离起来攻击他们的人。
Make clear the wonder of your mercy, O saviour of those who put their faith in your right hand, from those who come out against them.

求你保护我，如同保护眼中的瞳人。将我隐藏在你翅膀的荫下，
Keep me as the light of your eyes, covering me with the shade of your wings,

使我脱离那欺压我的恶人，就是围困我，要害我命的仇敌。
From the evil-doers who are violent to me, and from those who are round me, desiring my death.

他们的心被脂油包裹。他们用口说骄傲的话。
They are shut up in their fat: with their mouths they say words of pride.

他们围困了我们的脚步。他们瞪着眼，要把我们推倒在地。
They have made a circle round our steps: their eyes are fixed on us, forcing us down to the earth;

他像狮子急要抓食，又像少壮狮子蹲伏在暗处。
Like a lion desiring its food, and like a young lion waiting in secret places.

耶和华阿，求你起来，前去迎敌，将他打倒。用你的刀救护我命脱离恶人。
Up! Lord, come out against him, make him low, with your sword be my saviour from the evil-doer.

耶和华阿，求你用手救我脱离世人，脱离那只在今生有福分的世人。你把你的财宝充满他们的肚腹。他们因有儿女就心满意足，将其余的财物留给他们的婴孩。
With your hand, O Lord, from men, even men of the world, whose heritage is in this life, and whom you make full with your secret wealth: they are full of children; after their death their offspring take the rest of their goods.

至于我，我必在义中见你的面。我醒了的时候，得见你的形像（见或作看），就心满意足了。
As for me, I will see your face in righteousness: when I am awake it will be joy enough for me to see your form.

（耶和华的仆人大卫的诗，交与伶长。当耶和华救他脱离一切仇敌和扫罗之手的日子，他向耶和华念这诗的话。说：）耶和华我的力量阿，我爱你。
<To the chief music-maker. Of the servant of the Lord, of David, who said the words of this song to the Lord on the day when the Lord made him free from the hand of all his haters, and from the hand of Saul; and he said,> I will give you my love, O Lord, my strength.

耶和华是我的岩石，我的山寨，我的救主，我的神，我的磐石，我所投靠的。他是我的盾牌，是拯救我的角，是我的高台。
The Lord is my Rock, my walled town, and my saviour; my God, my Rock, in him will I put my faith; my breastplate, and the horn of my salvation, and my high tower.

我要求告当赞美的耶和华。这样我必从仇敌手中被救出来。
I will send up my cry to the Lord, who is to be praised; so will I be made safe from those who are against me.

曾有死亡的绳索缠绕我。匪类的急流使我惊惧。
The cords of death were round me, and the seas of evil put me in fear.

阴间的绳索缠绕我。死亡的网罗临到我。
The cords of hell were round me: the nets of death came on me.

我在急难中求告耶和华，向我的神呼求。他从殿中听了我的声音，我在他面前的呼求入了他的耳中。
In my trouble my voice went up to the Lord, and my cry to my God: my voice came to his hearing in his holy Temple, and my prayer came before him, even into his ears.

那时因他发怒，地就摇撼战抖，山的根基也震动摇撼。
Then trouble and shock came on the earth; and the bases of the mountains were moved and shaking, because he was angry.

从他鼻孔冒烟上腾，从他口中发火焚烧。连炭也着了。
There went up a smoke from his nose, and a fire of destruction from his mouth: flames were lighted by it.

他又使天下垂，亲自降临。有黑云在他脚下。
The heavens were bent, so that he might come down; and it was dark under his feet.

他坐着基路伯飞行。他借着风的翅膀快飞。
And he went in flight through the air, seated on a storm-cloud: going quickly on the wings of the wind.

他以黑暗为藏身之处，以水的黑暗，天空的厚云，为他四围的行宫。
He made the dark his secret place; his tent round him was the dark waters and thick clouds of the skies.

因他面前的光辉，他的厚云行过。便有冰雹火炭。
Before his shining light his dark clouds went past, raining ice and fire.

耶和华也在天上打雷。至高者发出声音，便有冰雹火炭。
The Lord made thunder in the heavens, and the voice of the Highest was sounding out: a rain of ice and fire.

他射出箭来，使仇敌四散。多多发出闪电，使他们扰乱。
He sent out his arrows, driving them in all directions; by his flames of fire they were troubled.

耶和华阿，你的斥责一发，你鼻孔的气一出，海底就出现，大地的根基也显露。
Then the deep beds of the waters were seen, and the bases of the world were uncovered, because of your words of wrath, O Lord, because of the breath from your mouth.

他从高天伸手抓住我。把我从大水中拉上来。
He sent from on high, he took me, pulling me out of great waters.

他救我脱离我的劲敌，和那些恨我的人。因为他们比我强盛。
He made me free from my strong hater, and from those who were against me, because they were stronger than I.

我遭遇灾难的日子，他们来攻击我。但耶和华是我的倚靠。
They came on me in the day of my trouble; but the Lord was my support.

他又领我到宽阔之处。他救拔我，因他喜悦我。
He took me out into a wide place; he was my saviour because he had delight in me.

耶和华按着我的公义报答我，按着我手中的清洁赏赐我。
The Lord gives me the reward of my righteousness, because my hands are clean before him.

因为我遵守了耶和华的道，未曾作恶离开我的神。
For I have kept the ways of the Lord; I have not been turned away in sin from my God.

他的一切典章常在我面前。他的律例我也未曾丢弃。
For all his decisions were before me, and I did not put away his laws from me.

我在他面前作了完全人。我也保守自己远离我的罪孽。
And I was upright before him, and I kept myself from sin.

所以耶和华按我的公义，按我在他眼前手中的清洁，偿还我。
Because of this the Lord has given me the reward of my righteousness, because my hands are clean in his eyes.

慈爱的人，你以慈爱待他。完全的人，你以完全待他。
On him who has mercy you will have mercy; to the upright you will be upright;

清洁的人，你以清洁待他。乖僻的人，你以弯曲待他。
He who is holy will see that you are holy; but to the man whose way is not straight you will be a hard judge.

困苦的百姓，你必拯救。高傲的眼目，你必使他降卑。
For you are the saviour of those who are in trouble; but eyes full of pride will be made low.

你必点着我的灯。耶和华我的神必照明我的黑暗。
You, O Lord, will be my light; by you, my God, the dark will be made bright for me.

我借着你冲入敌军，借着我的神跳过墙垣。
By your help I have made a way through the wall which was shutting me in; by the help of my God I have gone over a wall.

至于神，他的道是完全的。耶和华的话是炼净的。凡投靠他的，他便作他们的盾牌。
As for God, his way is completely good; the word of the Lord is tested; he is a breastplate for all those who put their faith in him.

除了耶和华，谁是神呢？除了我们的神，谁是磐石呢？
For who is God but the Lord? or who is a Rock but our God?

惟有那以力量束我的腰，使我行为完全的，他是神。
God puts a strong band about me, guiding me in a straight way.

他使我的脚快如母鹿的蹄，又使我在高处安稳。
He makes my feet like roes' feet, and puts me on high places.

他教导我的手能以争战，甚至我的膀臂能开铜弓。
He makes my hands expert in war, so that a bow of brass is bent by my arms.

你把你的救恩给我作盾牌。你的右手扶持我。你的温和使我为大。
You have given me the breastplate of your salvation: your right hand has been my support, and your mercy has made me great.

你使我脚下的地步宽阔。我的脚未曾滑跌。
You have made my steps wide under me, so that my feet are kept from slipping.

我要追赶我的仇敌，并要追上他们。不将他们灭绝，我总不归回。
I go after my haters and overtake them; not turning back till they are all overcome.

我要打伤他们，使他们不能起来。他们必倒在我的脚下。
I will give them wounds, so that they are not able to get up: they are stretched under my feet.

因为你曾以力量束我的腰，使我能争战。你也使那起来攻击我的，都服在我以下。
For I have been armed by you with strength for the fight: you have made low under me those who come out against me.

你又使我的仇敌在我面前转背逃跑，叫我能以剪除那恨我的人。
By you their backs are turned in flight, so that my haters are cut off.

他们呼求，却无人拯救，就是呼求耶和华，他也不应允。
They were crying out, but there was no one to come to their help: even to the Lord, but he gave them no answer.

我捣碎他们，如同风前的灰尘，倒出他们，如同街上的泥土。
Then they were crushed as small as dust before the wind; they were drained out like the waste of the streets.

你救我脱离百姓的争竞，立我作列国的元首。我素不认识的民必事奉我。
You have made me free from the fightings of the people; you have made me the head of the nations: a people of whom I had no knowledge will be my servants.

他们一听见我的名声，就必顺从我。外邦人要投降我。
From the time when my name comes to their ears they will be ruled by me: men of other countries will, with false hearts, put themselves under my authority.

外邦人要衰残，战战兢兢地出他们的营寨。
They will be wasting away, they will come out of their secret places shaking with fear.

耶和华是活神。愿我的磐石被人称颂。愿救我的神被人尊崇。
The Lord is living; praise be to my Rock, and let the God of my salvation be honoured.

这位神，就是那为我伸冤，使众民服在我以下的。
It is God who sends punishment on my haters, and puts peoples under my rule.

你救我脱离仇敌。又把我举起，高过那些起来攻击我的。你救我脱离强暴的人。
He makes me free from my haters; I am lifted up over those who come up against me: you have made me free from the violent man.

耶和华阿，因此我要在外邦中称谢你，歌颂你的名。
Because of this I will give you praise, O Lord, among the nations, and will make a song of praise to your name.

耶和华赐极大的救恩给他所立的王，施慈爱给他的受膏者，就是给大卫和他的后裔，直到永远。
Great salvation does he give to his king; he has mercy on the king of his selection, David, and on his seed for ever.

（大卫的诗，交与伶长。）诸天述说神的荣耀，穹苍传扬他的手段。
<To the chief music-maker. A Psalm. Of David.> The heavens are sounding the glory of God; the arch of the sky makes clear the work of his hands.

这日到那日发出言语。这夜到那夜传出知识。
Day after day it sends out its word, and night after night it gives knowledge.

无言无语，也无声音可听。
There are no words or language; their voice makes no sound.

他的量带通遍天下，他的言语传到地极。神在其间为太阳安设帐幕。
Their line has gone out through all the earth, and their words to the end of the world. In them has he put a tent for the sun,

太阳如同新郎出洞房，又如勇士欢然奔路。
Who is like a newly married man coming from his bride-tent, and is glad like a strong runner starting on his way.

他从天这边出来，绕到天那边。没有一物被隐藏不得他的热气。
His going out is from the end of the heaven, and his circle to the ends of it; there is nothing which is not open to his heat.

耶和华的律法全备，能苏醒人心。耶和华的法度确定，能使愚人有智慧。
The law of the Lord is good, giving new life to the soul: the witness of the Lord is certain, giving wisdom to the foolish.

耶和华的训词正直，能快活人的心。耶和华的命令清洁，能明亮人的眼目。
The orders of the Lord are right, making glad the heart: the rule of the Lord is holy, giving light to the eyes.

耶和华的道理洁净，存到永远。耶和华的典章真实，全然公义。
The fear of the Lord is clean, and has no end; the decisions of the Lord are true and full of righteousness.

都比金子可羡慕，且比极多的精金可羡慕。比蜜甘甜，且比蜂房下滴的蜜甘甜。
More to be desired are they than gold, even than much shining gold; sweeter than the dropping honey.

况且你的仆人因此受警戒。守着这些便有大赏。
By them is your servant made conscious of danger, and in keeping them there is great reward.

谁能知道自己的错失呢？愿你赦免我隐而未现的过错。
Who has full knowledge of his errors? make me clean from secret evil.

求你拦阻仆人，不犯任意妄为的罪。不容这罪辖制我。我便完全，免犯大罪。
Keep your servant back from sins of pride; let them not have rule over me: then will I be upright and free from great sin.

耶和华我的磐石，我的救赎主阿，愿我口中的言语，心里的意念，在你面前蒙悦纳。
Let the words of my mouth and the thoughts of my heart be pleasing in your eyes, O Lord, my strength and my salvation.

（大卫的诗，交与伶长。）愿耶和华在你遭难的日子应允你。愿名为雅各神的高举你。
<To the chief music-maker. A Psalm. Of David.> May the Lord give ear to you in the day of trouble; may you be placed on high by the name of the God of Jacob;

愿他从圣所救助你，从锡安坚固你。
May he send you help from the holy place, and give you strength from Zion;

记念你的一切供献，悦纳你的燔祭。（细拉）
May he keep all your offerings in mind, and be pleased with the fat of your burned offerings; (Selah.)

将你心所愿的赐给你，成就你的一切筹算。
May he give you your heart's desire, and put all your purposes into effect.

我们要因你的救恩夸胜，要奉我们神的名竖立旌旗。愿耶和华成就你一切所求的。
We will be glad in your salvation, and in the name of our God we will put up our flags: may the Lord give you all your requests.

现在我知道耶和华救护他的受膏者，必从他的圣天上应允他，用右手的能力救护他。
Now am I certain that the Lord gives salvation to his king; he will give him an answer from his holy heaven with the strength of salvation in his right hand.

有人靠车，有人靠马。但我们要提到耶和华我们神的名。
Some put their faith in carriages and some in horses; but we will be strong in the name of the Lord our God.

他们都屈身仆倒，我们却起来，立得正直。
They are bent down and made low; but we have been lifted up.

求耶和华施行拯救。我们呼求的时候，愿王应允我们。
Come to our help, Lord: let the king give ear to our cry.

（大卫的诗，交与伶长。）耶和华阿，王必因你的能力欢喜。因你的救恩，他的快乐何其大。
<To the chief music-maker. A Psalm. Of David.> The king will be glad in your strength, O Lord; how great will be his delight in your salvation!

他心里所愿的，你已经赐给他。他嘴唇所求的，你未尝不应允。（细拉）
You have given him his heart's desire, and have not kept back the request of his lips. (Selah.)

你以美福迎接他，把精金的冠冕戴在他头上。
For you go before him with the blessings of good things: you put a crown of fair gold on his head.

他向你求寿，你便赐给他，就是日子长久，直到永远。
He made request to you for life, and you gave it to him, long life for ever and ever.

他因你的救恩大有荣耀。你又将尊荣威严加在他身上。
His glory is great in your salvation: honour and authority have you put on him.

你使他有洪福，直到永远。又使他在你面前欢喜快乐。
For you have made him a blessing for ever: you have given him joy in the light of your face.

王倚靠耶和华，因至高者的慈爱必不摇动。
For the king has faith in the Lord, and through the mercy of the Most High he will not be moved.

你的手要搜出你的一切仇敌。你的右手要搜出那些恨你的人。
Your hand will make a search for all your haters; your right hand will be hard on all those who are against you.

你发怒的时候，要使他们如在炎热的火炉中。耶和华要在他的震怒中吞灭他们。那火要把他们烧尽了。
You will make them like a flaming oven before you; the Lord in his wrath will put an end to them, and they will be burned up in the fire.

你必从世上灭绝他们的子孙（子孙原文作果子），从人间灭绝他们的后裔。
Their fruit will be cut off from the earth, and their seed from among the children of men.

因为他们有意加害于你。他们想出计谋，却不能作成。
For their thoughts were bitter against you: they had an evil design in their minds, which they were not able to put into effect.

你必使他们转背逃跑，向他们的脸搭箭在弦。
Their backs will be turned when you make ready the cords of your bow against their faces.

耶和华阿，愿你因自己的能力显为至高。这样，我们就唱诗，歌颂你的大能。
Be lifted up, O Lord, in your strength; so will we make songs in praise of your power.

（大卫的诗，交与伶长。调用朝鹿。）我的神，我的神，为什么离弃我。为什么远离不救我，不听我唉哼的言语。
<To the chief music-maker on Aijeleth-hash-shahar. A Psalm. Of David.> My God, my God, why are you turned away from me? why are you so far from helping me, and from the words of my crying?

我的神阿，我白日呼求，你不应允。夜间呼求，并不住声。
O my God, I make my cry in the day, and you give no answer; and in the night, and have no rest.

但你是圣洁的，是用以色列的赞美为宝座的（宝座或作居所）。
But you are holy, O you who are seated among the praises of Israel.

我们的祖宗倚靠你。他们倚靠你，你便解救他们。
Our fathers had faith in you: they had faith and you were their saviour.

他们哀求你，便蒙解救。他们倚靠你，就不羞愧。
They sent up their cry to you and were made free: they put their faith in you and were not put to shame.

但我是虫，不是人。被众人羞辱，被百姓藐视。
But I am a worm and not a man; cursed by men, and looked down on by the people.

凡看见我的都嗤笑我。他们撇嘴摇头，说，
I am laughed at by all those who see me: pushing out their lips and shaking their heads they say,

他把自己交托耶和华，耶和华可以救他吧。耶和华既喜悦他，可以搭救他吧。
He put his faith in the Lord; let the Lord be his saviour now: let the Lord be his saviour, because he had delight in him.

但你是叫我出母腹的。我在母怀里，你就使我有倚靠的心。
But it was you who took care of me from the day of my birth: you gave me faith even from my mother's breasts.

我自出母胎就被交在你手里。从我母亲生我，你就是我的神。
I was in your hands even before my birth; you are my God from the time when I was in my mother's body.

求你不要远离我。因为急难临近了，没有人帮助我。
Be not far from me, for trouble is near; there is no one to give help.

有许多公牛围绕我。巴珊大力的公牛四面困住我。
A great herd of oxen is round me: I am shut in by the strong oxen of Bashan.

他们向我张口，好像抓撕吼叫的狮子。
I saw their mouths wide open, like lions crying after food.

我如水被倒出来。我的骨头都脱了节。我心在我里面如蜡熔化。
I am flowing away like water, and all my bones are out of place: my heart is like wax, it has become soft in my body.

我的精力枯干，如同瓦片。我的舌头贴在我牙床上。你将我安置在死地的尘土中。
My throat is dry like a broken vessel; my tongue is fixed to the roof of my mouth, and the dust of death is on my lips.

犬类围着我。恶党环绕我。他们扎了我的手，我的脚。
Dogs have come round me: I am shut in by the band of evil-doers; they made wounds in my hands and feet.

我的骨头，我都能数过。他们瞪着眼看我。
I am able to see all my bones; their looks are fixed on me:

他们分我的外衣，为我的里衣拈阄。
They make a division of my robes among them, by the decision of chance they take my clothing.

耶和华阿，求你不要远离我。我的救主阿，求你快来帮助我。
Do not be far from me, O Lord: O my strength, come quickly to my help.

求你救我的灵魂脱离刀剑，救我的生命脱离犬类（生命原文作独一者）。
Make my soul safe from the sword, my life from the power of the dog.

救我脱离狮子的口。你已经应允我，使我脱离野牛的角。
Be my saviour from the lion's mouth; let me go free from the horns of the cruel oxen.

我要将你的名传与我的弟兄。在会中我要赞美你。
I will give the knowledge of your name to my brothers: I will give you praise among the people.

你们敬畏耶和华的人，要赞美他。雅各的后裔，都要荣耀他。以色列的后裔，都要惧怕他。
You who have fear of the Lord, give him praise; all you seed of Jacob, give him glory; go in fear of him, all you seed of Israel.

因为他没有藐视憎恶受苦的人。也没有向他掩面。那受苦之人呼吁的时候，他就垂听。
For he has not been unmoved by the pain of him who is troubled; or kept his face covered from him; but he has given an answer to his cry.

我在大会中赞美你的话，是从你而来的。我要在敬畏耶和华的人面前还我的愿。
My praise will be of you in the great meeting: I will make my offerings before his worshippers.

谦卑的人必吃得饱足。寻求耶和华的人必赞美他。愿你们的心永远活着。
The poor will have a feast of good things: those who make search for the Lord will give him praise: your heart will have life for ever.

地的四极，都要想念耶和华，并且归顺他。列国的万族，都要在你面前敬拜。
All the ends of the earth will keep it in mind and be turned to the Lord: all the families of the nations will give him worship.

因为国权是耶和华的。他是管理万国的。
For the kingdom is the Lord's; he is the ruler among the nations.

地上一切丰肥的人，必吃喝而敬拜。凡下到尘土中不能存活自己性命的人，都要在他面前下拜。
All the fat ones of the earth will give him worship; all those who go down to the dust will make themselves low before him, even he who has not enough for the life of his soul.

他必有后裔事奉他。主所行的事，必传与后代。
A seed will be his servant; the doings of the Lord will be made clear to the generation which comes after.

他们必来把他的公义传给将要生的民，言明这事是他所行的。
They will come and make his righteousness clear to a people of the future because he has done this.

（大卫的诗。）耶和华是我的牧者。我必不至缺乏。
<A Psalm. Of David.> The Lord takes care of me as his sheep; I will not be without any good thing.

他使我躺卧在青草地上，领我在可安歇的水边。
He makes a resting-place for me in the green fields: he is my guide by the quiet waters.

他使我的灵魂苏醒，为自己的名引导我走义路。
He gives new life to my soul: he is my guide in the ways of righteousness because of his name.

我虽然行过死荫的幽谷，也不怕遭害。因为你与我同在。你的杖，你的竿，都安慰我。
Yes, though I go through the valley of deep shade, I will have no fear of evil; for you are with me, your rod and your support are my comfort.

在我敌人面前，你为我摆设筵席。你用油膏了我的头，使我的福杯满溢。
You make ready a table for me in front of my haters: you put oil on my head; my cup is overflowing.

我一生一世必有恩惠慈爱随着我。我且要住在耶和华的殿中，直到永远。
Truly, blessing and mercy will be with me all the days of my life; and I will have a place in the house of the Lord all my days.

（大卫的诗。）地和其中所充满的，世界和住在其间的，都属耶和华。
<A Psalm. Of David.> The earth is the Lord's, with all its wealth; the world and all the people living in it.

他把地建立在海上，安定在大水之上。
For by him it was based on the seas, and made strong on the deep rivers.

谁能登耶和华的山。谁能站在他的圣所。
Who may go up into the hill of the Lord? and who may come into his holy place?

就是手洁心清，不向虚妄，起誓不怀诡诈的人。
He who has clean hands and a true heart; whose desire has not gone out to foolish things, who has not taken a false oath.

他必蒙耶和华赐福，又蒙救他的神使他成义。
He will have blessing from the Lord, and righteousness from the God of his salvation.

这是寻求耶和华的族类，是寻求你面的雅各（细拉）。
This is the generation of those whose hearts are turned to you, even to your face, O God of Jacob. (Selah.)

众城门哪，你们要抬起头来。永久的门户，你们要被举起。那荣耀的王将要进来。
Let your heads be lifted up, O doors; be lifted up, O you eternal doors: that the King of glory may come in.

荣耀的王是谁呢？就是有力有能的耶和华，在战场上有能的耶和华。
Who is the King of glory? The Lord of strength and power, the Lord strong in war.

众城门哪，你们要抬起头来。永久的门户，你们要把头抬起。那荣耀的王将要进来。
Let your heads be lifted up, O doors; let them be lifted up, O you eternal doors: that the King of glory may come in.

荣耀的王是谁呢？万军之耶和华，他是荣耀的王。（细拉）
Who is the King of glory? The Lord of armies, he is the King of glory. (Selah.)

（大卫的诗。）耶和华阿，我的心仰望你。
<Of David.> To you, O Lord, my soul is lifted up.

我的神阿，我素来倚靠你。求你不要叫我羞愧。不要叫我的仇敌向我夸胜。
O my God, I have put my faith in you, let me not be shamed; let not my haters be glorying over me.

凡等候你的必不羞愧。惟有那无故行奸诈的，必要羞愧。
Let no servant of yours be put to shame; may those be shamed who are false without cause.

耶和华阿，求你将你的道指示我，将你的路教训我。
Make your steps clear to me, O Lord; give me knowledge of your ways.

求你以你的真理引导我，教训我。因为你是救我的神。我终日等候你。
Be my guide and teacher in the true way; for you are the God of my salvation; I am waiting for your word all the day.

耶和华阿，求你记念你的怜悯和慈爱。因为这是亘古以来所常有的。
O Lord, keep in mind your pity and your mercies; for they have been from the earliest times.

求你不要记念我幼年的罪愆，和我的过犯。耶和华阿，求你因你的恩惠，按你的慈爱记念我。
Do not keep in mind my sins when I was young, or my wrongdoing: let your memory of me be full of mercy, O Lord, because of your righteousness.

耶和华是良善正直的。所以他必指示罪人走正路。
Good and upright is the Lord: so he will be the teacher of sinners in the way.

他必按公平引领谦卑人，将他的道教训他们。
He will be an upright guide to the poor in spirit: he will make his way clear to them.

凡遵守他的约和他法度的人，耶和华都以慈爱诚实待他。
All the ways of the Lord are mercy and good faith for those who keep his agreement and his witness.

耶和华阿，求你因你的名赦免我的罪，因为我的罪重大。
Because of your name, O Lord, let me have forgiveness for my sin, which is very great.

谁敬畏耶和华，耶和华必指示他当选择的道路。
If a man has the fear of the Lord, the Lord will be his teacher in the way of his pleasure.

他必安然居住。他的后裔必承受地土。
His soul will be full of good things, and his seed will have the earth for its heritage.

耶和华与敬畏他的人亲密。他必将自己的约指示他们。
The secret of the Lord is with those in whose hearts is the fear of him; he will make his agreement clear to them.

我的眼目时常仰望耶和华。因为他必将我的脚从网里拉出来。
My eyes are turned to the Lord at all times; for he will take my feet out of the net.

求你转向我，怜恤我，因为我是孤独困苦。
Be turned to me, and have mercy on me; for I am troubled and have no helper.

我心里的愁苦甚多。求你救我脱离我的祸患。
The troubles of my heart are increased: O take me out of my sorrows.

求你看顾我的困苦，我的艰难，赦免我一切的罪。
Give thought to my grief and my pain; and take away all my sins.

求你察看我的仇敌，因为他们人多。并且痛痛的恨我。
See how those who are against me are increased, for bitter is their hate of me.

求你保护我的性命，搭救我，使我不至羞愧，因为我投靠你。
O keep my soul, and take me out of danger: let me not be shamed, for I have put my faith in you.

愿纯全正直保守我，因为我等候你。
For my clean and upright ways keep me safe, because my hope is in you.

神阿，求你救赎以色列脱离他一切的愁苦。
Give Israel salvation, O God, out of all his troubles.

（大卫的诗。）耶和华阿，求你为我伸冤，因我向来行事纯全，我又倚靠耶和华并不摇动。
<Of David.> O Lord, be my judge, for my behaviour has been upright: I have put my faith in the Lord, I am not in danger of slipping.

耶和华阿，求你察看我，试验我，熬炼我的肺腑心肠。
Put me in the scales, O Lord, so that I may be tested; let the fire make clean my thoughts and my heart.

因为你的慈爱常在我眼前。我也按你的真理而行。
For your mercy is before my eyes; and I have gone in the way of your good faith.

我没有和虚谎人同坐。也不与瞒哄人的同群。
I have not taken my seat with foolish persons, and I do not go with false men.

我恨恶恶人的会，必不与恶人同坐。
I have been a hater of the band of wrongdoers, and I will not be seated among sinners.

耶和华阿，我要洗手表明无辜，才环绕你的祭坛。
I will make my hands clean from sin; so will I go round your altar, O Lord;

我好发称谢的声音。也要述说你一切奇妙的作为。
That I may give out the voice of praise, and make public all the wonders which you have done.

耶和华阿，我喜爱你所住的殿，和你显荣耀的居所。
Lord, your house has been dear to me, and the resting-place of your glory.

不要把我的灵魂和罪人一同除掉，不要把我的性命和流人血的一同除掉。
Let not my soul be numbered among sinners, or my life among men of blood;

他们的手中有奸恶，右手满有贿赂。
In whose hands are evil designs, and whose right hands take money for judging falsely.

至于我，却要行事纯全。求你救赎我，怜恤我。
But as for me, I will go on in my upright ways: be my saviour, and have mercy on me.

我的脚站在平坦地方。在众会中我要称颂耶和华。
I have a safe resting-place for my feet; I will give praise to the Lord in the meetings of the people.

（大卫的诗。）耶和华是我的亮光，是我的拯救。我还怕谁呢？耶和华是我性命的保障（保障或作力量），我还惧谁呢？
<Of David.> The Lord is my light and my salvation; who is then a cause of fear to me? the Lord is the strength of my life; who is a danger to me?

那作恶的，就是我的仇敌，前来吃我肉的时候，就绊跌仆倒。
When evil-doers, even my haters, came on me to put an end to me, they were broken and put to shame.

虽有军兵安营攻击我，我的心也不害怕。虽然兴起刀兵攻击我，我必仍旧安稳。
Even if an army came against me with its tents, my heart would have no fear: if war was made on me, my faith would not be moved.

有一件事，我曾求耶和华，我仍要寻求。就是一生一世住在耶和华的殿中，瞻仰他的荣美，在他的殿里求问。
One prayer have I made to the Lord, and this is my heart's desire; that I may have a place in the house of the Lord all the days of my life, looking on his glory, and getting wisdom in his Temple.

因为我遭遇患难，他必暗暗地保守我。在他亭子里，把我藏在他帐幕的隐密处，将我高举在磐石上。
For in the time of trouble he will keep me safe in his tent: in the secret place of his tent he will keep me from men's eyes; high on a rock he will put me.

现在我得以昂首，高过四面的仇敌。我要在他的帐幕里欢然献祭。我要唱诗，歌颂耶和华。
And now my head will be lifted up higher than my haters who are round me: because of this I will make offerings of joy in his tent; I will make a song, truly I will make a song of praise to the Lord.

耶和华阿，我用声音呼吁的时候，求你垂听。并求你怜恤我，应允我。
O Lord, let the voice of my cry come to your ears: have mercy on me, and give me an answer.

你说，你们当寻求我的面。那时我心向你说，耶和华阿，你的面我正要寻求。
When you said, Make search for my face, my heart said to you, For your face will I make my search.

不要向我掩面，不要发怒赶逐仆人。你向来是帮助我的。救我的神阿，不要丢掉我，也不要离弃我。
Let not your face be covered from me; do not put away your servant in wrath; you have been my help: do not give me up or take your support from me, O God of my salvation.

我父母离弃我，耶和华必收留我。
When my father and my mother are turned away from me, then the Lord will be my support.

耶和华阿，求你将你的道指教我，因我仇敌的缘故引导我走平坦的路。
Make your way clear to me, O Lord, guiding me by the right way, because of my haters.

求你不要把我交给敌人，遂其所愿，因为妄作见证的，和口吐凶言的，起来攻击我。
Do not give me into their hands, because false witnesses have come out against me, and men breathing destruction.

我若不信在活人之地得见耶和华的恩惠，就早已丧胆了
I had almost given up my hope of seeing the blessing of the Lord in the land of the living.

要等候耶和华。当壮胆，坚固你的心。我再说，要等候耶和华。
Let your hope be in the Lord: take heart and be strong; yes, let your hope be in the Lord.

（大卫的诗。）耶和华阿，我要求告你。我的磐石阿，不要向我缄默。倘若你向我闭口，我就如将死的人一样。
<Of David.> My cry goes up to you, O Lord, my Rock; do not keep back your answer from me, so that I may not become like those who go down into the underworld.

我呼求你，向你至圣所举手的时候，求你垂听我恳求的声音。
Give ear to the voice of my prayer, when I am crying to you, when my hands are lifted up to your holy place.

不要把我和恶人，并作孽的，一同除掉。他们与邻舍说和平话，心里却是奸恶。
Do not take me away with the sinners and the workers of evil, who say words of peace to their neighbours, but evil is in their hearts.

愿你按着他们所作的，并他们所行的恶事待他们。愿你照着他们手所作的待他们。将他们所应得的报应加给他们。
Give them the right reward of their acts, and of their evil doings: give them punishment for the works of their hands, let them have their full reward.

他们既然不留心耶和华所行的，和他手所作的，他就必毁坏他们，不建立他们。
Because they have no respect for the works of the Lord, or for the things which his hands have made, they will be broken down and not lifted up by him.

耶和华是应当称颂的，因为他听了我恳求的声音。
May the Lord be praised, because he has given ear to the voice of my prayer.

耶和华是我的力量，是我的盾牌。我心里倚靠他，就得帮助。所以我心中欢乐。我必用诗歌颂赞他。
The Lord is my strength and my breastplate, my heart had faith in him and I am helped; for this cause my heart is full of rapture, and I will give him praise in my song.

耶和华是他百姓的力量，又是他受膏者得救的保障。
The Lord is their strength, and a strong place of salvation for his king.

求你拯救你的百姓，赐福给你的产业，牧养他们，扶持他们，直到永远。
Be a saviour to your people, and send a blessing on your heritage: be their guide, and let them be lifted up for ever.

（大卫的诗。）神的众子阿，你们要将荣耀能力，归给耶和华。归给耶和华。
<A Psalm. Of David.> Give to the Lord, you sons of the gods, give to the Lord glory and strength.

要将耶和华的名所当得的荣耀归给他。以圣洁的妆饰（的或作为）敬拜耶和华。
Give to the Lord the full glory of his name; give him worship in holy robes.

耶和华的声音发在水上。荣耀的神打雷，耶和华打雷在大水之上。
The voice of the Lord is on the waters: the God of glory is thundering, the Lord is on the great waters.

耶和华的声音大有能力。耶和华的声音满有威严。
The voice of the Lord is full of power; the voice of the Lord has a noble sound.

耶和华的声音震破香柏树。耶和华震碎利巴嫩的香柏树。
By the voice of the Lord are the cedar-trees broken, even the cedars of Lebanon are broken by the Lord.

他也使之跳跃如牛犊，使利巴嫩和西连跳跃如野牛犊。
He makes them go jumping about like a young ox; Lebanon and Sirion like a young mountain ox.

耶和华的声音使火焰分岔。
At the voice of the Lord flames of fire are seen.

耶和华的声音震动旷野。耶和华震动加低斯的旷野。
At the voice of the Lord there is a shaking in the waste land, even a shaking in the waste land of Kadesh.

耶和华的声音惊动母鹿落胎，树木也脱落净光。凡在他殿中的，都称说他的荣耀。
At the voice of the Lord the roes give birth, the leaves are taken from the trees: in his Temple everything says, Glory.

洪水泛滥之时，耶和华坐着为王。耶和华坐着为王，直到永远。
The Lord had his seat as king when the waters came on the earth; the Lord is seated as king for ever.

耶和华必赐力量给他的百姓。耶和华必赐平安的福给他的百姓。
The Lord will give strength to his people; the Lord will give his people the blessing of peace.

（大卫在献殿的时候，作这诗歌。）耶和华阿，我要尊崇你，因为你曾提拔我，不叫仇敌向我夸耀。
<A Psalm. A Song at the blessing of the House. Of David.> I will give you praise and honour, O Lord, because through you I have been lifted up; you have not given my haters cause to be glad over me.

耶和华我的神阿，我曾呼求你，你医治了我。
O Lord my God, I sent up my cry to you, and you have made me well.

耶和华阿，你曾把我的灵魂从阴间救上来，使我存活，不至于下坑。
O Lord, you have made my soul come again from the underworld: you have given me life and kept me from going down among the dead.

耶和华的圣民哪，你们要歌颂他，称赞他可记念的圣名。
Make songs to the Lord, O you saints of his, and give praise to his holy name.

因为他的怒气不过是转眼之间。他的恩典乃是一生之久。一宿虽然有哭泣，早晨便必欢呼。
For his wrath is only for a minute; in his grace there is life; weeping may be for a night, but joy comes in the morning.

至于我，我凡事平顺，便说，我永不动摇。
When things went well for me I said, I will never be moved.

耶和华阿，你曾施恩，叫我的江山稳固。你掩了面，我就惊惶。
Lord, by your grace you have kept my mountain strong: when your face was turned from me I was troubled.

耶和华阿，我曾求告你。我向耶和华恳求，说，
My voice went up to you, O Lord; I made my prayer to the Lord.

我被害流血，下到坑中，有什么益处呢？尘土岂能称赞你，传说你的诚实吗？
What profit is there in my blood if I go down into the underworld? will the dust give you praise, or be a witness to your help?

耶和华阿，求你应允我，怜恤我。耶和华阿，求你帮助我。
Give ear to me, O Lord, and have mercy on me: Lord, be my helper.

你已将我的哀哭变为跳舞，将我的麻衣脱去，给我披上喜乐。
By you my sorrow is turned into dancing; you have taken away my clothing of grief, and given me robes of joy;

好叫我的灵（原文作荣耀）歌颂你，并不住声。耶和华我的神阿，我要称谢你，直到永远。
So that my glory may make songs of praise to you and not be quiet. O Lord my God, I will give you praise for ever.

（大卫的诗，交与伶长。）耶和华阿，我投靠你，求你使我永不羞愧，凭你的公义搭救我。
<To the chief music-maker. A Psalm. Of David.> In you, O Lord, have I put my hope; let me never be shamed; keep me safe in your righteousness.

求你侧耳而听，快快救我，作我坚固的磐石，拯救我的保障。
Let your ear be turned to me; take me quickly out of danger; be my strong Rock, my place of strength where I may be safe.

因为你是我的岩石，我的山寨。所以求你为你名的缘故，引导我，指点我。
For you are my Rock and my strong tower; go in front of me and be my guide, because of your name.

求你救我脱离人为我暗设的网罗。因为你是我的保障。
Take me out of the net which they have put ready for me secretly; for you are my strength.

我将我的灵魂交在你手里。耶和华诚实的神阿，你救赎了我。
Into your hands I give my spirit; you are my saviour, O Lord God for ever true.

我恨恶那信奉虚无之神的人。我却倚靠耶和华。
I am full of hate for those who go after false gods; but my hope is in the Lord.

我要为你的慈爱高兴欢喜。因为你见过我的困苦，知道我心中的艰难。
I will be glad and have delight in your mercy; because you have seen my trouble; you have had pity on my soul in its sorrows;

你未曾把我交在仇敌手里。你使我的脚站在宽阔之处。
And you have not given me into the hand of my hater; you have put my feet in a wide place.

耶和华阿，求你怜恤我，因为我在急难之中。我的眼睛因忧愁而干瘪，连我的身心，也不安舒。
Have mercy on me, O Lord, for I am in trouble; my eyes are wasted with grief, I am wasted in soul and body.

我的生命为愁苦所消耗。我的年岁为叹息所旷废。我的力量因我的罪孽衰败。我的骨头也枯干。
My life goes on in sorrow, and my years in weeping; my strength is almost gone because of my sin, and my bones are wasted away.

我因一切敌人成了羞辱，在我的邻舍跟前更甚。那认识我的都惧怕我。在外头看见我的都躲避我。
Because of all those who are against me, I have become a word of shame to my neighbours; a cause of shaking the head and a fear to my friends: those who saw me in the street went in flight from me.

我被人忘记，如同死人，无人记念。我好像破碎的器皿。
I have gone from men's minds and memory like a dead man; I am like a broken vessel.

我听见了许多人的谗谤，四围都是惊吓。他们一同商议攻击我的时候，就图谋要害我的性命。
False statements against me have come to my ears; fear was on every side: they were talking together against me, designing to take away my life.

耶和华阿，我仍旧倚靠你。我说，你是我的神。
But I had faith in you, O Lord; I said, You are my God.

我终身的事在你手中。求你救我脱离仇敌的手，和那些逼迫我的人。
The chances of my life are in your hand; take me out of the hands of my haters, and of those who go after me.

求你使你的脸光照仆人，凭你的慈爱拯救我。
Let your servant see the light of your face; in your mercy be my saviour.

耶和华阿，求你叫我不至羞愧。因为我曾呼吁你。求你使恶人羞愧，使他们在阴间缄默无声。
Let me not be shamed, O Lord, for I have made my prayer to you; let the sinners be shamed, and let their mouths be shut in the underworld.

那撒谎的人，逞骄傲轻慢，出狂妄的话攻击义人。愿他的嘴哑而无言。
Let the false lips be shut, which say evil against the upright, looking down on him in their pride.

敬畏你投靠你的人，你为他们所积存的，在世人面前所施行的恩惠，是何等大呢。
O how great is your grace, which you have put in store for your worshippers, and which you have made clear to those who had faith in you, before the sons of men!

你必把他们藏在你面前的隐密处，免得遇见人的计谋。你必暗暗地保守他们在亭子里，免受口舌的争闹。
You will keep them safe in your house from the designs of man; in the secret of your tent will you keep them from angry tongues.

耶和华是应当称颂的。因为他在坚固城里，向我施展奇妙的慈爱。
May the Lord be praised, because he has made clear to me the wonder of his grace in a strong town.

至于我，我曾急促的说，我从你眼前被隔绝。然而我呼求你的时候，你仍听我恳求的声音。
And as for me, I said in my fear, I am cut off from before your eyes; but you gave ear to the voice of my prayer, when my cry went up to you.

耶和华的圣民哪，你们都要爱他。耶和华保护诚实人，足足报应行事骄傲的人。
O have love for the Lord, all you his saints; for the Lord keeps safe from danger all those who are true to him, and gives the workers of pride their right reward.

凡仰望耶和华的人，你们都要壮胆，坚固你们的心。
Put away fear and let your heart be strong, all you whose hope is in the Lord.

（大卫的训诲诗。）得赦免其过，遮盖其罪的，这人是有福的。
<Of David. Maschil.> Happy is he who has forgiveness for his wrongdoing, and whose sin is covered.

凡心里没有诡诈，耶和华不算为有罪的，这人是有福的。
Happy is the man in whom the Lord sees no evil, and in whose spirit there is no deceit.

我闭口不认罪的时候，因终日唉哼，而骨头枯干。
When I kept my mouth shut, my bones were wasted, because of my crying all through the day.

黑夜白日，你的手在我身上沉重。我的精液耗尽，如同夏天的干旱。（细拉）
For the weight of your hand was on me day and night; my body became dry like the earth in summer. (Selah.)

我向你陈明我的罪，不隐瞒我的恶。我说，我要向耶和华承认我的过犯，你就赦免我的罪恶。（细拉）
I made my wrongdoing clear to you, and did not keep back my sin. I said, I will put it all before the Lord; and you took away my wrongdoing and my sin. (Selah.)

为此，凡虔诚人，都当趁你可寻找的时候祷告你。大水泛溢的时候，必不能到他那里。
For this cause let every saint make his prayer to you at a time when you are near: then the overflowing of the great waters will not overtake him.

你是我藏身之处。你必保佑我脱离苦难，以得救的乐歌，四面环绕我。（细拉）
You are my safe and secret place; you will keep me from trouble; you will put songs of salvation on the lips of those who are round me. (Selah.)

我要教导你，指示你当行的路。我要定睛在你身上劝戒你。
I will give you knowledge, teaching you the way to go; my eye will be your guide.

你不可像那无知的骡马，必用嚼环辔头勒住他，不然，就不能驯服。
Do not be like the horse or the ass, without sense; ...

恶人必多受苦楚。惟独倚靠耶和华的，必有慈爱四面环绕他。
The sinner will be full of trouble; but mercy will be round the man who has faith in the Lord.

你们义人应当靠耶和华欢喜快乐。你们心里正直的人，都当欢呼。
Be glad in the Lord with joy, you upright men; give cries of joy, all you whose hearts are true.

义人哪，你们应当靠耶和华欢乐。正直人的赞美是合宜的。
Be glad in the Lord, O doers of righteousness; for praise is beautiful for the upright.

你们应当弹琴称谢耶和华，用十弦瑟歌颂他。
Give praise to the Lord on the corded instrument; make melody to him with instruments of music.

应当向他唱新歌，弹得巧妙，声音洪亮。
Make a new song to him; playing expertly with a loud noise.

因为耶和华的言语正直。凡他所作的，尽都诚实。
For the word of the Lord is upright, and all his works are certain.

他喜爱仁义公平。遍地满了耶和华的慈爱。
His delight is in righteousness and wisdom; the earth is full of the mercy of the Lord.

诸天借耶和华的命而造，万象借他口中的气而成。
By the word of the Lord were the heavens made; and all the army of heaven by the breath of his mouth.

他聚集海水如垒，收藏深洋在库房。
He makes the waters of the sea come together in a mass; he keeps the deep seas in store-houses.

愿全地都敬畏耶和华。愿世上的居民，都惧怕他。
Let the earth be full of the fear of the Lord; let all the people of the world be in holy fear of him.

因为他说有，就有。命立，就立。
For he gave the word, and it was done; by his order it was fixed for ever.

耶和华使列国的筹算归于无有，使众民的思念无有功效。
The Lord undoes the designs of the nations; he makes the thoughts of the peoples without effect.

耶和华的寿算永远立定，他心中的思念万代常存。
The Lord's purpose is eternal, the designs of his heart go on through all the generations of man.

以耶和华为神的，那国是有福的。他所拣选为自己产业的，那民是有福的。
Happy is the nation whose God is the Lord; and the people whom he has taken for his heritage.

耶和华从天上观看。他看见一切的世人。
The Lord is looking down from heaven; he sees all the sons of men;

从他的居所，往外察看地上一切的居民。
From his house he keeps watch on all who are living on the earth;

他是那造成他们众人心的，留意他们一切作为的。
He makes all their hearts; their works are clear to him.

君王不能因兵多得胜。勇士不能因力大得救。
A king's salvation is not in the power of his army; a strong man does not get free by his great strength.

靠马得救是枉然的。马也不能因力大救人。
A horse is a false hope; his great power will not make any man free from danger.

耶和华的眼目，看顾敬畏他的人，和仰望他慈爱的人，
See, the eye of the Lord is on those in whose hearts is the fear of him, on those whose hope is in his mercy;

要救他们的命脱离死亡，并使他们在饥荒中存活。
To keep their souls from death; and to keep them living in time of need.

我们的心向来等候耶和华。他是我们的帮助，我们的盾牌。
Our souls are waiting for the Lord; he is our help and our salvation.

我们的心必靠他欢喜，因为我们向来倚靠他的圣名。
For in him our hearts have joy; in his holy name is our hope.

耶和华阿，求你照着我们所仰望你的，向我们施行慈爱。
Let your mercy be on us, O Lord, as we are waiting for you.

（大卫在亚比米勒面前装疯，被他赶出去，就作这诗。）我要时时称颂耶和华。赞美他的话必常在我口中。
<Of David. When he made a change in his behaviour before Abimelech, who sent him away, and he went.> I will be blessing the Lord at all times; his praise will be ever in my mouth.

我的心必因耶和华夸耀。谦卑人听见，就要喜乐。
My soul will say great things of the Lord: the poor in spirit will have knowledge of it and be glad.

你们和我当称耶和华为大，一同高举他的名。
O give praise to the Lord with me; let us be witnesses together of his great name.

我曾寻求耶和华，他就应允我，救我脱离了一切的恐惧。
I was searching for the Lord, and he gave ear to my voice, and made me free from all my fears.

凡仰望他的，便有光荣。他们的脸，必不蒙羞。
Let your eyes be turned to him and you will have light, and your faces will not be shamed.

我这困苦人呼求，耶和华便垂听，救我脱离一切患难。
This poor man's cry came before the Lord, and he gave him salvation from all his troubles.

耶和华的使者，在敬畏他的人四围安营，搭救他们。
The angel of the Lord is ever watching over those who have fear of him, to keep them safe.

你们要尝尝主恩的滋味，便知道他是美善。投靠他的人有福了。
By experience you will see that the Lord is good; happy is the man who has faith in him.

耶和华的圣民哪，你们当敬畏他，因敬畏他的一无所缺。
Keep yourselves in the fear of the Lord, all you his saints; for those who do so will have no need of anything.

少壮狮子，还缺食忍饿。但寻求耶和华的。什么好处都不缺。
The young lions are in need and have no food; but those who are looking to the Lord will have every good thing.

众弟子阿，你们当来听我的话。我要将敬畏耶和华的道教训你们。
Come, children, give attention to me; I will be your teacher in the fear of the Lord.

有何人喜好存活，爱慕长寿，得享美福。
What man has a love of life, and a desire that his days may be increased so that he may see good?

就要禁止舌头不出恶言，嘴唇不说诡诈的话。
Keep your tongue from evil, and your lips from words of deceit.

要离恶行善，寻求和睦，一心追赶。
Be turned from evil, and do good; make a search for peace, desiring it with all your heart.

耶和华的眼目，看顾义人，他的耳朵，听他们的呼求。
The eyes of the Lord are on the upright, and his ears are open to their cry.

耶和华向行恶的人变脸，要从世上除灭他们的名号。
The face of the Lord is against those who do evil, to take away the memory of them from the earth.

义人呼求，耶和华听见了，便救他们脱离一切患难。
The cry of the upright comes before the Lord, and he takes them out of all their troubles.

耶和华靠近伤心的人，拯救灵性痛悔的人。
The Lord is near the broken-hearted; he is the saviour of those whose spirits are crushed down.

义人多有苦难。但耶和华救他脱离这一切。
Great are the troubles of the upright: but the Lord takes him safely out of them all.

又保全他一身的骨头，连一根也不折断。
He keeps all his bones: not one of them is broken.

恶必害死恶人。恨恶义人的，必被定罪。
Evil will put an end to the sinner, and those who are haters of righteousness will come to destruction.

耶和华救赎他仆人的灵魂。凡投靠他的，必不至定罪。
The Lord will be the saviour of the souls of his servants, and no one who has faith in him will be put to shame.

（大卫的诗。）耶和华阿，与我相争的，求你与他们相争。与我相战的，求你与他们相战。
<Of David.> O Lord, be on my side against those who are judging me; be at war with those who make war against me.

拿着大小的盾牌，起来帮助我。
Be a breastplate to me, and give me your help.

抽出枪来，挡住那追赶我的。求你对我的灵魂说，我是拯救你的。
Take up your spear and keep back my attackers; say to my soul, I am your salvation.

愿那寻索我命的，蒙羞受辱。愿那谋害我的，退后羞愧。
Let them be overcome and put to shame who make attempts to take my soul; let those who would do me damage be turned back and made foolish.

愿他们像风前的糠，有耶和华的使者赶逐他们。
Let them be like dust from the grain before the wind; let the angel of the Lord send them in flight.

愿他们的道路，又暗又滑，有耶和华的使者追赶他们。
Let their way be dark and full of danger; let them be troubled by the angel of the Lord.

因他们无故地为我暗设网罗。无故地挖坑要害我的性命。
For without cause they have put a net ready for me secretly, in which to take my soul.

愿灾祸忽然临到他身上。愿他暗设的网缠住自己。愿他落在其中遭灾祸。
Let destruction come on them without their knowledge; let them be taken themselves in their secret nets, falling into the same destruction.

我的心必靠耶和华快乐，靠他的救恩高兴。
And my soul will have joy in the Lord; it will be glad in his salvation.

我的骨头都要说，耶和华阿，谁能象你救护困苦人，脱离那比他强壮的，救护困苦穷乏人，脱离那抢夺他的。
All my bones will say, Lord, who is like you? The saviour of the poor man from the hands of the strong, of him who is poor and in need from him who takes his goods.

凶恶的见证人起来，盘问我所不知道的事。
False witnesses got up: they put questions to me about crimes of which I had no knowledge.

他们向我以恶报善，使我的灵魂孤苦。
They gave me back evil for good, troubling my soul.

至于我，当他们有病的时候，我便穿麻衣，禁食刻苦己心。我所求的都归到自己的怀中。
But as for me, when they were ill I put on the clothing of sorrow: I went without food and was sad, and my prayer came back again to my heart.

我这样行，好像他是我的朋友，我的弟兄。我屈身悲哀，如同人为母亲哀痛。
My behaviour was as if it had been my friend or my brother: I was bent low in grief like one whose mother is dead.

我在患难中，他们却欢喜，大家聚集。我所不认识的那些下流人，聚集攻击我。他们不住地把我撕裂。
But they took pleasure in my trouble, and came together, yes, low persons came together against me without my knowledge; they never came to an end of wounding me.

他们如同席上好嬉笑的狂妄人，向我咬牙。
Like men of deceit they put me to shame; the voice of their wrath was loud against me.

主阿，你看着不理，要到几时呢？求你救我的灵魂，脱离他们的残害，救我的生命，脱离少壮狮子。（生命原文作独一者）
Lord, how long will you be looking on? take my soul from their destruction, my life from the lions.

我在大会中要称谢你，在众民中要赞美你。
I will give you praise in the great meeting; I will give you honour among a strong people.

求你不容那无理与我为仇的，向我夸耀。不容那无故恨我的，向我挤眼。
Do not let my haters be glad over me falsely; let not those who are against me without cause make sport of me.

因为他们不说和平话。倒想出诡诈的言语，害地上的安静人。
For they do not say words of peace; in their deceit they are designing evil things against the quiet ones in the land.

他们大大张口攻击我，说，阿哈，阿哈，我们的眼已经看见了。
Their mouths were open wide against me, and they said, Aha, aha, our eyes have seen it.

耶和华阿，你已经看见了。求你不要闭口。主阿，求你不要远离我。
You have seen this, O Lord; be not unmoved: O Lord, be not far from me.

我的神我的主阿，求你奋兴醒起，判清我的事，伸明我的冤。
Be awake, O Lord, be moved to take up my cause, my God and my Lord.

耶和华我的神阿，求你按你的公义判断我，不容他们向我夸耀。
Be my judge, O Lord my God, in your righteousness; do not let them be glad over me.

不容他们心里说，阿哈，遂我们的心愿了。不容他们说，我们已经把他吞了。
Let them not say in their hearts, So we will have it: let them not say, We have put an end to him.

愿那喜欢我遭难的，一同抱愧蒙羞。愿那向我妄自尊大的，披惭愧，蒙羞辱。
Let all those who take pleasure in my troubles be shamed and come to nothing: let those who are lifted up against me be covered with shame and have no honour.

愿那喜悦我冤屈得伸的，（冤屈得伸原文作公义），欢呼快乐。愿他们常说，当尊耶和华为大。耶和华喜悦他的仆人平安。
Let those who are on my side give cries of joy; let them ever say, The Lord be praised, for he has pleasure in the peace of his servant.

我的舌头，要终日论说你的公义，时常赞美你。
And my tongue will be talking of your righteousness and of your praise all the day.

（耶和华的仆人大卫的诗，交与伶长。）恶人的罪过，在他心里说，我眼中不怕神。
<To the chief music-maker. Of the servant of the Lord. Of David.> The sin of the evil-doer says in his heart, There is no fear of the Lord before his eyes.

他自夸自媚，以为他的罪孽终不显露，不被恨恶。
For he takes comfort in the thought that his sin will not be uncovered and hated.

他口中的言语，尽是罪孽诡诈。他与智慧善行，已经断绝。
In the words of his mouth are evil and deceit; he has given up being wise and doing good.

他在床上图谋罪孽，定意行不善的道，不憎恶恶事。
He gives thought to evil on his bed; he takes a way which is not good; he is not a hater of evil.

耶和华阿，你的慈爱，上及诸天。你的信实，达到穹苍。
Your mercy, O Lord, is in the heavens, and your strong purpose is as high as the clouds.

你的公义，好像高山。你的判断，如同深渊。耶和华阿，人民牲畜，你都救护。
Your righteousness is like the mountains of God; your judging is like the great deep; O Lord, you give life to man and beast.

神阿，你的慈爱，何其宝贵。世人投靠在你翅膀的荫下。
How good is your loving mercy, O God! the children of men take cover under the shade of your wings.

他们必因你殿里的肥甘，得以饱足。你也必叫他们喝你乐河的水
The delights of your house will be showered on them; you will give them drink from the river of your pleasures.

因为在你那里，有生命的源头。在你的光中，我们必得见光
For with you is the fountain of life: in your light we will see light.

愿你常施慈爱给认识你的人。常以公义待心里正直的人。
O let there be no end to your loving mercy to those who have knowledge of you, or of your righteousness to the upright in heart.

不容骄傲人的脚践踏我，不容凶恶人的手赶逐我。
Let not the foot of pride come against me, or the hand of the evil-doers put me out of my place.

在那里作孽的人，已经仆倒。他们被推倒，不能再起来。
There the workers of evil have come down: they have been made low, and will not be lifted up.

（大卫的诗。）不要为作恶的，心怀不平，也不要向那行不义的，生出嫉妒。
<Of David.> Do not be angry because of the wrongdoers, or have envy of the workers of evil.

因为他们如草快被割下，又如青菜快要枯干。
For they will quickly be cut down like grass, and become dry like the green plants.

你当倚靠耶和华而行善。住在地上，以他的信实为粮。
Have faith in the Lord, and do good; be at rest in the land, and go after righteousness.

又要以耶和华为乐。他就将你心里所求的赐给你。
So will your delight be in the Lord, and he will give you your heart's desires.

当将你的事交托耶和华，并倚靠他，他就必成全。
Put your life in the hands of the Lord; have faith in him and he will do it.

他要使你的公义，如光发出，使你的公平，明如正午。
And he will make your righteousness be seen like the light, and your cause like the shining of the sun.

你当默然倚靠耶和华，耐性等候他。不要因那道路通达的，和那恶谋成就的，心怀不平。
Take your rest in the Lord, waiting quietly for him; do not be angry because of the man who does well in his evil ways, and gives effect to his bad designs.

当止住怒气，离弃忿怒。不要心怀不平，以致作恶。
Put an end to your wrath and be no longer bitter; do not give way to angry feeling which is a cause of sin.

因为作恶的，必被剪除。惟有等候耶和华的，必承受地土。
For the evil-doers will be cut off: but those who have faith in the Lord will have the earth for their heritage.

还有片时，恶人要归于无有。你就是细察他的住处，也要归于无有。
For in a short time the evil-doer will be gone: you will go searching for his place, and it will not be there.

但谦卑人必承受地土，以丰盛的平安为乐。
But the gentle will have the earth for their heritage; they will take their delight in peace without measure.

恶人设谋害义人，又向他咬牙。
The sinner has evil designs against the upright, lifting up the voice of wrath against him.

主要笑他，因见他受罚的日子将要来到。
He will be laughed at by the Lord, who sees that his day is coming.

恶人已经弓上弦，刀出鞘，要打倒困苦穷乏的人，要杀害行动正直的人。
The evil-doers have taken out their swords, their bows are bent; for crushing the poor, and to put to death those who are upright in their ways.

他们的刀，必刺入自己的心，他们的弓，必被折断。
But their swords will be turned into their hearts, and their bows will be broken.

一个义人所有的虽少，强过许多恶人的富余。
The little which the good man has is better than the wealth of evil-doers.

因为恶人的膀臂，必被折断。但耶和华是扶持义人。
For the arms of the evil-doers will be broken: but the Lord is the support of the good.

耶和华知道完全人的日子。他们的产业，要存到永远。
The days of the upright are numbered by the Lord, and their heritage will be for ever.

他们在急难的时候，不至羞愧，在饥荒的日子，必得饱足。
They will not be shamed in the evil time, and in the days when all are in need of food they will have enough.

恶人却要灭亡。耶和华的仇敌，要像羊羔的脂油。（或作像草地的华美）他们要消灭，要如烟消灭。
But the wrongdoers will come to destruction, and the haters of the Lord will be like the fat of lambs, they will be burned up; they will go up in smoke, and never again be seen.

恶人借贷而不偿还。义人却恩待人，并且施舍。
The sinner takes money and does not give it back; but the upright man has mercy, and gives to others.

蒙耶和华赐福的，必承受地土。被他咒诅的，必被剪除。
Those who have his blessing will have the earth for their heritage; but those who are cursed by him will be cut off.

义人的脚步，被耶和华立定。他的道路，耶和华也喜爱。
The steps of a good man are ordered by the Lord, and he takes delight in his way.

他虽失脚，也不至全身仆倒。因为耶和华用手搀扶他。（或作搀扶他的手）
Even if he has a fall he will not be without help: for the hand of the Lord is supporting him.

我从前年幼，现在年老，却未见过义人被弃。也未见过他的后裔讨饭。
I have been young, and now am old, but I have not seen the good man without help, or his children looking for bread.

他终日恩待人，借给人。他的后裔也蒙福。
All the day he is ready to have mercy and to give; his children are a blessing.

你当离恶行善，就可永远安居。
Be turned from evil, and do good; and your place will be for ever.

因为耶和华喜爱公平，不撇弃他的圣民。他们永蒙保佑。但恶人的后裔，必被剪除。
For the Lord is a lover of righteousness, and takes care of his saints; they will be kept safe for ever; but the seed of the evil-doers will be cut off.

义人必承受地土，永居其上。
The upright will have the earth for their heritage, and will go on living there for ever.

义人的口谈论智慧，他的舌头讲说公平。
The mouth of the good man says words of wisdom; the talk of his tongue is of righteousness.

神的律法在他心里。他的脚总不滑跌。
The law of his God is in his heart; he will never make a false step.

恶人窥探义人，想要杀他。
The sinners are watching the upright man, desiring to put him to death.

耶和华必不撇他在恶人手中，当审判的时候，也不定他的罪。
The Lord will not give him into their hands, or be against him when he is judged.

你当等候耶和华，遵守他的道，他就抬举你，使你承受地土。恶人被剪除的时候，你必看见。
Be waiting for the Lord, and keep his way; and you will be lifted up, and have the land for your heritage: when the evil-doers are cut off, you will see it.

我见过恶人大有势力，好像一根青翠树在本土生发。
I have seen the evil-doer in great power, covering the earth like a great tree.

有人从那里经过，不料，他没有了。我也寻找他，却寻不着。
But he came to an end, and there was no sign of him; I made a search for him and he was not there.

你要细察那完全人，观看那正直人。因为和平人有好结局。
Give attention to the good man, and take note of the upright; because the end of that man is peace.

至于犯法的人，必一同灭绝。恶人终必剪除。
But as for the sinners, they will be cut off together; the end of the wrongdoers is destruction.

但义人得救，是由于耶和华。他在患难时作他们的营寨。
But the Lord is the saviour of the upright: he is their strength in the time of trouble.

耶和华帮助他们，解救他们。他解救他们脱离恶人，把他们救出来，因为他们投靠他。
And the Lord will be their help, and keep them safe: he will take them out of the hands of the evil-doers, and be their saviour, because they had faith in him.

（大卫的记念诗）耶和华阿，求你不要在怒中责备我。不要在烈怒中惩罚我。
<A Psalm. Of David. To keep in memory.> O Lord, be not bitter with me in your wrath; let not your hand be on me in the heat of your passion.

因为你的箭射入我身，你的手压住我。
For your arrows have gone into my flesh, and I am crushed under the weight of your hand.

因你的恼怒，我的肉无一完全。因我的罪过，我的骨头也不安宁。
My flesh is wasted because of your wrath; and there is no peace in my bones because of my sin.

我的罪孽高过我的头，如同重担叫我担当不起。
For my crimes have gone over my head; they are like a great weight which is more than my strength.

因我的愚昧，我的伤发臭流脓。
My wounds are poisoned and evil-smelling, because of my foolish behaviour.

我疼痛，大大拳曲，终日哀痛。
I am troubled, I am made low; I go weeping all the day.

我满腰是火。我的肉无一完全。
For my body is full of burning; all my flesh is unhealthy.

我被压伤，身体疲倦。因心里不安，我就唉哼。
I am feeble and crushed down; I gave a cry like a lion because of the grief in my heart.

主阿，我的心愿都在你面前。我的叹息不向你隐瞒。
Lord, all my desire is before you; my sorrow is not kept secret from you.

我心跳动，我力衰微，连我眼中的光，也没有了。
My heart goes out in pain, my strength is wasting away; as for the light of my eyes, it is gone from me.

我的良朋密友，因我的灾病，都躲在旁边站着。我的亲戚本家，也远远地站立。
My lovers and my friends keep away from my disease; my relations keep far away.

那寻索我命的，设下网罗。那想要害我的，口出恶言，终日思想诡计。
Those who have a desire to take my life put nets for me; those who are designing my destruction say evil things against me, all the day their minds are full of deceit.

但我如聋子不听，像哑巴不开口。
But I kept my ears shut like a man without hearing; like a man without a voice, never opening his mouth.

我如不听见的人，口中没有回话。
So I was like a man whose ears are shut, and in whose mouth there are no sharp words.

耶和华阿，我仰望你。主我的神阿，你必应允我。
In you, O Lord, is my hope: you will give me an answer, O Lord, my God.

我曾说，恐怕他们向我夸耀。我失脚的时候，他们向我夸大。
I said, Let them not be glad over me; when my foot is moved, let them not be lifted up with pride against me.

我几乎跌倒，我的痛苦常在我面前。
My feet are near to falling, and my sorrow is ever before me.

我要承认我的罪孽。我要因我的罪忧愁。
I will make clear my wrongdoing, with sorrow in my heart for my sin.

但我的仇敌又活泼又强壮。无理恨我的增多了。
But they are strong who have hate for me without cause: those who are against me falsely are increased in numbers.

以恶报善的与我作对，因我是追求良善。
They give me back evil for good; they are my haters because I go after the thing which is right.

耶和华阿，求你不要撇弃我。我的神阿，求你不要远离我。
Do not give me up, O Lord; O my God, be near to me.

拯救我的主阿，求你快快帮助我。
Come quickly to give me help, O Lord, my salvation.

（大卫的诗，交与伶长耶杜顿。）我曾说，我要谨慎我的言行，免得我舌头犯罪。恶人在我面前的时候，我要用嚼环勒住我的口。
<To the chief music-maker. Of Jeduthun. A Psalm. Of David.> I said, I will give attention to my ways, so that my tongue may do no wrong; I will keep my mouth under control, while the sinner is before me.

我默然无声，连好话也不出口。我的愁苦就发动了。
I made no sound, I said no word, even of good; and I was moved with sorrow.

我的心在我里面发热。我默想的时候，火就烧起，我便用舌头说话。
My heart was burning in my breast; while I was deep in thought the fire was lighted; then I said with my tongue,

耶和华阿，求你叫我晓得我身之终，我的寿数几何，叫我知道我的生命不长。
Lord, give me knowledge of my end, and of the measure of my days, so that I may see how feeble I am.

你使我的年日，窄如手掌。我一生的年数，在你面前，如同无有。各人最稳妥的时候，真是全然虚幻。（细拉）
You have made my days no longer than a hand's measure; and my years are nothing in your eyes; truly, every man is but a breath. (Selah.)

世人行动实系幻影。他们忙乱，真是枉然。积蓄财宝，不知将来有谁收取。
Truly, every man goes on his way like an image; he is troubled for no purpose: he makes a great store of wealth, and has no knowledge of who will get it.

主阿，如今我等什么呢？我的指望在乎你。
And now, Lord, what am I waiting for? my hope is in you.

求你救我脱离一切的过犯。不要使我受愚顽人的羞辱。
Make me free from all my sins; do not let me be shamed by the man of evil behaviour.

因我所遭遇的是出于你，我就默然不语。
I was quiet, and kept my mouth shut; because you had done it.

求你把你的责罚，从我身上免去。因你手的责打，我便消灭。
No longer let your hand be hard on me; I am wasted by the blows of your hand.

你因人的罪恶，惩罚他的时候，叫他的笑容消灭，（的笑容或作所喜爱的）如衣被虫所咬。世人真是虚幻。（细拉）
By the weight of your wrath against man's sin, the glory of his form is wasted away; truly every man is but a breath. (Selah.)

耶和华阿。求你听我的祷告，留心听我的呼求。我流泪，求你不要静默无声。因为我在你面前是客旅，是寄居的，像我列祖一般。
Let my prayer come to your ears, O Lord, and give attention to my cry, make an answer to my weeping: for my time here is short before you, and in a little time I will be gone, like all my fathers.

求你宽容我，使我在去而不返之先，可以力量复原。
Let your wrath be turned away from me, so that I may be comforted, before I go away from here, and become nothing.

（大卫的诗，交与伶长）我曾耐性等候耶和华。他垂听我的呼求。
<To the chief music-maker. Of David. A Psalm.> When I was waiting quietly for the Lord, his heart was turned to me, and he gave ear to my cry.

他从祸坑里，从淤泥中，把我拉上来，使我的脚立在磐石上，使我脚步稳当。
He took me up out of a deep waste place, out of the soft and sticky earth; he put my feet on a rock, and made my steps certain.

他使我口唱新歌，就是赞美我们神的话。许多人必看见而惧怕，并要倚靠耶和华。
And he put a new song in my mouth, even praise to our God; numbers have seen it with fear, and put their faith in the Lord.

那倚靠耶和华，不理会狂傲和偏向虚假之辈的，这人便为有福。
Happy is the man who has faith in the Lord, and does not give honour to the men of pride or to those who are turned away to deceit.

耶和华我的神阿，你所行的奇事，并你向我们所怀的意念甚多，不能向你陈明。若要陈明，其事不可胜数。
O Lord my God, great are the wonders which you have done in your thought for us; it is not possible to put them out in order before you; when I would give an account of them, their number is greater than I may say.

祭物和礼物，你不喜悦。你已经开通我的耳朵。燔祭和赎罪祭，非你所要。
You had no desire for offerings of beasts or fruits of the earth; ears you made for me: for burned offerings and sin offerings you made no request.

那时我说，看哪，我来了。我的事在经卷上已经记载了。
Then I said, See, I come; it is recorded of me in the roll of the book,

我的神阿，我乐意照你的旨意行。你的律法在我心里。
My delight is to do your pleasure, O my God; truly, your law is in my heart.

我在大会中宣传公义的佳音。我必不止住我的嘴唇。耶和华阿，这是你所知道的。
I have given news of righteousness in the great meeting; O Lord, you have knowledge that I have not kept back my words.

我未曾把你的公义藏在心里。我已陈明你的信实，和你的救恩。我在大会中未曾隐瞒你的慈爱，和诚实。
