Your righteousness has not been folded away in my heart; I have made clear your true word and your salvation; I have not kept secret your mercy or your faith from the great meeting.

耶和华阿，求你不要向我止住你的慈悲。愿你的慈爱和诚实，常常保佑我。
Take not away your gentle mercies from me, O Lord; let your mercy and your faith keep me safe for ever.

因有无数的祸患围困我。我的罪孽追上了我，使我不能昂首。这罪孽比我的头发还多。我就心寒胆战。
For unnumbered evils are round about me; my sins have overtaken me, so that I am bent down with their weight; they are more than the hairs of my head, my strength is gone because of them.

耶和华阿，求你开恩搭救我。耶和华阿，求你速速帮助我。
Be pleased, O Lord, to take me out of danger; O Lord, come quickly and give me help.

愿那些寻找我，要灭我命的，一同抱愧蒙羞。愿那些喜悦我受害的，退后受辱。
Let those who go after my soul for its destruction have shame and trouble together; let them be turned back and made foolish who take pleasure in my trouble.

愿那些对我说，阿哈，阿哈的，因羞愧而败亡。
Let those who say to me, Aha, aha! be surprised because of their shame.

愿一切寻求你的，因你高兴欢喜。愿那些喜爱你救恩的，常说，当尊耶和华为大。
Let all those who are looking for you be glad and have joy in you; let the lovers of your salvation ever say, May the Lord be great.

但我是困苦穷乏的，主仍顾念我。你是帮助我的，搭救我的。神阿，求你不要耽延。
Though I am poor and in need, the Lord has me in mind; you are my help and my saviour; let there be no waiting, O my God.

（大卫的诗，交与伶长。）眷顾贫穷的有福了。他遭难的日子，耶和华必搭救他。
<To the chief music-maker. A Psalm. Of David.> Happy is the man who gives thought to the poor; the Lord will be his saviour in the time of trouble.

耶和华必保全他，使他存活。他必在地上享福。求你不要把他交给仇敌，遂其所愿。
The Lord will keep him safe, and give him life; the Lord will let him be a blessing on the earth, and will not give him into the hand of his haters.

他病重在榻，耶和华必扶持他。他在病中，你必给他铺床。
The Lord will be his support on his bed of pain: by you will all his grief be turned to strength.

我曾说，耶和华阿，求你怜恤我，医治我。因为我得罪了你。
I said, Lord, have mercy on me; make my soul well, because my faith is in you.

我的仇敌用恶言议论我，说，他几时死，他的名才灭亡呢？
My haters say evil against me, When will he be dead, and his name come to an end?

他来看我，就说假话。他心存奸恶，走到外边才说出来。
If one comes to see me, deceit is in his heart; he keeps a store of evil, which he makes public in every place.

一切恨我的，都交头接耳的议论我。他们设计要害我。
All my haters are talking secretly together against me; they are designing my downfall.

他们说，有怪病贴在他身上。他已躺卧，必不能再起来。
They say, He has an evil disease, which will not let him go: and now that he is down he will not get up again.

连我知己的朋友，我所倚靠吃过我饭的，也用脚踢我。
Even my dearest friend, in whom I had faith, who took bread with me, is turned against me.

耶和华阿，求你怜恤我，使我起来，好报复他们。
But you, O Lord, have mercy on me, lifting me up, so that I may give them their punishment.

因我的仇敌不得向我夸胜。我从此便知道你喜爱我。
By this I see that you have pleasure in me, because my hater does not overcome me.

你因我纯正，就扶持我，使我永远站在你的面前。
And as for me, you are my support in my righteousness, giving me a place before your face for ever.

耶和华以色列的神，是应当称颂的，从亘古直到永远。阿们，阿们。
May the Lord God of Israel be praised, through eternal days and for ever. So be it. So be it.

（可拉后裔的训诲诗，交与伶长。）神阿，我的心切慕你，如鹿切慕溪水。
<To the chief music-maker. Maschil. Of the sons of Korah.> Like the desire of the roe for the water-streams, so is my soul's desire for you, O God.

我的心渴想神，就是永生神。我几时得朝见神呢？
My soul is dry for need of God, the living God; when may I come and see the face of God?

我昼夜以眼泪当饮食。人不住地对我说，你的神在哪里呢？
My tears have been my food day and night, while they keep saying to me, Where is your God?

我从前与众人同往，用欢呼称赞的声音，领他们到神的殿里，大家守节。我追想这些事，我的心极其悲伤。
Let my soul be overflowing with grief when these things come back to my mind, how I went in company to the house of God, with the voice of joy and praise, with the song of those who were keeping the feast.

我的心哪，你为何忧闷，为何在我里面烦躁。应当仰望神。因他笑脸帮助我，我还要称赞他。
Why are you crushed down, O my soul? and why are you troubled in me? put your hope in God; for I will again give him praise who is my help and my God.

我的神阿，我的心在我里面忧闷。所以我从约但地，从黑门岭，从米萨山，记念你。
My soul is crushed down in me, so I will keep you in mind; from the land of Jordan and of the Hermons, from the hill Mizar.

你的瀑布发声，深渊就与深渊响应。你的波浪洪涛漫过我身。
Deep is sounding to deep at the noise of your waterfalls; all your waves have gone rolling over me.

白昼耶和华必向我施慈爱。黑夜我要歌颂祷告赐我生命的神。
But the Lord will send his mercy in the daytime, and in the night his song will be with me, a prayer to the God of my life.

我要对神我的磐石说，你为何忘记我呢？我为何因仇敌的欺压时常哀痛呢？
I will say to God my Rock, Why have you let me go from your memory? why do I go in sorrow because of the attacks of my haters?

我的敌人辱骂我，好像打碎我的骨头，不住地对我说，你的神在哪里呢？
The cruel words of my haters are like a crushing of my bones; when they say to me every day, Where is your God?

我的心哪，你为何忧闷？为何在我里面烦躁？应当仰望神。因我还要称赞他。他是我脸上的光荣，（原文作帮助），是我的神。
Why are you crushed down, O my soul? and why are you troubled in me? put your hope in God; for I will again give him praise who is my help and my God.

神阿，求你伸我的冤，向不虔诚的国，为我辨屈。求你救我脱离诡诈不义的人。
Be my judge, O God, supporting my cause against a nation without religion; O keep me from the false and evil man.

因为你是赐我力量的神，为何丢弃我呢？我为何因仇敌的欺压时常哀痛呢？
You are the God of my strength; why have you put me from you? why do I go in sorrow because of the attacks of my haters?

求你发出你的亮光和真实，好引导我，带我到你的圣山，到你的居所。
O send out your light and your true word; let them be my guide: let them take me to your holy hill, and to your tents.

我就走到神的祭坛，到我最喜乐的神那里。神阿，我的神，我要弹琴称赞你。
Then I will go up to the altar of God, to the God of my joy; I will be glad and give praise to you on an instrument of music, O God, my God.

我的心哪，你为何忧闷？为何在我里面烦躁？应当仰望神。因我还要称赞他。他是我脸上的光荣，（原文作帮助）是我的神。
Why are you crushed down, O my soul? and why are you troubled in me? put your hope in God, for I will again give him praise who is my help and my God.

（可拉后裔的训诲诗，交与伶长。）神阿，你在古时，我们列祖的日子，所行的事，我们亲耳听见了，我们的列祖，也给我们述说过。
<To the chief music-maker. Of the sons of Korah Maschil.> It has come to our ears, O God, our fathers have given us the story, of the works which you did in their days, in the old times,

你曾用手赶出外邦人，却栽培了我们列祖。你苦待列邦，却叫我们列祖发达。
Uprooting the nations with your hand, and planting our fathers in their place; cutting down the nations, but increasing the growth of your people.

因为他们不是靠自己的刀剑得地土，也不是靠自己的膀臂得胜。乃是靠你的右手，你的膀臂，和你脸上的亮光，因为你喜悦他们。
For they did not make the land theirs by their swords, and it was not their arms which kept them safe; but your right hand, and your arm, and the light of your face, because you had pleasure in them.

神阿，你是我的王，求你出令，使雅各得胜。
You are my King and my God; ordering salvation for Jacob.

我们靠你要推倒我们的敌人。靠你的名要践踏那起来攻击我们的人。
Through you will we overcome our haters; by your name will they be crushed under our feet who are violent against us.

因为我必不靠我的弓，我的刀也不能使我得胜。
I will not put faith in my bow, my sword will not be my salvation.

惟你救了我们脱离敌人，使恨我们的人羞愧。
But it is you who have been our saviour from those who were against us, and have put to shame those who had hate for us.

我们终日因神夸耀，还要永远称谢你的名。（细拉）
Our pride is in God at all times, to his name we give praise for ever. (Selah.)

但如今你丢弃了我们，使我们受辱，不和我们的军兵同去。
But now you have sent us away from you, and put us to shame; you do not go out with our armies.

你使我们向敌人转身退后。那恨我们的人任意抢夺。
Because of this we are turned back by the attacker: those who have hate for us take our goods for themselves.

你使我们当作快要被吃的羊，把我们分散在列邦中。
You have made us like sheep which are taken for meat; we are put to flight among the nations.

你卖了你的子民，也不赚利。所得的价值，并不加添你的资财。
You let your people go for nothing; your wealth is not increased by their price.

你使我们受邻国的羞辱，被四围的人嗤笑讥刺。
You have made us to be looked down on by our neighbours, we are laughed at and shamed by those who are round about us.

你使我们在列邦中作了笑谈，使众民向我们摇头。
Our name is a word of shame among the nations, a sign for the shaking of heads among the peoples.

我的凌辱，终日在我面前。我脸上的羞愧，将我遮蔽。
My downfall is ever before me, and I am covered with the shame of my face;

都因那辱骂毁谤人的声音，又因仇敌和报仇人的缘故。
Because of the voice of him who says sharp and bitter words; because of the hater and him who is the instrument of punishment.

这都临到我们身上。我们却没有忘记你。也没有违背你的约。
All this has come on us, but still we have kept you in our memory; and we have not been false to your word.

我们的心没有退后，我们的脚也没有偏离你的路。
Our hearts have not gone back, and our steps have not been turned out of your way;

你在野狗之处压伤我们，用死荫遮蔽我们。
Though you have let us be crushed in the place of jackals, though we are covered with darkest shade.

倘若我们忘了神的名，或向别神举手，
If the name of our God has gone out of our minds, or if our hands have been stretched out to a strange god,

神岂不鉴察这事吗？因为他晓得人心里的隐秘。
Will not God make search for it? for he sees the secrets of the heart.

我们为你的缘故终日被杀，人看我们如将宰的羊。
Truly, because of you we are put to death every day; we are numbered like sheep for destruction.

主阿，求你睡醒，为何尽睡呢？求你兴起，不要永远丢弃我们。
Why are you sleeping, O Lord? awake! and come to our help, do not give us up for ever.

你为何掩面，不顾我们所遭的苦难，和所受的欺压。
Why is your face covered, and why do you give no thought to our trouble and our cruel fate?

我们的性命伏于尘土。我们的肚腹紧贴地面。
For our souls are crushed down to the dust: our bodies are stretched out on the earth.

求你起来帮助我们，凭你的慈爱救赎我们。
Up! and come to our help, and give us salvation because of your mercy.

（可拉后裔的训诲诗，又是爱慕歌，交与伶长，调用百合花。）我心里涌出美辞。我论到我为王作的事。我的舌头是快手笔。
<To the chief music-maker; put to Shoshannim. Of the sons of Korah. Maschil. A Song of loves.> My heart is flowing over with good things; my words are of that which I have made for a king; my tongue is the pen of a ready writer.

你比世人更美，在你嘴里满有恩惠。所以神赐福给你，直到永远。
You are fairer than the children of men; grace is flowing through your lips; for this cause the blessing of God is with you for ever.

大能者阿，愿你腰间佩刀，大有荣耀和威严。
Put on your sword, make it ready at your side, O strong chief, with your glory and power.

为真理，谦卑，公义，赫然坐车前往，无不得胜。你的右手必显明可畏的事。
And go nobly on in your power, because you are good and true and without pride; and your right hand will be teaching you things of fear.

你的箭锋快，射中王敌之心。万民仆倒在你以下。
Your arrows are sharp in the heart of the king's haters; because of them the peoples are falling under you.

神阿，你的宝座是永永远远的，你的国权是正直的。
Your seat of power, O God, is for ever and ever; the rod of your kingdom is a rod of honour.

你喜爱公义，恨恶罪恶。所以神，就是你的神，用喜乐油膏你，胜过膏你的同伴。
You have been a lover of righteousness and a hater of evil: and so God, your God, has put the oil of joy on your head, lifting you high over all other kings.

你的衣服，都有没药沉香肉桂的香气。象牙宫中有丝弦乐器的声音，使你欢喜。
Your robes are full of the smell of all sorts of perfumes and spices; music from the king's ivory houses has made you glad.

有君王的女儿，在你尊贵妇女之中。王后佩戴俄斐金饰，站在你右边。
Kings' daughters are among your noble women: on your right is the queen in gold of Ophir.

女子阿，你要听，要想，要侧耳而听。不要记念你的民，和你的父家。
O daughter, give thought and attention, and let your ear be open; no longer keep in mind your people, and your father's house;

王就羡慕你的美貌。因为他是你的主。你当敬拜他。
So will the king have a great desire for you, seeing how beautiful you are; because he is your lord, give him honour.

推罗的民，（民原文作女子），必来送礼。民中的富足人，也必向你求恩。
And the daughters of Tyre will be there with an offering; those who have wealth among the people will be looking for your approval.

王女在宫里，极其荣华。他的衣服是用金线绣的。
In the great house the king's daughter is all shining: her clothing is worked with gold.

他要穿锦绣的衣服，被引到王前。随从他的陪伴童女，也要被带到你面前。
She will come before the king in robes of needlework; the virgins in her train will come before you.

他们要欢喜快乐被引导。他们要进入王宫。
With joy and rapture will they come; they will go into the king's house.

你的子孙要接续你的列祖。你要立他们在全地作王。
Your children will take the place of your fathers; so that you may make them rulers over all the earth.

我必叫你的名被万代记念。所以万民要永永远远称谢你。
I will keep the memory of your name living through all generations; and because of this the people will give you praise for ever.

（可拉后裔的诗歌，交与伶长，调用女音。）神是我们的避难所，是我们的力量，是我们在患难中随时的帮助。
<To the chief music-maker. Of the sons of Korah; put to Alamoth. A Song.> God is our harbour and our strength, a very present help in trouble.

所以地虽改变，山虽摇动到海心，
For this cause we will have no fear, even though the earth is changed, and though the mountains are moved in the heart of the sea;

其中的水虽砰訇翻腾，山虽因海涨而战抖，我们也不害怕。（细拉）。
Though its waters are sounding and troubled, and though the mountains are shaking with their violent motion. (Selah.)

有一道河。这河的分汊，使神的城欢喜。这城就是至高者居住的圣所。
There is a river whose streams make glad the resting-place of God, the holy place of the tents of the Most High.

神在其中。城必不动摇。到天一亮，神必帮助这城。
God has taken his place in her; she will not be moved: he will come to her help at the dawn of morning.

外邦喧嚷，列国动摇。神发声，地便熔化。
The nations were angry, the kingdoms were moved; at the sound of his voice the earth became like wax.

万军之耶和华与我们同在。雅各的神是我们的避难所。（细拉）。
The Lord of armies is with us; the God of Jacob is our high tower. (Selah.)

你们来看耶和华的作为，看他使地怎样荒凉。
Come, see the works of the Lord, the destruction which he has made in the earth.

他止息刀兵，直到地极。他折弓断枪，把战车焚烧在火中。
He puts an end to wars over all the earth; by him the bow is broken, and the spear cut in two, and the carriage burned in the fire.

你们要休息，要知道我是神。我必在外邦中被尊崇，在遍地上也被尊崇。
Be at peace in the knowledge that I am God: I will be lifted up among the nations, I will be honoured through all the earth.

万军之耶和华与我们同在。雅各的神，是我们的避难所。
The Lord of armies is with us; the God of Jacob is our high tower. (Selah.)

（可拉后裔的诗，交与伶长。）万民哪，你们都要拍掌。要用夸胜的声音向神呼喊。
<To the chief music-maker. A Psalm. Of the sons of Korah.> O make a glad noise with your hands, all you peoples; letting your voices go up to God with joy.

因为耶和华至高者是可畏的。他是治理全地的大君王。
For the Lord Most High is to be feared; he is a great King over all the earth.

他叫万民服在我们以下，又叫列邦服在我们脚下。
He will put down the peoples under us, and the nations under our feet.

他为我们选择产业，就是他所爱之雅各的荣耀。（细拉）。
He will give us our heritage, the glory of Jacob who is dear to him. (Selah.)

神上升，有喊声相送。耶和华上升，有角声相送。
God has gone up with a glad cry, the Lord with the sound of the horn.

你们要向神歌颂，歌颂，向我们王歌颂，歌颂。
Give praises to God, make songs of praise; give praises to our King, make songs of praise.

因为神是全地的王。你们要用悟性歌颂。
For God is the King of all the earth; make songs of praise with knowledge.

神作王治理万国。神坐在他的圣宝座上。
God is the ruler over the nations; God is on the high seat of his holy rule.

列邦的君王聚集，要作亚伯拉罕之神的民。因为世界的盾牌，是属神的。他为至高。
The rulers of the peoples have come together, with the people of the God of Abraham; because the powers of the earth are God's: he is lifted up on high.

（可拉后裔的诗歌。）耶和华本为大，在我们神的城中，在他的圣山上，该受大赞美。
<A Song. A Psalm. Of the sons of Korah.> Great is the Lord and greatly to be praised, in the town of our God, in his holy mountain.

锡安山，大君王的城，在北面居高华美，为全地所喜悦。
Beautiful in its high position, the joy of all the earth, is the mountain of Zion, the mountain of God, the town of the great King.

神在其宫中自显为避难所。
In its buildings God is seen to be a high tower.

看哪，众王会合，一同经过。
For see! the kings came together by agreement, they were joined together.

他们见了这城，就惊奇丧胆，急忙逃跑。
They saw it, and so were full of wonder; they were troubled, and went quickly away in fear.

他们在那里被战兢疼痛抓住，好像产难的妇人一样。
Shaking came on them and pain, as on a woman in childbirth.

神阿，你用东风打破他施的船只。
By you the ships of Tarshish are broken as by an east wind.

我们在万军之耶和华的城中，就是我们神的城中，所看见的，正如我们所听见的。神必坚立这城，直到永远。（细拉）。
As it came to our ears so have we seen it, in the town of the Lord of armies, in the town of our God; God will keep it fixed for ever. (Selah.)

神阿，我们在你的殿中，想念你的慈爱。
Our thoughts were of your mercy, O God, while we were in your Temple.

神阿，你受的赞美，正与你的名相称，直到地极。你的右手满了公义。
As your name is, O God, so is your praise to the ends of the earth; your right hand is full of righteousness.

因你的判断，锡安山应当欢喜，犹大的城邑，应当快乐。（城邑原文作女子）
Let there be joy in the mountain of Zion, and let the daughters of Judah be glad, because of your wise decisions.

你们当周游锡安，四围旋绕，数点城楼，
Make your way about Zion, and go round it, numbering its towers.

细看他的外郭，察看他的宫殿，为要传说到后代。
Take note of its strong walls, looking well at its fair buildings; so that you may give word of it to the generation which comes after.

因为这神永永远远为我们的神。他必作我们引路的，直到死时。
Because this God is our God for ever and ever: he will be our guide.

（可拉后裔的诗，交与伶长。）万民哪，你们都当听这话，世上一切的居民，
<Alamoth. To the chief music-maker. Of the sons of Korah. A Psalm.> Give attention to this, all you peoples; let your ears be open, all you who are living in the world.

无论上流下流，富足贫穷，都当留心听。
High and low together, the poor, and those who have wealth.

我口要说智慧的言语。我心要想通达的道理。
From my mouth will come words of wisdom; and in the thoughts of my heart will be knowledge.

我要侧耳听比喻，用琴解谜语。
I will put my teaching into a story; I will make my dark sayings clear with music.

在患难的日子，奸恶随我脚跟，四面环绕我，我何必惧怕。
What cause have I for fear in the days of evil, when the evil-doing of those who are working for my downfall is round about me?

那些倚仗财货自夸钱财多的人，
Even of those whose faith is in their wealth, and whose hearts are lifted up because of their stores.

一个也无法赎自己的弟兄，也不能替他将赎价给神，
Truly, no man may get back his soul for a price, or give to God the payment for himself;

叫他长远活着，不见朽坏。因为赎他生命的价值极贵，只可永远罢休。
(Because it takes a great price to keep his soul from death, and man is not able to give it.)


So that he might have eternal life, and never see the underworld.

他必见智慧人死。又见愚顽人和畜类人，一同灭亡，将他们的财货留给别人。
For he sees that wise men come to their end, and foolish persons of low behaviour come to destruction together, letting their wealth go to others.

他们心里思想，他们的家室必永存，住宅必留到万代。他们以自己的名，称自己的地。
The place of the dead is their house for ever, and their resting-place through all generations; those who come after them give their names to their lands.

但人居尊贵中不能长久，如同死亡的畜类一样。
But man, like the animals, does not go on for ever; he comes to an end like the beasts.

他们行的这道，本为自己的愚昧。但他们以后的人，还佩服他们的话语。（细拉）。
This is the way of the foolish; their silver is for those who come after them, and their children get the pleasure of their gold. (Selah.)

他们如同羊群派定下阴间。死亡必作他们的牧者。到了早晨，正直人必管辖他们。他们的美容，必被阴间所灭，以致无处可存。
Death will give them their food like sheep; the underworld is their fate and they will go down into it; their flesh is food for worms; their form is wasted away; the underworld is their resting-place for ever.

只是神必救赎我的灵魂，脱离阴间的权柄，因他必收纳我。（细拉）
But God will get back my soul; for he will take me from the power of death. (Selah.)

见人发财家室增荣的时候，你不要惧怕。
Have no fear when wealth comes to a man, and the glory of his house is increased;

因为他死的时候，什么也不能带去。他的荣耀不能随他下去。
For at his death, he will take nothing away; his glory will not go down after him.

他活着的时候，虽然自夸为有福，（你若利己，人必夸奖你）。
Though he might have pride in his soul in his life-time, and men will give you praise if you do well for yourself,

他仍必归到他历代的祖宗那里，永不见光。
He will go to the generation of his fathers; he will not see the light again.

人在尊贵中，而不醒悟，就如死亡的畜类一样。
Man, like the animals, does not go on for ever; he comes to an end like the beasts.

（亚萨的诗。）大能者神耶和华，已经发言招呼天下，从日出之地到日落之处。
<A Psalm. Of Asaph.> The God of gods, even the Lord, has sent out his voice, and the earth is full of fear; from the coming up of the sun to its going down.

从全美的锡安中，神已经发光了。
From Zion, most beautiful of places, God has sent out his light.

我们的神要来，决不闭口。有烈火在他面前吞灭，有暴风在他四围大刮。
Our God will come, and will not keep quiet; with fire burning before him, and storm-winds round him.

他招呼上天下地，为要审判他的民，
His voice will go out to the heavens and to the earth, for the judging of his people:

说，招聚我的圣民到我这里来，就是那些用祭物与我立约的人。
Let my saints come together to me; those who have made an agreement with me by offerings.

诸天必表明他的公义。因为神是施行审判的。（细拉）
And let the heavens make clear his righteousness; for God himself is the judge. (Selah.)

我的民哪，你们当听我的话。以色列阿，我要劝戒你。我是神，是你的神。
Give ear, O my people, to my words; O Israel, I will be a witness against you; I am God, even your God.

我并不因你的祭物责备你。你的燔祭常在我面前。
I will not take up a cause against you because of your offerings, or because of your burned offerings, which are ever before me.

我不从你家中取公牛，也不从你圈内取山羊。
I will take no ox out of your house, or he-goats from your flocks;

因为树林中的百兽是我的，千山上的牲畜也是我的。
For every beast of the woodland is mine, and the cattle on a thousand hills.

山中的飞鸟，我都知道。野地的走兽，也都属我。
I see all the birds of the mountains, and the beasts of the field are mine.

我若是饥饿，我不用告诉你。因为世界，和其中所充满的，都是我的。
If I had need of food, I would not give you word of it; for the earth is mine and all its wealth.

我岂吃公牛的肉呢？我岂喝山羊的血呢？
Am I to take the flesh of the ox for my food, or the blood of goats for my drink?

你们要以感谢为祭献与神。又要向至高者还你的愿。
Make an offering of praise to God; keep the agreements which you have made with the Most High;

并要在患难之日求告我，我必搭救你。你也要荣耀我。
Let your voice come up to me in the day of trouble; I will be your saviour, so that you may give glory to me.

但神对恶人说，你怎敢传说我的律例，口中提到我的约呢？
But to the sinner, God says, What are you doing, talking of my laws, or taking the words of my agreement in your mouth?

其实你恨恶管教，将我的言语丢在背后。
Seeing that you have no desire for my teaching, turning your back on my words.

你见了盗贼，就乐意与他同伙，又与行奸淫的人，一同有分。
When you saw a thief, you were in agreement with him, and you were joined with those who took other men's wives.

你口任说恶言，你舌编造诡诈。
You have given your mouth to evil, your tongue to words of deceit.

你坐着毁谤你的兄弟，谗毁你亲母的儿子。
You say evil of your brother; you make false statements against your mother's son.

你行了这些事，我还闭口不言。你想我恰和你一样。其实我要责备你，将这些事摆在你眼前。
These things have you done, and I said nothing; it seemed to you that I was such a one as yourself; but I will make a protest against you, and put them in order before your eyes.

你们忘记神的，要思想这事，免得我把你们撕碎，无人搭救。
Now keep this in mind, you who have no memory of God, for fear that you may be crushed under my hand, with no one to give you help:

凡以感谢献上为祭的，便是荣耀我。那按正路而行的，我必使他得着我的救恩。
Whoever makes an offering of praise gives glory to me; and to him who is upright in his ways I will make clear the salvation of God.

（大卫与拔示巴同室以后，先知拿单来见他。他作这诗，交与伶长。）神阿，求你按你的慈爱怜恤我，按你丰盛的慈悲涂抹我的过犯。
<To the chief music-maker. A Psalm. Of David. When Nathan the prophet came to him, after he had gone in to Bath-sheba.> Have pity on me, O God, in your mercy; out of a full heart, take away my sin.

求你将我的罪孽洗除净尽，并洁除我的罪。
Let all my wrongdoing be washed away, and make me clean from evil.

因为我知道我的过犯，我的罪常在我面前。
For I am conscious of my error; my sin is ever before me.

我向你犯罪，惟独得罪了你，在你眼前行了这恶，以致你责备我的时候，显为公义。判断我的时候，显为清正。
Against you, you only, have I done wrong, working that which is evil in your eyes; so that your words may be seen to be right, and you may be clear when you are judging.

我是在罪孽里生的。在我母亲怀胎的时候，就有了罪。
Truly, I was formed in evil, and in sin did my mother give me birth.

你所喜爱的，是内里诚实。你在我隐密处，必使我得智慧。
Your desire is for what is true in the inner parts: in the secrets of my soul you will give me knowledge of wisdom.

求你用牛膝草洁净我，我就干净，求你洗涤我，我就比雪更白。
Make me free from sin with hyssop: let me be washed whiter than snow.

求你使我得听欢喜快乐的声音，使你所压伤的骨头，可以踊跃。
Make me full of joy and rapture; so that the bones which have been broken may be glad.

求你掩面不看我的罪，涂抹我一切的罪孽。
Let your face be turned from my wrongdoing, and take away all my sins.

神阿，求你为我造清洁的心，使我里面重新有正直的灵。（正直或作坚定）。
Make a clean heart in me, O God; give me a right spirit again.

不要丢弃我，使我离开你的面。不要从我收回你的圣灵。
Do not put me away from before you, or take your holy spirit from me.

求你使我仍得救恩之乐，赐我乐意的灵扶持我。
Give me back the joy of your salvation; let a free spirit be my support.

我就把你的道指教有过犯的人。罪人必归顺你。
Then will I make your ways clear to wrongdoers; and sinners will be turned to you.

神阿，你是拯救我的神。求你救我脱离流人血的罪。我的舌头就高声歌唱你的公义。
Be my saviour from violent death, O God, the God of my salvation; and my tongue will give praise to your righteousness.

主阿，求你使我嘴唇张开，我的口便传扬赞美你的话。
O Lord, let my lips be open, so that my mouth may make clear your praise.

你本不喜爱祭物。若喜爱，我就献上。燔祭你也不喜悦。
You have no desire for an offering or I would give it; you have no delight in burned offerings.

神所要的祭，就是忧伤的灵。神阿，忧伤痛悔的心，你必不轻看。
The offerings of God are a broken spirit; a broken and sorrowing heart, O God, you will not put from you.

求你随你的美意善待锡安，建造耶路撒冷的城墙。
Do good to Zion in your good pleasure, building up the walls of Jerusalem.

那时，你必喜爱公义的祭，和燔祭并全牲的燔祭。那时，人必将公牛献在你坛上。
Then you will have delight in the offerings of righteousness, in burned offerings and offerings of beasts; then they will make offerings of oxen on your altar.

（以东人多益来告诉扫罗说，大卫到了亚希米勒家。那时，大卫作这训诲诗，交与伶长。）勇士阿，你为何以作恶自夸。神的慈爱是常存的。
<To the chief music-maker. Maschil. Of David. When Doeg the Edomite came to Saul saying, David has come to the house of Ahimelech.> Why do you take pride in wrongdoing, lifting yourself up against the upright man all the day?

你的舌头邪恶诡诈，好像剃头刀，快利伤人。
Purposing destruction, using deceit; your tongue is like a sharp blade.

你爱恶胜似爱善，又爱说谎，不爱说公义。（细拉）
You have more love for evil than for good, for deceit than for works of righteousness. (Selah.)

诡诈的舌头阿，你爱说一切毁灭的话。
Destruction is in all your words, O false tongue.

神也要毁灭你，直到永远。他要把你拿去，从你的帐棚中抽出，从活人之地将你拔出。（细拉）
But God will put an end to you for ever; driving you out from your tent, uprooting you from the land of the living. (Selah.)

义人要看见而惧怕，并要笑他。
The upright will see it with fear, and will say, laughing at you:

说，看哪，这就是那不以神为他力量的人。只倚仗他丰富的财物，在邪恶上坚立自己。
See, this is the man who did not make God his strength, but had faith in his goods and his property, and made himself strong in his wealth.

至于我，就像神殿中的青橄榄树。我永永远远倚靠神的慈爱。
But I am like a branching olive-tree in the house of God; I have put my faith in his mercy for ever and ever.

我要称谢你，直到永远，因为你行了这事。我也要在你圣民面前仰望你的名。这名本为美好。
I will give you praise without end for what you have done; I will give honour to your name before your saints, for it is good.

（大卫的训诲诗，交与伶长，调用麻哈拉。）愚顽人心里说，没有神。他们都是邪恶，行了可憎恶的罪孽。没有一个人行善。
<To the chief music-maker; put to Mahalath. Maschil. Of David.> The foolish man has said in his heart, God will not do anything. They are unclean, they have done evil works; there is not one who does good.

神从天上垂看世人，要看有明白的没有，有寻求他的没有。
God was looking down from heaven on the children of men, to see if there were any who had wisdom, searching after God.

他们各人都退后，一同变为污秽。并没有行善的。连一个也没有。
Every one of them has gone back; they are unclean: there is not one who does good, no, not one.

作孽的没有知识吗？他们吞吃我的百姓如同吃饭一样。并不求告神。
Have the workers of evil no knowledge? they take my people for food, as they would take bread; they make no prayer to God.

他们在无可惧怕之处，就大大害怕。因为神把那安营攻击你之人的骨头散开了。你使他们蒙羞，因为神弃绝了他们。
They were in great fear, where there was no cause for fear: for the bones of those who make war on you have been broken by God; you have put them to shame, because God has no desire for them.

但愿以色列的救恩从锡安而出。神救回他被掳的子民，那时，雅各要快乐，以色列要欢喜。
May the salvation of Israel come out of Zion! When the fate of his people is changed by God, Jacob will have joy, and Israel will be glad.

（西弗人来对扫罗说，大卫岂不是在我们那里藏身吗？那时大卫作这训诲诗，交与伶长。用丝弦的乐器。）神阿，求你以你的名救我，凭你的大能为我伸冤。
<To the chief music-maker; on Neginoth. Maschil. Of David. When the Ziphites came and said to Saul, Is not David keeping himself secret among us?> Let your name be my salvation, O God; let my cause be judged by your strength.

神阿，求你听我的祷告，留心听我口中的言语。
Let my prayer come before you, O God; give ear to the words of my mouth.

因为外人起来攻击我，强暴人寻索我的命。他们眼中没有神。（细拉）
For men who are going after me have come out against me, violent men are purposing to take my soul; they have not put God before their eyes. (Selah.)

神是帮助我的，是扶持我命的。
See, God is my helper: the Lord is the great supporter of my soul.

他要报应我仇敌所行的恶。求你凭你的诚实灭绝他们。
Let the evil works of my haters come back on them again; let them be cut off by your good faith.

我要把甘心祭献给你。耶和华阿，我要称赞你的名。这名本为美好。
Freely will I make my offerings to you; I will give praise to your name, O Lord, for it is good.

他从一切的急难中，把我救出来。我的眼睛也看见了我仇敌遭报。
Because it has been my saviour from all my trouble; and my eyes have seen the punishment of my haters.

（大卫的训诲诗，交与伶长，用丝弦的乐器）神阿，求你留心听我的祷告。不要隐藏不听我的恳求。
<To the chief music-maker, on Neginoth. Maschil. Of David.> Give hearing to my prayer, O God; and let not your ear be shut against my request.

求你侧耳听我，应允我。我哀叹不安，发声唉哼。
Give thought to me, and let my prayer be answered: I have been made low in sorrow;

都因仇敌的声音，恶人的欺压。因为他们将罪孽加在我身上，发怒气逼迫我。
I am troubled because of the voice of the cruel ones, because of the loud cry of the evil-doers; for they put a weight of evil on me, and they are cruel in their hate for me.

我心在我里面甚是疼痛。死的惊惶临到我身。
My heart is deeply wounded, and the fear of death has come on me.

恐惧战兢归到我身，惊恐漫过了我。
Fear and shaking have come over me, with deep fear I am covered.

我说，但愿我有翅膀像鸽子，我就飞去得享安息。
And I said, If only I had wings like a dove! for then I would go in flight from here and be at rest.

我必远游宿在旷野。（细拉）
I would go wandering far away, living in the waste land. (Selah.)

我必速速逃到避所，脱离狂风暴雨。
I would quickly take cover from the driving storm and from the violent wind.

主阿，求你吞灭他们，变乱他们的舌头。因为我在城中见了强暴争竞的事。
Send destruction on them, O Lord, make a division of tongues among them: for I have seen fighting and violent acts in the town.

他们在城墙上昼夜绕行。在城内也有罪孽和奸恶。
By day and night they go round the town, on the walls; trouble and sorrow are in the heart of it.

邪恶在其中，欺压和诡诈不离街市。
Evil is there; cruel rule and deceit are ever in the streets.

原来不是仇敌辱骂我。若是仇敌，还可忍耐。也不是恨我的人向我狂大。若是恨我的人，就必躲避他。
For it was not my hater who said evil of me; that would have been no grief to me; it was not one outside the number of my friends who made himself strong against me, or I would have kept myself from him in a secret place;

不料是你，你原与我平等，是我的同伴，是我知己的朋友。
But it was you, my equal, my guide, my well-loved friend.

我们素常彼此谈论，以为甘甜。我们与群众在神的殿中同行。
We had loving talk together, and went to the house of God in company.

愿死亡忽然临到他们。愿他们活活地下入阴间。因为他们的住处，他们的心中，都是邪恶。
Let the hand of death come on them suddenly, and let them go down living into the underworld; because evil is in their houses and in their hearts.

至于我，我要求告神。耶和华必拯救我。
As for me, I will make my prayer to God, and he will be my saviour.

我要晚上，早晨，晌午，哀声悲叹。他也必听我的声音。
In the evening and in the morning and in the middle of the day I will make my prayer with sounds of grief; and my voice will come to his ears.

他救赎我命脱离攻击我的人，使我得享平安。因为与我相争的人甚多。
He has taken my soul away from the attack which was made against me, and given it peace; for great numbers were against me.

那没有更变，不敬畏神的人，从太古常存的神，必听见而苦待他。
God will give thought to me; he who from early times is strong will send pain and trouble on them. (Selah.) Because they are unchanged, they have no fear of God.

他背了约，伸手攻击与他和好的人。
He has put out his hand against those who were at peace with him; he has not kept his agreement.

他的口如奶油光滑，他的心却怀着争战。他的话比油柔和，其实是拔出来的刀。
The words of his mouth were smoother than butter, but war was in his heart; his words were softer than oil, but they were sharp swords.

你要把你的重担卸给耶和华，他必抚养你，他永不叫义人动摇。
Put your cares on the Lord, and he will be your support; he will not let the upright man be moved.

神阿，你必使恶人下入灭亡的坑。流人血行诡诈的人，必活不到半世，但我要倚靠你。
But you, O God, will send them down into the underworld; the cruel and the false will be cut off before half their days are ended; but I will have faith in you.

（非利士人在迦特拿住大卫。那时他作这金诗，交与伶长，调用远方无声鸽）神阿，求你怜悯我，因为人要把我吞了，终日攻击欺压我。
<To the chief music-maker; put to Jonath elem rehokim. Of David. Michtam. When the Philistines took him in Gath.> Have mercy on me, O God, for man is attempting my destruction; every day he makes cruel attacks against me.

我的仇敌终日要把我吞了。因逞骄傲攻击我的人甚多。
My haters are ever ready to put an end to me; great numbers are lifting themselves up against me.

我惧怕的时候要倚靠你。
In the time of my fear, I will have faith in you.

我倚靠神。我要赞美他的话。我倚靠神，必不惧怕。血气之辈能把我怎么样呢？
In God will I give praise to his word; in God have I put my hope; I will have no fear of what flesh may do to me.

他们终日颠倒我的话。他们一切的心思，都是要害我。
Every day they make wrong use of my words; all their thoughts are against me for evil.

他们聚集，埋伏窥探我的脚踪。等候要害我的命。
They come together, they are waiting in secret places, they take note of my steps, they are waiting for my soul.

他们岂能因罪孽逃脱吗？神阿，求你在怒中使众民堕落。
By evil-doing they will not get free from punishment. In wrath, O God, let the peoples be made low.

我几次流离，你都记数。求你把我眼泪装在你的皮袋里。这不都记在你册子上吗？
You have seen my wanderings; put the drops from my eyes into your bottle; are they not in your record?

我呼求的日子，我的仇敌都要转身退后。神帮助我，这是我所知道的。
When I send up my cry to you, my haters will be turned back; I am certain of this, for God is with me.

我倚靠神。我要赞美他的话。我倚靠耶和华。我要赞美他的话。
In God will I give praise to his word; in the Lord will I give praise to his word.

我倚靠神，必不惧怕。人能把我怎么样呢？
In God have I put my hope, I will have no fear of what man may do to me.

神阿，我向你所许的愿在我身上。我要将感谢祭献给你。
I keep the memory of my debt to you, O God; I will give you the offerings of praise.

因为你救我的命脱离死亡。你岂不是救护我的脚不跌倒，使我在生命光中行在神面前吗？
Because you have taken my soul from the power of death; and kept my feet from falling, so that I may be walking before God in the light of life.

（大卫逃避扫罗，藏在洞里。那时他作这金诗，交与伶长，调用休要毁坏）神阿，求你怜悯我，怜悯我。因为我的心投靠你。我要投靠在你翅膀的荫下，等到灾害过去。
<To the chief music-maker; put to Al-tashheth. Michtam. Of David. When he went in flight from Saul, in the hole of the rock.> Have mercy on me, O God, have mercy on me; for the hope of my soul is in you: I will keep myself safely under the shade of your wings, till these troubles are past.

我要求告至高的神，就是为我成全诸事的神。
I will send up my cry to the Most High God; to God who does all things for me.

那要吞我的人辱骂我的时候，神从天上必施恩救我。也必向我发出慈爱和诚实。
He will send from heaven, and take me from the power of him whose desire is for my destruction. God will send out his mercy and his good faith.

我的性命在狮子中间。我躺卧在性如烈火的世人当中。他们的牙齿是枪，箭。他们的舌头是快刀。
My soul is among lions; I am stretched out among those who are on fire, even the sons of men, whose teeth are spears and arrows, and whose tongue is a sharp sword.

神阿，愿你崇高，过于诸天。愿你的荣耀，高过全地。
O God, be lifted up higher than the heavens; let your glory be over all the earth.

他们为我的脚设下网罗，压制我的心。他们在我面前挖了坑，自己反掉在其中。（细拉）
They have made ready a net for my steps; my soul is bent down; they have made a great hole before me, and have gone down into it themselves. (Selah.)

神阿，我心坚定，我心坚定。我要唱诗，我要歌颂。
My heart is fixed, O God, my heart is fixed; I will make songs, and give praise.

我的灵阿，（原文作荣耀）你当醒起，琴瑟阿，你们当醒起。我自己要极早醒起。
You are my glory; let the instruments of music be awake; I myself will be awake with the dawn.

主阿，我要在万民中称谢你。在列邦中歌颂你。
I will give you praise, O Lord, among the peoples; I will make songs to you among the nations.

因为你的慈爱，高及诸天。你的诚实，达到穹苍。
For your mercy is great, stretching up to the heavens, and your righteousness goes up to the clouds.

神阿，愿你崇高，过于诸天。愿你的荣耀，高过全地。
Be lifted up, O God, higher than the heavens, let your glory be over all the earth.

（大卫的金诗，交与伶长，调用休要毁坏）世人哪，你们默然不语，真合公义吗？施行审判，岂按正直吗？
<To the chief music-maker; put to Al-tashheth. Michtam. Of David.> Is there righteousness in your mouths, O you gods? are you upright judges, O you sons of men?

不然，你们是心中作恶。你们在地上秤出你们手所行的强暴。
The purposes of your hearts are evil; your hands are full of cruel doings on the earth.

恶人一出母胎，就与神疏远。一离母腹，便走错路，说谎话。
The evil-doers are strange from the first; from the hour of their birth they go out of the true way, saying false words.

他们的毒气，好像蛇的毒气。他们好像塞耳的聋虺，
Their poison is like the poison of a snake; they are like the adder, whose ears are shut;

不听行法术的声音。虽用极灵的咒语，也是不听。
Who will not be moved by the voice of the wonder-worker, however great are his powers.

神阿，求你敲碎他们口中的牙。耶和华阿，求你敲掉少壮狮子的大牙。
O God, let their teeth be broken in their mouths; let the great teeth of the young lions be pulled out, O Lord.

愿他们消灭如急流的水一般。他们瞅准射箭的时候，愿箭头仿佛砍断。
Let them be turned to liquid like the ever-flowing waters; let them be cut off like the grass by the way.

愿他们像蜗牛消化过去，又像妇人坠落未见天日的胎。
Let them be like an after-birth which is turned to water and comes to an end; like the fruit of a woman who gives birth before her time, let them not see the sun.

你们用荆棘烧火。锅还未热，他要用旋风把青的和烧着的一齐刮去。
Before they are conscious of it, let them be cut down like thorns; let a strong wind take them away like waste growth.

义人见仇敌遭报，就欢喜，要在恶人的血中洗脚。
The upright man will be glad when he sees their punishment; his feet will be washed in the blood of the evil-doer.

因此，人必说，义人诚然有善报。在地上果有施行判断的神。
So that men will say, Truly there is a reward for righteousness; truly there is a God who is judge on the earth.

（扫罗打发人窥探大卫的房屋，要杀他。那时大卫用这金诗，交与伶长，调用休要毁坏）我的神阿，求你救我脱离仇敌，把我安置在高处，得脱那些起来攻击我的人。
<To the chief music-maker; put to At-tashheth. Michtam. Of David. When Saul sent, and they were watching the house, to put him to death.> Take me out of the hands of the cruel ones, O my God; keep me safe from those who come up against me.

求你救我脱离作孽的人，和喜爱流人血的人。
Take me out of the power of the workers of evil, and keep me safe from the men of blood.

因为他们埋伏，要害我的命，有能力的人聚集来攻击我。耶和华阿，这不是为我的过犯，也不是为我的罪愆。
For see, they are watching in secret for my soul; the strong have come together against me? but not because of my sin, or my evil-doing, O Lord.

我虽然无过，他们预备整齐，跑来攻击我。求你兴起鉴察帮助我。
For no sin of mine they go quickly and get themselves ready; be awake and come to my help, and see.

万军之神耶和华以色列的神阿，求你兴起，惩治万邦。不要怜悯行诡诈的恶人。（细拉）
You, O Lord God of armies, are the God of Israel; come now and give punishment to the nations; have no mercy on any workers of deceit. (Selah.)

他们晚上转回，叫号如狗，围城绕行。
They come back in the evening; they make a noise like a dog, and go round the town.

他们口中喷吐恶言，嘴里有刀，他们说有谁听见。
See, hate is dropping from their lips; curses are on their tongues: they say, Who gives attention to it?

但你耶和华必笑话他们。你要嗤笑万邦。
But you are laughing at them, O Lord; you will make sport of all the nations.

我的力量阿，我必仰望你。因为神是我的高台。
O my strength, I will put my hope in you; because God is my strong tower.

我的神要以慈爱迎接我。神要叫我看见我仇敌遭报。
The God of my mercy will go before me: God will let me see my desire effected on my haters.

不要杀他们，恐怕我的民忘记。主阿，你是我们的盾牌。求你用你的能力使他们四散，且降为卑。
Put them not to death, for so my people will keep the memory of them: let them be sent in all directions by your power; make them low, O Lord our saviour.

因他们口中的罪，和嘴里的言语，并咒骂虚谎的话，愿他们在骄傲之中被缠住了。
Because of the sin of their mouths and the word of their lips, let them even be taken in their pride; and for their curses and their deceit,

求你发怒，使他们消灭，以至归于无有，叫他们知道神在雅各中间掌权，直到地极。（细拉）
Put an end to them in your wrath, put an end to them, so that they may not be seen again; let them see that God is ruling in Jacob and to the ends of the earth. (Selah.)

到了晚上，任凭他们转回。任凭他们叫号如狗，围城绕行。
And in the evening let them come back, and make a noise like a dog, and go round the town.

他们必走来走去，寻找食物。若不得饱，就终夜在外。
Let them go wandering up and down in search of food, and be there all night if they have not enough.

但我要歌颂你的力量，早晨要高唱你的慈爱。因为你作过我的高台。在我急难的日子，作过我的避难所。
But I will make songs of your power; yes, I will give cries of joy for your mercy in the morning; because you have been my strength and my high tower in the day of my trouble.

我的力量阿，我要歌颂你。因为神是我的高台，是赐恩与我的神。
To you, O my strength, will I make my song: because God is my high tower, even the God of my mercy.

（大卫与两河间的亚兰并琐巴的亚兰争战的时候，约押转回，在盐谷攻击以东，杀了一万二千人。那时大卫作这金诗，叫人学习，交与伶长。调用为证的百合花。）神阿，你丢弃了我们，使我们破败；你向我们发怒，求你使我们复兴。
<To the chief music-maker; put to Shushan-eduth. Michtam. Of David. For teaching. When he was fighting against Aram-naharaim and Aramzobah, when Joab came back, and put twelve thousand of the Edomites to death, in the Valley of Salt.> God, you have put us away from you, you have sent us in all directions, you have been angry; O be turned to us again.

你使地震动，而且崩裂。求你将裂口医好。因为地摇动。
By the power of your hand the earth is shaking and broken; make it strong again, for it is moved.

你叫你的民遇见艰难。你叫我们喝那使人东倒西歪的酒。
You have made the people see hard times; you have given us the wine of shaking for our drink.

你把旌旗赐给敬畏你的人，可以为真理扬起来。（细拉）
Give a safe place to those who have fear of you, where they may go in flight from before the bow. (Selah.)

求你应允我们，用右手拯救我们，好叫你所亲爱的人得救。
So that your loved ones may be made safe, let your right hand be my salvation, and give me an answer.

神已经指着他的圣洁说，（说或作应许我）我要欢乐。我要分开示剑，丈量疏割谷。
God has said in his holy place, I will be glad: I will make a division of Shechem, and the valley of Succoth will be measured out.

基列是我的。玛拿西也是我的。以法莲是护卫我头的。犹大是我的杖。
Gilead is mine, and Manasseh is mine; and Ephraim is the strength of my head; Judah is my law-giver;

摩押是我的沐浴盆。我要向以东抛鞋。非利士阿，你还能因我欢呼吗？
Moab is my washpot; over Edom will I put out my shoe; over Philistia will a glad cry be sounded.

谁能领我进坚固城。谁能引我到以东地。
Who will take me into the strong town? who will be my guide into Edom?

神阿，你不是丢弃了我们吗？神阿，你不和我们的军兵同去吗？
Have not you put us away, O God? and you have not gone out with our armies.

求你帮助我们攻击敌人，因为人的帮助是枉然的。
Give us help in our trouble; for there is no help in man.

我们倚靠神，才得施展大能，因为践踏我们敌人的就是他。
Through God we will do great things, for through him our haters will be crushed under our feet.

（大卫的诗，交与伶长。用丝弦的乐器。）神阿，求你听我的呼求，侧耳听我的祷告。
<To the chief music-maker. On a corded instrument. Of David.> Let my cry come to you, O God; let your ears be open to my prayer.

我心里发昏的时候，我要从地极求告你。求你领我到那比我更高的磐石。
From the end of the earth will I send up my cry to you, when my heart is overcome: take me to the rock which is over-high for me.

因为你作过我的避难所，作过我的坚固台，脱离仇敌。
For you have been my secret place, and my high tower from those who made war on me.

我要永远住在你的帐幕里。我要投靠在你翅膀下的隐密处。（细拉）
I will make your tent my resting-place for ever: I will keep myself under the cover of your wings. (Selah.)

神阿，你原是听了我所许的愿。你将产业赐给敬畏你名的人。
For you, O God, have made answer to my prayers; you have given me the heritage of those who give honour to your name.

你要加添王的寿数。他的年岁必存到世世。
You will give the king long life; and make his years go on through the generations.

他必永远坐在神面前。愿你预备慈爱和诚实保佑他。
May the seat of his authority be before God for ever; may mercy and righteousness keep him safe.

这样，我要歌颂你的名直到永远，好天天还我所许的愿。
So will I make songs in praise of your name for ever, giving to God that which is right day by day.

（大卫的诗，照耶杜顿的作法，交与伶长。）我的心默默无声，专等候神。我的救恩是从他而来。
<To the chief music-maker. After Jeduthun. A Psalm. Of David.> My soul, put all your faith in God; for from him comes my salvation.

惟独他是我的磐石，我的拯救。他是我的高台。我必不很动摇。
He only is my Rock and my salvation; he is my high tower; I will not be greatly moved.

你们大家攻击一人，把他毁坏。如同毁坏歪斜的墙，将倒的壁，要到几时呢？
How long will you go on designing evil against a man? running against him as against a broken wall, which is on the point of falling?

他们彼此商议，专要从他的尊位上把他推下。他们喜爱谎话。口虽祝福，心却咒诅。（细拉）
Their only thought is to put him down from his place of honour; their delight is in deceit: blessing is in their mouths but cursing in their hearts. (Selah.)

我的心哪，你当默默无声，专等候神。因为我的盼望是从他而来。
My soul, put all your faith in God; for from him comes my hope.

惟独他是我的磐石，我的拯救。他是我的高台。我必不动摇。
He only is my Rock and my salvation; he is my high tower; I will not be greatly moved.

我的拯救，我的荣耀，都在乎神。我力量的磐石，我的避难所，都在乎神。
In God is my salvation, and my glory; the Rock of my strength, and my safe place.

你们众民当时时倚靠他，在他面前倾心吐意。神是我们的避难所。（细拉）
Have faith in him at all times, you people; let your hearts go flowing out before him: God is our safe place. (Selah.)

下流人真是虚空，上流人也是虚假。放在天平里就必浮起。他们一共比空气还轻。
Truly men of low birth are nothing, and men of high position are not what they seem; if they are put in the scales together they are less than a breath.

不要仗势欺人，也不要因抢夺而骄傲。若财宝加增，不要放在心上。
Have no faith in the rewards of evil-doing, or in profits wrongly made: if your wealth is increased, do not put your hopes on it.

神说了一次，两次，我都听见，就是能力都属乎神。
Once has God said, twice has it come to my ears, that power is God's:

主阿，慈爱也是属乎你。因为你照着各人所行的报应他。
And mercy, O Lord, is yours, for you give to every man the reward of his work.

（大卫在犹大旷野的时候，作了这诗。）神阿，你是我的神，我要切切地寻求你。在干旱疲乏无水之地，我渴想你，我的心切慕你。
<A Psalm. Of David. When he was in the waste land of Judah.> O God, you are my God; early will I make my search for you: my soul is dry for need of you, my flesh is wasted with desire for you, as a dry and burning land where no water is;

我在圣所中曾如此瞻仰你，为要见你的能力，和你的荣耀。
To see your power and your glory, as I have seen you in the holy place.

因你的慈爱比生命更好，我的嘴唇要颂赞你。
Because your mercy is better than life, my lips will give you praise.

我还活的时候，要这样称颂你。我要奉你的名举手。
So will I go on blessing you all my life, lifting up my hands in your name.

我在床上记念你，在夜更的时候思想你，我的心就像饱足了骨髓肥油。我也要以欢乐的嘴唇赞美你。
My soul will be comforted, as with good food; and my mouth will give you praise with songs of joy;


When the memory of you comes to me on my bed, and when I give thought to you in the night-time.

因为你曾帮助我，我就在你翅膀的荫下欢呼。
Because you have been my help, I will have joy in the shade of your wings.

我心紧紧的跟随你。你的右手扶持我。
My soul keeps ever near you: your right hand is my support.

但那些寻索要灭我命的人，必往地底下去。
But those whose desire is my soul's destruction will go down to the lower parts of the earth.

他们必被刀剑所杀，被野狗所吃。
They will be cut off by the sword; they will be food for foxes.

但是王必因神欢喜。凡指着他发誓的，必要夸口。因为说谎之人的口，必被塞住。
But the king will have joy in God; everyone who takes an oath by him will have cause for pride; but the false mouth will be stopped.

（大卫的诗，交与伶长。）神阿，我哀叹的时候，求你听我的声音。求你保护我的性命，不受仇敌的惊恐。
<To the chief music-maker. A Psalm. Of David.> O God, let the voice of my grief come to your ear: keep my life from the fear of those who are against me.

求你把我隐藏，使我脱离作恶之人的暗谋，和作孽之人的扰乱。
Keep me safe from the secret purpose of wrongdoers; from the band of the workers of evil;

他们磨舌如刀，发出苦毒的言语，好像比准了的箭。
Who make their tongues sharp like a sword, and whose arrows are pointed, even bitter words;

要在暗地射完全人。他们忽然射他，并不惧怕。
So that in secret they may let loose their arrows at the upright, suddenly and unseen.

他们彼此勉励设下恶计。他们商量暗设网罗，说，谁能看见。
They make themselves strong in an evil purpose; they make holes for secret nets; they say, Who will see it,

他们图谋奸恶，说，我们是极力图谋的。他们各人的意念心思是深的。
Or make discovery of our secret purpose? The design is framed with care; and the inner thought of a man, and his heart, is deep.

但神要射他们。他们忽然被箭射伤。
But God sends out an arrow against them; suddenly they are wounded.

他们必然绊跌，被自己的舌头所害。凡看见他们的，必都摇头。
The evil of their tongues is the cause of their fall; all those who see them are shaking their heads at them.

众人都要害怕，要传扬神的工作，并且明白他的作为。
And in fear men make public the works of God; and giving thought to his acts they get wisdom.

义人必因耶和华欢喜，并要投靠他。凡心里正直的人，都要夸口。
The upright will be glad in the Lord and have hope in him; and all the lovers of righteousness will give him glory.

（大卫的诗歌，交与伶长。）神阿，锡安的人都等候赞美你，所许的愿，也要向你偿还。
<To the chief music-maker. A Psalm. Of David. A Song.> It is right for you, O God, to have praise in Zion: to you let the offering be made.

听祷告的主阿，凡有血气的，都要来就你。
To you, O hearer of prayer, let the words of all flesh come.

罪孽胜了我。至于我们的过犯，你都要赦免。
Evils have overcome us: but as for our sins, you will take them away.

你所拣选，使他亲近你，住在你院中的，这人便为有福。我们必因你居所，你圣殿的美福知足了。
Happy is the man of your selection, to whom you give a resting-place in your house; we will be full of the good things out of your holy place.

拯救我们的神阿，你必以威严秉公义应允我们。你本是一切地极，和海上远处的人所倚靠的。
You will give us an answer in righteousness by great acts of power, O God of our salvation; you who are the hope of all the ends of the earth, and of the far-off lands of the sea;

他既以大能束腰，就用力量安定诸山。
The God by whose strength the mountains are fixed; who is robed with power:

使诸海的响声，和其中波浪的响声，并万民的喧哗，都平静了。
Who makes the loud voice of the sea quiet, and puts an end to the sound of its waves.

住在地极的人，因你的神迹惧怕。你使日出日落之地都欢呼。
Those in the farthest parts of the earth have fear when they see your signs: the outgoings of the morning and evening are glad because of you.

你眷顾地，降下透雨，使地大得肥美。神的河满了水。你这样浇灌了地，好为人预备五谷。
You have given your blessing to the earth, watering it and making it fertile; the river of God is full of water: and having made it ready, you give men grain.

你浇透地的犁沟，润平犁脊。降甘霖，使地软和。其中发长的，蒙你赐福。
You make the ploughed lands full of water; you make smooth the slopes: you make the earth soft with showers, sending your blessing on its growth.

你以恩典为年岁的冠冕。你的路径都滴下脂油。
The year is crowned with the good you give; life-giving rain is dropping from your footsteps,

滴在旷野的草场上。小山以欢乐束腰。
Falling on the grass of the waste land: and the little hills are glad on every side.

草场以羊群为衣。谷中也长满了五谷。这一切都欢呼歌唱。
The grass-land is thick with flocks; the valleys are full of grain; they give glad cries and songs of joy.

（一篇诗歌，交与伶长。）全地都当向神欢呼。
<To the chief music-maker. A Song. A Psalm.> Send up a glad cry to God, all the earth:

歌颂他名的荣耀。用赞美的言语，将他的荣耀发明。
Make a song in honour of his name: give praise and glory to him.

当对神说，你的作为何等可畏。因你的大能仇敌要投降你。
Say to God, How greatly to be feared are your works! because of your great power your haters are forced to put themselves under your feet.

全地要敬拜你，歌颂你，要歌颂你的名。（细拉）
Let all the earth give you worship, and make songs to you; let them make songs to your name. (Selah.)

你们来看神所行的。他向世人所作之事，是可畏的。
Come and see the works of God: he is to be feared in all he does to the children of men.

他将海变成干地。众民步行过河。我们在那里因他欢喜。
The sea was turned into dry land: they went through the river on foot: there did we have joy in him.

他用权能治理万民，直到永远。他的眼睛鉴察列邦。悖逆的人不可自高。（细拉）
He is ruling in power for ever; his eyes are watching the nations: may his haters have no strength against him. (Selah.)

万民哪，你们当称颂我们的神。使人得听赞美他的声音。
Give blessings to our God, O you peoples, let the voice of his praise be loud;

他使我们的性命存活，也不叫我们的脚摇动。
Because he gives us life, and has not let our feet be moved.

神阿，你曾试验我们，熬炼我们，如熬炼银子一样。
For you, O God, have put us to the test: testing us by fire like silver.

你使我们进入网罗，把重担放在我们的身上。
You let us be put in prison; chains were put on our legs.

你使人坐车轧我们的头。我们经过水火。你却使我们到丰富之地。
You let men go driving over our heads; we went through fire and through water; but you took us out into a wide place.

我要用燔祭进你的殿，向你还我的愿。
I will come into your house with burned offerings, I will make payment of my debt to you,

就是在急难时我嘴唇所发的，口中所许的。
Keeping the word which came from my lips, and which my mouth said, when I was in trouble.

我要把肥牛作燔祭，将公羊的香祭献给你。又把公牛和山羊献上。（细拉）
I will give you burned offerings of fat beasts, and the smoke of sheep; I will make offerings of oxen and goats. (Selah.)

凡敬畏神的人，你们都来听。我要述说他为我所行的事。
Come, give ear to me, all you God-fearing men, so that I may make clear to you what he has done for my soul.

我曾用口求告他，我的舌头，也称他为高。
My voice went up to him, and I was lifted up from the underworld.

我若心里注重罪孽，主必不听。
I said in my heart, The Lord will not give ear to me:

但神实在听见了。他侧耳听了我祷告的声音。
But truly God's ear has been open; he has give attention to the voice of my prayer.

神是应当称颂的。他并没有推却我的祷告，也没有叫他的慈爱离开我。
Praise be to God who has not taken away his good faith and his mercy from me.

（一篇诗歌，交与伶长。用丝弦的乐器。）愿神怜悯我们，赐福与我们，用脸光照我们。（细拉）
<To the chief music-maker. With corded instruments. A Psalm. A Song.> May God give us mercy and blessing, and let the light of his face be shining on us; (Selah.)

好叫世界得知你的道路，万国得知你的救恩。
So that men may see your way on the earth, and your salvation among all nations.

神阿，愿列邦称赞你，愿万民都称赞你。
Let the peoples give you praise, O God; let all the peoples give you praise.

愿万国都快乐欢呼。因为你必按公正审判万民，引导世上的万国。（细拉）
O let the nations be glad, and make song of joy; for you will be the judge of the peoples in righteousness, guiding the nations of the earth. (Selah.)

神阿，愿列邦称赞你。愿万民都称赞你。
Let the peoples give you praise, O God; let all the peoples give you praise.

地已经出了土产。神，就是我们的神，要赐福与我们。
The earth has given her increase; and God, even our God, will give us his blessing.

神要赐福与我们。地的四极都要敬畏他。
God will give us his blessing; so let all the ends of the earth be in fear of him.

（大卫的诗歌，交与伶长。）愿神兴起，使他的仇敌四散，叫那恨他的人，从他面前逃跑。
<To the chief music-maker. Of David. A Psalm. A Song.> Let God be seen, and let his haters be put to flight; let those who are against him be turned back before him.

他们被驱逐，如烟被风吹散。恶人见神之面而消灭，如蜡被火熔化。
Let them be like smoke before the driving wind; as wax turning soft before the fire, so let them come to an end before the power of God.

惟有义人必然欢喜，在神面前高兴快乐。
But let the upright be glad; let them have delight before God; let them be full of joy.

你们当向神唱诗，歌颂他的名。为那坐车行过旷野的，修平大路。他的名是耶和华。要在他面前欢乐。
Make songs to God, make songs of praise to his name; make a way for him who comes through the waste lands; his name is Jah; be glad before him.

神在他的圣所作孤儿的父，作寡妇的伸冤者。
A father to those who have no father, a judge of the widows, is God in his holy place.

神叫孤独的有家，使被囚的出来享福。惟有悖逆的住在干燥之地。
Those who are without friends, God puts in families; he makes free those who are in chains; but those who are turned away from him are given a dry land.

神阿，你曾在你百姓前头出来，在旷野行走。（细拉）
O God, when you went out before your people, wandering through the waste land; (Selah.)

那时地见神的面而震动，天也落雨。西乃山见以色列神的面也震动。
The earth was shaking and the heavens were streaming, because God was present; even Sinai itself was moved before God, the God of Israel.

神阿，你降下大雨。你产业以色列疲乏的时候，你使他坚固。
You, O God, did freely send the rain, giving strength to the weariness of your heritage.

你的会众住在其中。神阿，你的恩惠是为困苦人预备的。
Those whose resting-place was there, even the poor, were comforted by your good things, O God.

主发命令，传好信息的妇女成了大群。
The Lord gives the word; great is the number of the women who make it public.

统兵的君王逃跑了，逃跑了。在家等候的妇女，分受所夺的。
Kings of armies quickly go in flight: and the women in the houses make a division of their goods.

你们安卧在羊圈的时候，好像鸽子的翅膀镀白银，翎毛镀黄金一般。
Will you take your rest among the flocks? like the wings of a dove covered with silver, and its feathers with yellow gold.

全能者在境内赶散列王的时候，势如飘雪在撒们。
When the Most High put the kings to flight, it was as white as snow in Salmon.

巴珊山是神的山。巴珊山是多峰多岭的山。
A hill of God is the hill of Bashan; a hill with high tops is the hill of Bashan.

你们多峰多岭的山哪，为何斜看神所愿居住的山。耶和华必住这山。直到永远。
Why are you looking with envy, you high hills, on the hill desired by God as his resting-place? truly, God will make it his house for ever.

神的车辇累万盈千。主在其中，好像在西乃圣山一样。
The war-carriage of God is among Israel's thousands; the Lord has come from Sinai to the holy place.

你已经升上高天，掳掠仇敌，你在人间，就是在悖逆的人间，受了供献，叫耶和华神可以与他们同住。
You have gone up on high, taking your prisoners with you; you have taken offerings from men; the Lord God has taken his place on the seat of his power.

天天背负我们重担的主，就是拯救我们的神。是应当称颂的。（细拉）
Praise be to the Lord, who is our support day by day, even the God of our salvation. (Selah.)

神是为我们施行诸般救恩的神。人能脱离死亡，是在乎主耶和华。
Our God is for us a God of salvation; his are the ways out of death.

但神要打破他仇敌的头，就是那常犯罪之人的发顶。
The heads of the haters of God will be crushed; even the head of him who still goes on in his evil ways.

主说，我要使众民从巴珊而归，使他们从深海而回。
The Lord said, I will make them come back from Bashan, and from the deep parts of the sea;

使你打碎仇敌，你的脚踹在血中，使你狗的舌头，从其中得分。
So that your foot may be red with blood, and the tongues of your dogs with the same.

神阿，你是我的神，我的王。人已经看见你行走，进入圣所。
We see your going, O God: even the going of my God, my King, into the holy place.

歌唱的行在前，作乐的随在后，都在击鼓的童女中间。
The makers of songs go before, the players of music come after, among the young girls playing on brass instruments.

从以色列源头而来的，当在各会中称颂主神。
Give praise to God in the great meeting; even the Lord, you who come from the fountain of Israel.

在那里有统管他们的小便雅悯，有犹大的首领，和他们的群众。有西布伦的首领。有拿弗他利的首领。
There is little Benjamin ruling them, the chiefs of Judah and their army, the rulers of Zebulun and the rulers of Naphtali.

以色列的能力，是神所赐的。神阿，求你坚固你为我们所成全的事。
O God, send out your strength; the strength, O God, with which you have done great things for us,

因你耶路撒冷的殿，列王必带贡物献给你。
Out of your Temple in Jerusalem.

求你叱喝芦苇中的野兽，和群公牛，并列邦中的牛犊，把银块踹在脚下。神已经赶散好争战的列邦。
Say sharp words to the beast among the water-plants, the band of strong ones, with the lords of the peoples, put an end to the people whose delight is in war.

埃及的公侯要出来朝见神。古实人要急忙举手祷告。
Kings will give you offerings, they will come out of Egypt; from Pathros will come offerings of silver; Ethiopia will be stretching out her hands to God.

世上的列国阿，你们要向神歌唱。愿你们歌颂主，
Make songs to God, you kingdoms of the earth; O make songs of praise to the Lord; (Selah.)

歌颂那自古驾行在诸天以上的主。他发出声音，是极大的声音。
To him who goes or the clouds of heaven, the heaven which was from earliest times; he sends out his voice of power.

你们要将能力归给神。他的威荣在以色列之上，他的能力是在穹苍。
Make clear that strength is God's: he is lifted up over Israel, and his power is in the clouds.

神阿，你从圣所显为可畏。以色列的神，是那将力量权能赐给他百姓的。神是应当称颂的。
O God, you are to be feared in your holy place: the God of Israel gives strength and power to his people. Praise be to God.

（大卫的诗，交与伶长，调用百合花。）神阿，求你救我。因为众水要淹没我。
<To the chief music-maker; put to Shoshannim. Of David.> Be my saviour, O God; because the waters have come in, even to my neck.

我陷在深淤泥中，没有立脚之地。我到了深水中。大水漫过我身。
My feet are deep in the soft earth, where there is no support; I have come into deep waters, the waves are flowing over me.

我因呼求困乏，喉咙发干。我因等候神，眼睛失明。
I am tired with my crying; my throat is burning: my eyes are wasted with waiting for my God.

无故恨我的，比我头发还多。无理与我为仇，要把我剪除的甚为强盛。我没有抢夺的，要叫我偿还。
Those who have hate for me without cause are greater in number than the hairs of my head; those who are against me, falsely desiring my destruction, are very strong; I gave back what I had not taken away.

神阿，我的愚昧你原知道。我的罪愆不能隐瞒。
O God, you see how foolish I am; and my wrongdoing is clear to you.

万军的主耶和华阿，求你叫那等候你的，不要因我蒙羞。以色列的神阿，求你叫那寻求你的，不要因我受辱。
Let not those who have hope in you be put to shame because of me, O Lord God of armies: let not those who are waiting for you be made low because of me, O God of Israel.

因我为你的缘故受了辱骂，满面羞愧。
I have been wounded with sharp words because of you; my face has been covered with shame.

我的弟兄看我为外路人。我的同胞看我为外邦人。
I have become strange to my brothers, and like a man from a far country to my mother's children.

因我为你的殿心里焦急，如同火烧。并且辱骂你人的辱骂，都落在我身上。
I am on fire with passion for your house; and the hard things which are said about you have come on me.

我哭泣，以禁食刻苦我心，这倒算为我的羞辱。
My bitter weeping, and my going without food, were turned to my shame.

我拿麻布当衣裳。就成了他们的笑谈。
When I put on the clothing of grief, they said evil of me.

坐在城门口的谈论我。酒徒也以我为歌曲。
I am a cause of wonder to those in authority; a song to those who are given to strong drink.

但我在悦纳的时候，向你耶和华祈祷。神阿，求你按你丰盛的慈爱，凭你拯救的诚实，应允我。
But as for me, let my prayer be made to you, O Lord, at a time when you are pleased; O God, give me an answer in your great mercy, for your salvation is certain.

求你搭救我出离淤泥，不叫我陷在其中。求你使我脱离那些恨我的人，使我出离深水。
Take me from the grip of the sticky earth, so that I may not go down into it; let me be lifted up from the deep waters.

求你不容大水漫过我，不容深渊吞灭我，不容坑坎在我以上合口。
Let me not be covered by the flowing waters; let not the deep waters go over my head, and let me not be shut up in the underworld.

耶和华阿，求你应允我，因为你的慈爱本为美好。求你按你丰盛的慈悲，回转眷顾我。
Give an answer to my words, O Lord; for your mercy is good: be turned to me, because of your great pity.

不要掩面不顾你的仆人。我是在急难之中。求你速速地应允我。
Let not your face be covered from your servant, for I am in trouble; quickly give me an answer.

求你亲近我，救赎我。求你因我的仇敌把我赎回。
Come near to my soul, for its salvation: be my saviour, because of those who are against me.

你知道我受的辱骂，欺凌，羞辱。我的敌人都在你面前。
You have seen my shame, how I was laughed at and made low; my haters are all before you.

辱骂伤破了我的心。我又满了忧愁。我指望有人体恤，却没有一个。我指望有人安慰，却找不着一个。
My heart is broken by bitter words, I am full of grief; I made a search for some to have pity on me, but there was no one; I had no comforter.

他们拿苦胆给我当食物。我渴了，他们拿醋给我喝。
They gave me poison for my food; and bitter wine for my drink.

愿他们的筵席，在他们面前变为网罗，在他们平安的时候，变为机槛。
Let their table before them be for their destruction; let their feasts become a net to take them.

愿他们的眼睛昏蒙，不得看见。愿你使他们的腰常常战抖。
Let their eyes be blind so that they may not see; let their bodies for ever be shaking.

求你将你的恼恨，倒在他们身上，叫你的烈怒追上他们。
Let your curse come on them; let the heat of your wrath overtake them.

愿他们的住处，变为荒场。愿他们的帐棚，无人居住。
Give their houses to destruction, and let there be no one in their tents.

因为你所击打的，他们就逼迫。你所击伤的他们戏说他的愁苦。
Because they are cruel to him against whom your hand is turned; they make bitter the grief of him who is wounded by you.

愿你在他们的罪上加罪，不容他们在你面前称义。
Let their punishment be increased; let them not come into your righteousness.

愿他们从生命册上被涂抹，不得记录在义人之中。
Let their names be taken from the book of the living, let them not be numbered with the upright.

但我是困苦忧伤的。神阿，愿你的救恩，将我安置在高处。
But I am poor and full of sorrow; let me be lifted up by your salvation, O Lord.

我要以诗歌赞美神的名，以感谢称他为大。
I will give praise to the name of God with a song; I will give glory to him for what he has done.

这便叫耶和华喜悦，胜似献牛，或是献有角有蹄的公牛。
This will be more pleasing to the Lord than an ox, or a young ox of full growth.

谦卑的人看见了，就喜乐。寻求神的人，愿你们的心苏醒。
The poor will see it and be glad: you who are lovers of God, let your hearts have life.

因为耶和华听了穷乏人，不藐视被囚的人。
For the ears of the Lord are open to the poor, and he takes thought for his prisoners.

愿天和地，洋海，和其中一切的动物，都赞美他。
Let the heavens and the earth give praise to him, the seas, and everything moving in them.

因为神要拯救锡安，建造犹大的城邑。他的民要在那里居住，得以为业。
For God will be the saviour of Zion, and the builder of the towns of Judah; so that it may be their resting-place and heritage.

他仆人的后裔，要承受为业。爱他名的人，也要住在其中。
The seed of his servants will have their part in it, and there the lovers of his name will have rest.

（大卫的记念诗，交与伶长。）神阿，求你快快搭救我。耶和华阿，求你速速帮助我。
<To the chief music-maker. Of David. To keep in memory.> Let your salvation come quickly, O God; come quickly to my help, O Lord.

愿那些寻索我命的，抱愧蒙羞。愿那些喜悦我遭害的，退后受辱。
Let those who go after my soul have shame and trouble; let those who have evil designs against me be turned back and made foolish.

愿那些对我说，阿哈，阿哈的，因羞愧退后。
Let those who say Aha, aha! be turned back as a reward of their shame.

愿一切寻求你的，因你高兴欢喜。愿那些喜爱你救恩的常说，当尊神为大。
Let all those who are looking for you be glad and have joy in you; let the lovers of your salvation ever say, May God be great.

但我是困苦穷乏的。神阿，求你速速到我这里来。你是帮助我的，搭救我的。耶和华阿，求你不要耽延。
But I am poor and in need; come to me quickly, O God; you are my help and my saviour; let there be no waiting, O Lord.

耶和华阿，我投靠你。求你叫我永不羞愧。
In you, O Lord, have I put my hope; let me never be shamed.

求你凭你的公义搭救我，救拔我，侧耳听我，拯救我。
Keep me safe in your righteousness, and come to my help; give ear to my voice, and be my saviour.

求你作我常住的磐石。你已经命定要救我。因为你是我的岩石，我的山寨。
Be my strong Rock, the strong place of my salvation; for you are my Rock, and my safe place.

我的神阿，求你救我脱离恶人的手，脱离不义和残暴之人的手。
O my God, take me out of the hand of the sinner, out of the hand of the evil and cruel man.

主耶和华阿，你是我所盼望的。从我年幼你是我所倚靠的。
For you are my hope, O Lord God; I have had faith in you from the time when I was young.

我从出母胎被你扶持。使我出母腹的是你。我必常常赞美你。
You have been my support from the day of my birth; you took me out of my mother's body; my praise will be ever of you.

许多人以我为怪。但你是我坚固的避难所。
I am a wonder to all; but you are my strong tower.

你的赞美，你的荣耀，终日必满了我的口。
My mouth will be full of your praise and glory all the day.

我年老的时候，求你不要丢弃我。我力气衰弱的时候，求你不要离弃我。
Do not give me up when I am old; be my help even when my strength is gone.

我的仇敌议论我。那些窥探要害我命的彼此商议，
For my haters are waiting secretly for me; and those who are watching for my soul are banded together in their evil designs,

说，神已经离弃他。我们追赶他，捉拿他吧。因为没有人搭救。
Saying, God has given him up; go after him and take him, for he has no helper.

神阿，求你不要远离我。我的神阿，求你速速帮助我。
O God, be not far from me; O my God, come quickly to my help.

愿那与我性命为敌的，羞愧被灭。愿那谋害我的，受辱蒙羞。
Let those who say evil against my soul be overcome and put to shame; let my haters be made low and have no honour.

我却要常常盼望，并要越发赞美你。
But I will go on ever hoping, and increasing in all your praise.

我的口终日要述说你的公义，和你的救恩。因我不计其数。
My mouth will make clear your righteousness and your salvation all the day; for they are more than may be measured.

我要来说主耶和华大能的事。我单要提说你的公义。
I will give news of the great acts of the Lord God; my words will be of your righteousness, and of yours only.

神阿，自我年幼时，你就教训我。直到如今，我传扬你奇妙的作为。
O God, you have been my teacher from the time when I was young; and I have been talking of your works of wonder even till now.

神阿，我到年老发白的时候，求你不要离弃我，等我将你的能力指示下代，将你的大能指示后世的人。
Now when I am old and grey-headed, O God, give me not up; till I have made clear your strength to this generation, and your power to all those to come.

神阿，你的公义甚高。行过大事的神阿，谁能象你。
Your righteousness, O God, is very high; you have done great things; O God, who is like you?

你是叫我们多经历重大急难的，必使我们复活。从地的深处救上来。
You, who have sent great and bitter troubles on me, will give me life again, lifting me up from the deep waters of the underworld.

求你使我越发昌大，又转来安慰我。
You will make me greater than before, and give me comfort on every side.

我的神阿，我要鼓瑟称赞你，称赞你的诚实。以色列的圣者阿，我要弹琴歌颂你。
I will give praise to you with instruments of music, O my God, for you are true; I will make songs to you with music, O Holy One of Israel.

我歌颂你的时候，我的嘴唇，和你所赎我的灵魂，都必欢呼。
Joy will be on my lips when I make melody to you; and in my soul, to which you have given salvation.

并且我的舌头，必终日讲论你的公义，因为那些谋害我的人，已经蒙羞受辱了。
My tongue will be talking of your righteousness all the day; for those whose purpose is to do me evil have been crushed and put to shame.

（所罗门的诗。）神阿，求你将判断的权柄赐给王，将公义赐给王的儿子。
<Of Solomon.> Give the king your authority, O God, and your righteousness to the king's son.

他要按公义审判你的民，按公平审判你的困苦人。
May he be a judge of your people in righteousness, and make true decisions for the poor.

大山小山，都要因公义使民得享平安。
May the mountains give peace to the people, and the hills righteousness.

他必为民中的困苦人伸冤，拯救穷乏之辈，压碎那欺压人的。
May he be a judge of the poor among the people, may he give salvation to the children of those who are in need; by him let the violent be crushed.

太阳还存，月亮还在，人要敬畏你，直到万代。
May his life go on as long as the sun and moon, through all generations.

他必降临，像雨降在已割的草地上，如甘霖滋润田地。
May he come down like rain on the cut grass; like showers watering the earth.

在他的日子义人要发旺，大有平安，好像月亮长存。
In his days may the upright do well, living in peace as long as there is a moon in heaven.

他要执掌权柄，从这海直到那海，从大河直到地极。
Let his kingdom be from sea to sea, from the River to the ends of the earth.

住在旷野的，必在他面前下拜。他的仇敌，必要舔土。
Let those who are against him go down before him; and let his haters be low in the dust.

他施和海岛的王要进贡。示巴和西巴的王要献礼物。
Let the kings of Tarshish and of the islands come back with offerings; let the kings of Sheba and Seba give of their stores.

诸王都要叩拜他，万国都要事奉他。
Yes, let all kings go down before him; let all nations be his servants.

因为穷乏人呼求的时候，他要搭救，没有人帮助的困苦人，他也要搭救。
For he will be a saviour to the poor in answer to his cry; and to him who is in need, without a helper.

他要怜恤贫寒和穷乏的人，拯救穷苦人的性命。
He will have pity on the poor, and be the saviour of those who are in need.

他要救赎他们脱离欺压和强暴。他们的血在他眼中看为宝贵。
He will keep their souls free from evil designs and violent attacks; and their blood will be of value in his eyes.

他们要存活。示巴的金子要奉给他。人要常常为他祷告，终日称颂他。
May he have long life, and may gold from Sheba be given to him: may prayers be made for him at all times; may blessings be on him every day.

在地的山顶上，五谷必然茂盛。（五谷必然茂盛或作有一把五谷）所结的谷实，要响动如利巴嫩的树林。城里的人，要发旺如地上的草。
May there be wide-stretching fields of grain in the land, shaking on the top of the mountains, full of fruit like Lebanon: may its stems be unnumbered like the grass of the earth.

他的名要存到永远，要留传如日之久。人要因他蒙福。万国要称他有福。
May his name go on for ever, as long as the sun: may men be blessing themselves by him; may all nations be blessing his name.

独行奇事的耶和华以色列的神，是应当称颂的。
Praise be to the Lord God, the God of Israel, the only doer of wonders.

他荣耀的名，也当称颂，直到永远。愿他的荣耀，充满全地。阿们，阿们。
Praise to the glory of his noble name for ever; let all the earth be full of his glory. So be it, So be it.

耶西的儿子大卫的祈祷完毕。
The prayers of David, the son of Jesse, are ended. <A Psalm. Of Asaph.>

（亚萨的诗。）神实在恩待以色列那些清心的人。
Truly, God is good to Israel, even to such as are clean in heart.

至于我，我的脚几乎失闪。我的脚险些滑跌。
But as for me, my feet had almost gone from under me; I was near to slipping;

我见恶人和狂傲人享平安，就心怀不平。
Because of my envy of the men of pride, when I saw the well-being of the wrongdoers.

他们死的时候，没有疼痛。他们的力气，却也壮实。
For they have no pain; their bodies are fat and strong.

他们不像别人受苦，也不像别人遭灾。
They are not in trouble as others are; they have no part in the unhappy fate of men.

所以骄傲如链子戴在他们的项上。强暴像衣裳遮住他们的身体。
For this reason pride is round them like a chain; they are clothed with violent behaviour as with a robe.

他们的眼睛，因体胖而凸出。他们所得的，过于心里所想的。
Their eyes are bursting with fat; they have more than their heart's desire.

他们讥笑人，凭恶意说欺压人的话。他们说话自高。
Their thoughts are deep with evil designs; their talk from their seats of power is of cruel acts.

他们的口亵渎上天，他们的舌毁谤全地。
Their mouth goes up to heaven; their tongues go walking through the earth.

所以神的民归到这里，喝尽了满杯的苦水。
For this reason they are full of bread; and water is ever flowing for them.

他们说，神怎能晓得？至高者岂有知识呢？
And they say, How will the Lord see this? is there knowledge in the Most High?

看哪，这就是恶人。他们既是常享安逸，财宝便加增。
Truly, such are the sinners; they do well at all times, and their wealth is increased.

我实在徒然洁净了我的心，徒然洗手表明无辜。
As for me, I have made my heart clean to no purpose, washing my hands in righteousness;

因为我终日遭灾难，每早晨受惩治。
For I have been troubled all the day; every morning have I undergone punishment.

我若说，我要这样讲，这就是以奸诈待你的众子。
If I would make clear what it is like, I would say, You are false to the generation of your children.

我思索怎能明白这事，眼看实系为难。
When my thoughts were turned to see the reason of this, it was a weariness in my eyes;

等我进了神的圣所，思想他们的结局。
Till I went into God's holy place, and saw the end of the evil-doers.

你实在把他们安在滑地，使他们掉在沉沦之中。
You put their feet where there was danger of slipping, so that they go down into destruction.

他们转眼之间，成了何等的荒凉。他们被惊恐灭尽了。
How suddenly are they wasted! fears are the cause of their destruction.

人睡醒了怎样看梦，主阿，你醒了，也必照样轻看他们的影像。
As a dream when one is awake, they are ended; they are like an image gone out of mind when sleep is over.

因而我心里发酸，肺腑被刺。
My heart was made bitter, and I was pained by the bite of grief:

我这样愚昧无知，在你面前如畜类一般。
As for me, I was foolish, and without knowledge; I was like a beast before you.

然而我常与你同在。你搀着我的右手。
But still I am ever with you; you have taken me by my right hand.

你要以你的训言引导我，以后必接我到荣耀里。
Your wisdom will be my guide, and later you will put me in a place of honour.

除你以外，在天上我有谁呢？除你以外，在地上我也没有所爱慕的。
Whom have I in heaven but you? and having you I have no desire for anything on earth.

我的肉体，和我的心肠衰残。但神是我心里的力量，又是我的福分，直到永远。
My flesh and my heart are wasting away: but God is the Rock of my heart and my eternal heritage.

远离你的，必要死亡。凡离弃你行邪淫的，你都灭绝了。
For those who are far away from you will come to destruction: you will put an end to all those who have not kept faith with you.

但我亲近神是与我有益。我以主耶和华为我的避难所，好叫我述说你一切的作为。
But it is good for me to come near to God: I have put my faith in the Lord God, so that I may make clear all his works.

（亚萨的训诲诗。）神阿，你为何永远丢弃我们呢？你为何向你草场的羊发怒如烟冒出呢？
<Maschil. Of Asaph.> Of God, why have you put us away from you for ever? why is the fire of your wrath smoking against the sheep who are your care?

求你记念你古时所得来的会众，就是你所赎作你产业支派的。并记念你向来所居住的锡安山。
Keep in mind your band of worshippers, for whom you gave payment in the days which are past, whom you took for yourself as the people of your heritage; even this mountain of Zion, which has been your resting-place.

求你举步去看那日久荒凉之地，仇敌在圣所中所行的一切恶事。
Go up and see the unending destruction; all the evil which your haters have done in the holy place;

你的敌人在你会中吼叫。他们竖了自己的旗为记号。
Sending out their voices like lions among your worshippers; they have put up their signs to be seen.

他们好像人扬起斧子，砍伐林中的树。
They are cutting down, like a man whose blade is lifted up against the thick trees.

圣所中一切雕刻的，他们现在用斧子锤子打坏了。
Your doors are broken down with hammers and iron blades.

他们用火焚烧你的圣所，亵渎你名的居所，拆毁到地。
They have put on fire your holy place; they have made the place of your name unclean, pulling it down to the earth.

他们心里说，我们要尽行毁灭，他们就在遍地把神的会所都烧毁了。
They have said in their hearts, Let us put an end to them all together; they have given over to the fire all God's places of worship in the land.

我们不见我们的标帜。不再有先知。我们内中也没有人知道这灾祸要到几时呢？
We do not see our signs: there is no longer any prophet, or anyone among us to say how long.

神阿，敌人辱骂要到几时呢？仇敌亵渎你的名，要到永远吗？
O God, how long will those who are against us say cruel things? will the hater go on looking down on your name for ever?

你为什么缩回你的右手。求你从怀中伸出来，毁灭他们。
Why are you keeping back your hand, and covering your right hand in your robe?

神自古以来为我的王，在地上施行拯救。
For from the past God is my King, working salvation in the earth.

你曾用能力将海分开，将水中大鱼的头打破。
The sea was parted in two by your strength; the heads of the great sea-beasts were broken.

你曾砸碎鳄鱼的头，把他给旷野的禽兽为食物。（禽兽原文作民）
The heads of the great snake were crushed by you; you gave them as food to the fishes of the sea.

你曾分裂磐石，水便成了溪河，你使长流的江河干了。
You made valleys for fountains and springs; you made the ever-flowing rivers dry.

白昼属你，黑夜也属你。亮光和日头，是你所预备的。
The day is yours and the night is yours: you made the light and the sun.

地的一切疆界，是你所立的。夏天和冬天是你所定的。
By you all the limits of the earth were fixed; you have made summer and winter.

耶和华阿，仇敌辱骂，愚顽民亵渎了你的名，求你记念这事。
Keep this in mind, O Lord, that your haters have said cruel things, and that your name has been looked down on by a people of evil behaviour.

不要将你斑鸠的性命交给野兽。不要永远忘记你困苦人的性命。
O give not the soul of your dove to the hawk; let not the life of the poor go out of your memory for ever.

求你顾念所立的约。因为地上黑暗之处，都满了强暴的居所。
Keep in mind your undertaking; for the dark places of the earth are full of pride and cruel acts.

不要叫受欺压的人蒙羞回去。要叫困苦穷乏的人赞美你的名。
O let not the crushed be turned back in shame; let the low man and the poor give praise to your name.

神阿，求你起来，为自己伸诉。要记念愚顽人怎样终日辱骂你。
Up! O God, be the judge of your cause; keep in mind the bitter things which the man of evil behaviour says against you every day.

不要忘记你敌人的声音。那起来敌你之人的喧哗时常上升。
Keep in mind the voice of your haters; the outcry of those who come against you goes up every day.

（亚萨的诗歌，交与伶长，调用休要毁坏。）神阿，我们称谢你，我们称谢你，因为你的名相近，人都述说你奇妙的作为。
<To the chief music-maker; put to Al-tashheth. A Psalm. Of Asaph. A Song.> To you, O God, we give praise, to you we give praise: and those who give honour to your name make clear your works of power.

我到了所定的日期，必按正直施行审判。
When the right time has come, I will be the judge in righteousness.

地和其上的居民，都消化了。我曾立了地的柱子。（细拉）
When the earth and all its people become feeble, I am the support of its pillars. (Selah.)

我对狂傲人说，不要行事狂傲。对凶恶人说，不要举角。
I say to the men of pride, Let your pride be gone: and to the sinners, Let not your horn be lifted up.

不要把你们的角高举。不要挺着颈项说话。
Let not your horn be lifted up: let no more words of pride come from your outstretched necks.

因为高举非从东，非从西，也非从南而来。
For honour does not come from the east, or from the west, or uplifting from the south;

惟有神断定。他使这人降卑，使那人升高。
But God is the judge, putting down one, and lifting up another.

耶和华手里有杯。其中的酒起沫。杯内满了搀杂的酒。他倒出来。地上的恶人必都喝这酒的渣滓，而且喝尽。
For in the hand of the Lord is a cup, and the wine is red; it is well mixed, overflowing from his hand: he will make all the sinners of the earth take of it, even to the last drop.

但我要宣扬，直到永远。我要歌颂雅各的神。
But I will ever be full of joy, making songs of praise to the God of Jacob.

恶人一切的角，我要砍断。惟有义人的角，必被高举。
By him will all the horns of the sinners be cut off; but the horns of the upright will be lifted up.

（亚萨的诗歌，交与伶长，用丝弦的乐器。）在犹大神为人所认识。在以色列他的名为大。
<To the chief music-maker; put to Neginoth. A Psalm. Of Asaph. A Song.> In Judah is the knowledge of God; his name is great in Israel,

在撒冷有他的帐幕，在锡安有他的居所。
In Salem is his tent, his resting-place in Zion.

他在那里折断弓上的火箭，并盾牌，刀剑，和争战的兵器。（细拉）
There were the arrows of the bow broken, there he put an end to body-cover, sword, and fight. (Selah.)

你从有野食之山而来，有光华和荣美。
You are shining and full of glory, more than the eternal mountains.

心中勇敢的人，都被抢夺。他们睡了长觉。没有一个英雄能措手。
Gone is the wealth of the strong, their last sleep has overcome them; the men of war have become feeble.

雅各的神阿，你的斥责一发坐车的，骑马的，都沉睡了。
At the voice of your wrath, O God of Jacob, deep sleep has overcome carriage and horse.

惟独你是可畏的。你怒气一发，谁能在你面前站得住呢？
You, you are to be feared; who may keep his place before you in the time of your wrath?

你从天上使人听判断。神起来施行审判，要救地上一切谦卑的人。那时地就惧怕而静默。（细拉）
From heaven you gave your decision; the earth, in its fear, gave no sound,


When God took his place as judge, for the salvation of the poor on the earth. (Selah.)

人的忿怒，要成全你的荣美。人的余怒，你要禁止。
The ... will give you praise; the rest of ...

你们许愿，当向耶和华你们的神还愿。在他四面的人，都当拿贡物献给那可畏的主。
Give to the Lord your God what is his by right; let all who are round him give offerings to him who is to be feared.

他要挫折王子的骄气。他向地上的君王，显威可畏。
He puts an end to the wrath of rulers; he is feared by the kings of the earth.

（亚萨的诗，照耶杜顿的作法，交与伶长。）我要向神发声呼求。我向神发声，他必留心听我。
<To the chief music-maker. After Jeduthun. Of Asaph. A Psalm.> I was crying to God with my voice; even to God with my voice, and he gave ear to me.

我在患难之日寻求主。我在夜间不住地举手祷告。我的心不肯受安慰。
In the day of my trouble, my heart was turned to the Lord: my hand was stretched out in the night without resting; my soul would not be comforted.

我想念神，就烦躁不安。我沉吟悲伤，心便发昏。（细拉）
I will keep God in memory, with sounds of grief; my thoughts are troubled, and my spirit is overcome. (Selah.)

你叫我不能闭眼。我烦乱不安，甚至不能说话。
You keep my eyes from sleep; I am so troubled that no words come.

我追想古时之日，上古之年。
My thoughts go back to the days of the past, to the years which are gone.

我想起我夜间的歌曲，扪心自问。我心里也仔细省察。
The memory of my song comes back to me in the night; my thoughts are moving in my heart; my spirit is searching with care.

难道主要永远丢弃我，不再施恩吗？
Will the Lord put me away for ever? will he be kind no longer?

难道他的慈爱永远穷尽，他的应许世世废弃吗？
Is his mercy quite gone for ever? has his word come to nothing?

难道神忘记开恩。因发怒就止住他的慈悲吗？（细拉）
Has God put away the memory of his pity? are his mercies shut up by his wrath? (Selah.)

我便说，这是我的懦弱。但我要追念至高者显出右手之年代。
And I said, It is a weight on my spirit; but I will keep in mind the years of the right hand of the Most High.

我要提说耶和华所行的。我要记念你古时的奇事。
I will keep in mind the works of Jah: I will keep the memory of your wonders in the past.

我也要思想你的经营，默念你的作为。
I will give thought to all your work, while my mind goes over your acts of power.

神阿，你的作为是洁净的。有何神大如神呢？
Your way, O God, is holy: what god is so great as our God?

你是行奇事的神。你曾在列邦中彰显你的能力。
You are the God who does works of power: you have made your strength clear to the nations.

你曾用你的膀臂赎了你的民，就是雅各和约瑟的子孙。（细拉）
With your arm you have made your people free, the sons of Jacob and Joseph. (Selah.)

神阿，诸水见你，一见就都惊惶。深渊也都战抖。
The waters saw you, O God; the waters saw you, they were in fear: even the deep was troubled.

云中倒出水来。天空发出响声。你的箭也飞行四方。
The clouds sent out water; the skies gave out a sound; truly, your arrows went far and wide.

你的雷声在旋风中。电光照亮世界。大地战抖震动。
The voice of your thunder went rolling on; the world was flaming with the light of the storm; the earth was shaking.

你的道在海中，你的路在大水中，你的脚踪无人知道。
Your way was in the sea, and your road in the great waters; there was no knowledge of your footsteps.

你曾借摩西和亚伦的手，引导你的百姓，好像羊群一般。
You were guiding your people like a flock, by the hand of Moses and Aaron.

（亚萨的训诲诗。）我的民哪，你们要留心听我的训诲，侧耳听我口中的话。
<Maschil. Of Asaph.> Give ear, O my people, to my law; let your ears be bent down to the words of my mouth.

我要开口说比喻。我要说出古时的谜语。
Opening my mouth I will give out a story, even the dark sayings of old times;

是我们所听见所知道的，也是我们的祖宗告诉我们的。
Which have come to our hearing and our knowledge, as they were given to us by our fathers.

我们不将这些事向他们的子孙隐瞒。要将耶和华的美德和他的能力，并他奇妙的作为，述说给后代听。
We will not keep them secret from our children; we will make clear to the coming generation the praises of the Lord and his strength, and the great works of wonder which he has done.

因为他在雅各中立法度，在以色列中设律法，是他吩咐我们祖宗，要传给子孙的。
He put up a witness in Jacob, and made a law in Israel; which he gave to our fathers so that they might give knowledge of them to their children;

使将要生的后代子孙，可以晓得。他们也要起来告诉他们的子孙。
So that the generation to come might have knowledge of them, even the children of the future, who would give word of them to their children;

好叫他们仰望神，不忘记神的作为。惟要守他的命令。
So that they might put their hope in God, and not let God's works go out of their minds, but keep his laws;

不要像他们的祖宗，是顽梗悖逆居心不正之辈，向着神心不诚实。
And not be like their fathers, a stiff-necked and uncontrolled generation; a generation whose heart was hard, whose spirit was not true to God.

以法莲的子孙，带着兵器，拿着弓，临阵之日，转身退后。
The children of Ephraim, armed with bows, were turned back on the day of the fight.

他们不遵守神的约，不肯照他的律法行。
They were not ruled by God's word, and they would not go in the way of his law;

又忘记他所行的，和他显给他们奇妙的作为。
They let his works go out of their memory, and the wonders which he had made them see.

他在埃及地，在琐安田，在他们祖宗的眼前，施行奇事。
He did great works before the eyes of their fathers, in the land of Egypt, in the fields of Zoan.

他将海分裂，使他们过去。又叫水立起如垒。
The sea was cut in two so that they might go through; the waters were massed together on this side and on that.

他白日用云彩，终夜用火光，引导他们。
