In the daytime he was guiding them in the cloud, and all through the night with a light of fire.

他在旷野分裂磐石，多多地给他们水喝，如从深渊而出。
The rocks of the waste land were broken by his power, and he gave them drink as out of the deep waters.

他使水从磐石涌出，叫水如江河下流。
He made streams come out of the rock; and waters came flowing down like rivers.

他们却仍旧得罪他，在干燥之地悖逆至高者。
And they went on sinning against him even more, turning away from the Most High in the waste land;

他们心中试探神，随自己所欲的求食物。
Testing God in their hearts, requesting meat for their desire.

并且妄论神，说，神在旷野岂能摆设筵席吗？
They said bitter words against God, saying, Is God able to make ready a table in the waste land?

他曾击打磐石，使水涌出，成了江河。他还能赐粮食吗？还能为他的百姓预备肉吗？
See, the rock was cut open by his power, so that the water came rushing out, and overflowing streams; is he able to give us bread? is he able to get meat for his people?

所以耶和华听见，就发怒。有烈火向雅各烧起，有怒气向以色列上腾。
So these things came to the Lord's ears, and he was angry; and a fire was lighted against Jacob, and wrath came up against Israel;

因为他们不信服神，不倚赖他的救恩。
Because they had no faith in God, and no hope in his salvation.

他却吩咐天空，又敞开天上的门。
And he gave orders to the clouds on high, and the doors of heaven were open;

降吗哪像雨给他们吃，将天上的粮食赐给他们。
And he sent down manna like rain for their food, and gave them the grain of heaven.

各人（或作人）吃大能者的食物。他赐下粮食，使他们饱足。
Man took part in the food of strong ones; he sent them meat in full measure.

他领东风起在天空，又用能力引了南风来。
He sent an east wind from heaven, driving on the south wind by his power.

他降肉像雨在他们当中，多如尘土，又降飞鸟，多如海沙。
He sent down meat on them like dust, and feathered birds like the sand of the sea,

落在他们的营中，在他们住处的四面。
And he let it come down into their resting-place, round about their tents.

他们吃了，而且饱足。这样，就随了他们所欲的。
So they had food and were full; for he gave them their desire;

他们贪而无厌，食物还在他们口中的时候，
But they were not turned from their desires; and while the food was still in their mouths,

神的怒气，就向他们上腾，杀了他们内中的肥壮人。打倒以色列的少年人。
The wrath of God came on them, and put to death the fattest of them, and put an end to the young men of Israel.

虽是这样，他们仍旧犯罪，不信他奇妙的作为。
For all this they went on sinning even more, and had no faith in his great wonders.

因此他叫他们的日子，全归虚空，叫他们的年岁，尽属惊恐。
So their days were wasted like a breath, and their years in trouble.

他杀他们的时候，他们才求问他，回心转意，切切地寻求神。
When he sent death on them, then they made search for him; turning to him and looking for him with care;

他们也追念神是他们的磐石，至高的神，是他们的救赎主。
In the memory that God was their Rock, and the Most High God their saviour.

他们却用口谄媚他，用舌向他说谎。
But their lips were false to him, and their tongues were untrue to him;

因他们的心向他不正，在他的约上，也不忠心。
And their hearts were not right with him, and they did not keep their agreement with him.

但他有怜悯，赦免他们的罪孽，不灭绝他们。而且屡次消他的怒气，不发尽他的忿怒。
But he, being full of pity, has forgiveness for sin, and does not put an end to man: frequently turning back his wrath, and not being violently angry.

他想到他们不过是血气，是一阵去而不返的风。
So he kept in mind that they were only flesh; a breath which is quickly gone, and will not come again.

他们在旷野悖逆他，在荒地叫他担忧，何其多呢？
How frequently did they go against him in the waste land, and give him cause for grief in the dry places!

他们再三试探神，惹动以色列的圣者。
Again they put God to the test, and gave pain to the Holy One of Israel.

他们不追念他的能力（原文作手），和赎他们脱离敌人的日子。
They did not keep in mind the work of his hand, or the day when he took them from the power of their haters;

他怎样在埃及地显神迹，在琐安田显奇事。
How he had done his signs in Egypt, and his wonders in the field of Zoan;

把他们的江河，并河汊的水，都变为血，使他们不能喝。
So that their rivers were turned to blood, and they were not able to get drink from their streams.

他叫苍蝇成群，落在他们当中，嘬尽他们。又叫青蛙灭了他们。
He sent different sorts of flies among them, poisoning their flesh; and frogs for their destruction.

把他们的土产交给蚂蚱，把他们辛苦得来的交给蝗虫。
He gave the increase of their fields to worms, the fruits of their industry to the locusts.

他降冰雹打坏他们的葡萄树。下严霜打坏他们的桑树。
He sent ice for the destruction of their vines; their trees were damaged by the bitter cold.

又把他们的牲畜交给冰雹，把他们的群畜交给闪电。
Ice was rained down on their cattle; thunderstorms sent destruction among the flocks.

他使猛烈的怒气，和忿怒，恼恨，苦难，成了一群降灾的使者，临到他们。
He sent on them the heat of his wrath, his bitter disgust, letting loose evil angels among them.

他为自己的怒气修平了路，将他们交给瘟疫，使他们死亡。
He let his wrath have its way; he did not keep back their soul from death, but gave their life to disease.

在埃及击杀一切长子，在含的帐棚中，击杀他们强壮时头生的。
He gave to destruction all the first sons of Egypt; the first-fruits of their strength in the tents of Ham;

他却领出自己的民如羊，在旷野引他们如羊群。
But he took his people out like sheep, guiding them in the waste land like a flock.

他领他们稳稳妥妥的，使他们不至害怕。海却淹没他们的仇敌。
He took them on safely so that they had no fear; but their haters were covered by the sea.

他带他们到自己圣地的边界，到他右手所得的这山地。
And he was their guide to his holy land, even to the mountain, which his right hand had made his;

他在他们面前赶出外邦人，用绳子将外邦的地量给他们为业，叫以色列支派的人，住在他们的帐棚里。
Driving out nations before them, marking out the line of their heritage, and giving the people of Israel their tents for a resting-place.

他们仍旧试探悖逆至高的神，不守他的法度。
But they were bitter against the Most High God, testing him, and not keeping his laws;

反倒退后，行诡诈，像他们的祖宗一样。他们改变，如同翻背的弓。
Their hearts were turned back and untrue like their fathers; they were turned to one side like a twisted bow.

因他们的丘坛，惹了他的怒气，因他们雕刻的偶像，触动他的愤恨。
They made him angry with their high places; moving him to wrath with their images.

神听见，就发怒，极其憎恶以色列人。
When this came to God's ears he was very angry, and gave up Israel completely;

甚至他离弃示罗的帐幕，就是他在人间所搭的帐棚。
So that he went away from the holy place in Shiloh, the tent which he had put among men;

又将他的约柜（原文作能力）交与人掳去，将他的荣耀交在敌人手中。
And he let his strength be taken prisoner, and gave his glory into the hands of his hater.

并将他的百姓交与刀剑，向他的产业发怒。
He gave his people up to the sword, and was angry with his heritage.

少年人被火烧灭。处女也无喜歌。
Their young men were burned in the fire; and their virgins were not praised in the bride-song.

祭司倒在刀下。寡妇却不哀哭。
Their priests were put to death by the sword, and their widows made no weeping for them.

那时主像世人睡醒，像勇士饮酒呼喊。
Then was the Lord like one awaking from sleep, and like a strong man crying out because of wine.

他就打退了他的敌人，叫他们永蒙羞辱。
His haters were turned back by his blows and shamed for ever.

并且他弃掉约瑟的帐棚，不拣选以法莲支派，
And he put the tent of Joseph on one side, and took not the tribe of Ephraim;

却拣选犹大支派，他所喜爱的锡安山。
But he took the tribe of Judah for himself, and the mountain of Zion, in which he had pleasure.

盖造他的圣所，好像高峰，又像他建立永存之地。
And he made his holy place like the high heaven, like the earth which is fixed by him for ever.

又拣选他的仆人大卫，从羊圈中将他召来。
He took David to be his servant, taking him from the place of the flocks;

叫他不再跟从那些带奶的母羊，为要牧养自己的百姓雅各，和自己的产业以色列。
From looking after the sheep which were giving milk, he took him to give food to Jacob his people, and to Israel his heritage.

于是他按心中的纯正，牧养他们，用手中的巧妙，引导他们。
So he gave them food with an upright heart, guiding them by the wisdom of his hands.

（亚萨的诗。）神阿，外邦人进入你的产业，污秽你的圣殿，使耶路撒冷变成荒堆。
<A Psalm. Of Asaph.> O God, the nations have come into your heritage; they have made your holy Temple unclean; they have made Jerusalem a mass of broken walls.

把你仆人的尸首，交与天空的飞鸟为食，把你圣民的肉，交与地上的野兽。
They have given the bodies of your servants as food to the birds of the air, and the flesh of your saints to the beasts of the earth.

在耶路撒冷周围流他们的血如水，无人葬埋。
Their blood has been flowing like water round about Jerusalem; there was no one to put them in their last resting-place.

我们成为邻国的羞辱，成为我们四围人的嗤笑讥刺。
We are looked down on by our neighbours, we are laughed at and made sport of by those who are round us.

耶和华阿，这到几时呢？你要动怒到永远吗？你的愤恨要如火焚烧吗？
How long, O Lord? will you be angry for ever? will your wrath go on burning like fire?

愿你将你的忿怒倒在那不认识你的外邦，和那不求告你名的国度。
Let your wrath be on the nations who have no knowledge of you, and on the kingdoms who have not made prayer to your name.

因为他们吞了雅各，把他的住处变为荒场。
For they have taken Jacob for their meat, and made waste his house.

求你不要记念我们先祖的罪孽，向我们追讨。愿你的慈悲快迎着我们。因为我们落到极卑微的地步。
Do not keep in mind against us the sins of our fathers; let your mercy come to us quickly, for we have been made very low.

拯救我们的神阿，求你因你名的荣耀，帮助我们，为你名的缘故，搭救我们，赦免我们的罪。
Give us help, O God of our salvation, for the glory of your name; take us out of danger and give us forgiveness for our sins, because of your name.

为何容外邦人说，他们的神在哪里呢？愿你使外邦人知道你在我们眼前，伸你仆人流血的冤。
Why may the nations say, Where is their God? Let payment for the blood of your servants be made openly among the nations before our eyes.

愿被囚之人的叹息，达到你面前。愿你按你的大能力，存留那些将要死的人。
Let the cry of the prisoner come before you; with your strong arm make free the children of death;

主阿，愿你将我们邻邦所羞辱你的羞辱，加七倍归到他们身上。
And give punishment seven times over into the breast of our neighbours for the bitter words which they have said against you, O Lord.

这样，你的民，你草场的羊，要称谢你，直到永远。要述说赞美你的话，直到万代。
So we your people, and the sheep of your flock, will give you glory for ever: we will go on praising you through all generations.

（亚萨的诗，交与伶长，调用为证的百合花。）领约瑟如领羊群之以色列的牧者阿，求你留心听。坐在二基路伯上的阿，求你发出光来。
<To the chief music-maker; put to Shoshannim-eduth. Of Asaph. A Psalm.> Give ear, O Keeper of Israel, guiding Joseph like a flock; you who have your seat on the winged ones, let your glory be seen.

在以法莲便雅悯玛拿西前面施展你的大能，来救我们。
Before Ephraim and Benjamin and Manasseh, let your strength be awake from sleep, and come as our salvation.

神阿，求你使我们回转（回转或作复兴），使你的脸发光，我们便要得救。
Take us back again, O God; let us see the shining of your face, and let us be safe.

耶和华万军之神阿，你向你百姓的祷告发怒，要到几时呢？
O Lord God of armies, how long will your wrath be burning against the rest of your people?

你以眼泪当食物给他们吃，又多量出眼泪给他们喝。
You have given them the bread of weeping for food; for their drink you have given them sorrow in great measure.

你使邻邦因我们分争。我们的仇敌彼此戏笑。
You make us a cause of war among our neighbours; our haters are laughing at us among themselves.

万军之神阿，求你使我们回转，使你的脸发光，我们便要得救。
Take us back again, O God of armies; let us see the shining of your face, and let us be safe.

你从埃及挪出一棵葡萄树，赶出外邦人，把这树栽上。
You took a vine out of Egypt: driving out the nations, and planting it in their land.

你在这树根前预备了地方，他就深深扎根，爬满了地。
You made ready a place for it, so that it might take deep root, and it sent out its branches over all the land.

他的影子遮满了山，枝子好像佳美的香柏树。
The mountains were covered with its shade, and the great trees with its branches.

他发出枝子，长到大海，发出蔓子，延到大河。
It sent out its arms to the Sea, and its branches to the River.

你为何拆毁这树的篱笆，任凭一切过路的人摘取。
Why are its walls broken down by your hands, so that all who go by may take its fruit?

林中出来的野猪，把他糟踏，野地的走兽，拿他当食物。
It is uprooted by the pigs from the woods, the beasts of the field get their food from it.

万军之神阿，求你回转，从天上垂看，眷顾这葡萄树，
Come back, O God of armies: from heaven let your eyes be turned to this vine, and give your mind to it,

保护你右手所栽的，和你为自己所坚固的枝子。
Even to the tree which was planted by your right hand, and to the branch which you made strong for yourself.

这树已经被火焚烧被刀砍伐，他们因你脸上的怒容就灭亡了。
It is burned with fire; it is cut down: they are made waste by the wrath of your face.

愿你的手扶持你右边的人，就是你为自己所坚固的人子。
Let your hand be on the man of your right hand, on the son of man whom you made strong for yourself.

这样，我们便不退后离开你。求你救活我们，我们就要求告你的名。
So will we not be turned back from you; keep us in life, and we will give praise to your name.

耶和华万军之神阿，求你使我们回转，使你的脸发光，我们便要得救。
Take us back, O Lord God of armies; let us see the shining of your face, and let us be safe.

（亚萨的诗，交与伶长。用迦特乐器。）你们当向神我们的力量大声欢呼，向雅各的神发声欢乐，
<To the chief music-maker; put to the Gittith. Of Asaph.> Make a song to God our strength: make a glad cry to the God of Jacob.

唱起诗歌，打手鼓，弹美琴与瑟。
Take up the melody, playing on an instrument of music, even on corded instruments.

当在月朔，并月望，我们过节的日期，吹角。
Let the horn be sounded in the time of the new moon, at the full moon, on our holy feast-day:

因这是为以色列定的律例，是雅各神的典章。
For this is a rule for Israel, and a law of the God of Jacob.

他去攻击埃及地的时候，在约瑟中间立此为证。我在那里听见我所不明白的言语。
He gave it to Joseph as a witness, when he went out over the land of Egypt; then the words of a strange tongue were sounding in my ears.

神说，我使你的肩得脱重担，你的手放下筐子。
I took the weight from his back; his hands were made free from the baskets.

你在急难中呼求，我就搭救你。我在雷的隐密处应允你，在米利巴水那里试验你。（细拉）
You gave a cry in your trouble, and I made you free; I gave you an answer in the secret place of the thunder; I put you to the test at the waters of Meribah. (Selah.)

我的民哪，你当听。我要劝戒你。以色列阿，甚愿你肯听从我。
Give ear, O my people, and I will give you my word, O Israel, if you will only do as I say!

在你当中不可有别的神。外邦的神，你也不可下拜。
There is to be no strange god among you; you are not to give worship to any other god.

我是耶和华你的神，曾把你从埃及地领上来。你要大大张口，我就给你充满。
I am the Lord your God, who took you up from the land of Egypt: let your mouth be open wide, so that I may give you food.

无奈我的民不听我的声音。以色列全不理我。
But my people did not give ear to my voice; Israel would have nothing to do with me.

我便任凭他们心里刚硬，随自己的计谋而行。
So I gave them up to the desires of their hearts; that they might go after their evil purposes.

甚愿我的民肯听从我，以色列肯行我的道。
If only my people would give ear to me, walking in my ways!

我便速速治服他们的仇敌，反手攻击他们的敌人。
I would quickly overcome their haters: my hand would be turned against those who make war on them.

恨耶和华的人必来投降，但他的百姓，必永久长存。
The haters of the Lord would be broken, and their destruction would be eternal.

他也必拿上好的麦子给他们吃。又拿从磐石出的蜂蜜，叫他们饱足。
I would give them the best grain for food; you would be full of honey from the rock.

（亚萨的诗。）神站在有权力者的会中。在诸神中行审判。
<A Psalm. Of Asaph.> God is in the meeting-place of God; he is judging among the gods.

说，你们审判不秉公义，徇恶人的情面，要到几时呢？（细拉）
How long will you go on judging falsely, having respect for the persons of evil-doers? (Selah.)

你们当为贫寒的人和孤儿伸冤。当为困苦和穷乏的人施行公义。
Give ear to the cause of the poor and the children without fathers; let those who are troubled and in need have their rights.

当保护贫寒和穷乏的人，救他们脱离恶人的手。
Be the saviour of the poor and those who have nothing: take them out of the hand of the evil-doers.

你们仍不知道，也不明白，在黑暗中走来走去。地的根基都摇动了。
They have no knowledge or sense; they go about in the dark: all the bases of the earth are moved.

我曾说，你们是神，都是至高者的儿子。
I said, You are gods; all of you are the sons of the Most High:

然而你们要死，与世人一样。要仆倒，像王子中的一位。
But you will come to death like men, falling like one of the rulers of the earth.

神阿，求你起来，审判世界。因为你要得万邦为业。
Up! O God, come as judge of the earth; for all the nations are your heritage.

（亚萨的诗歌。）神阿，求你不要静默。神阿，求你不要闭口，也不要不作声。
<A Song. A Psalm. Of Asaph.> O God, do not keep quiet: let your lips be open and take no rest, O God.

因为你的仇敌喧嚷。恨你的抬起头来。
For see! those who make war on you are out of control; your haters are lifting up their heads.

他们同谋奸诈，要害你的百姓，彼此商议，要害你所隐藏的人。
They have made wise designs against your people, talking together against those whom you keep in a secret place.

他们说，来吧，我们将他们剪灭，使他们不再成国。使以色列的名，不再被人记念。
They have said, Come, let us put an end to them as a nation; so that the name of Israel may go out of man's memory.

他们同心商议，彼此结盟，要抵挡你。
For they have all come to an agreement; they are all joined together against you:

就是住帐棚的以东人，和以实玛利人。摩押和夏甲人。
The tents of Edom and the Ishmaelites; Moab and the Hagarites;

迦巴勒，亚扪，和亚玛力，非利士，并推罗的居民。
Gebal and Ammon and Amalek; the Philistines and the people of Tyre;

亚述也与他们连合。他们作罗得子孙的帮手。（细拉）
Assur is joined with them; they have become the support of the children of Lot. (Selah.)

求你待他们如待米甸，如在基顺河待西西拉和耶宾一样。
Do to them what you did to the Midianites; what you did to Sisera and Jabin, at the stream of Kishon:

他们在隐多珥灭亡，成了地上的粪土。
Who came to destruction at En-dor; their bodies became dust and waste.

求你叫他们的首领，像俄立和西伊伯，叫他们的王子，都像西巴和撒慕拿。
Make their chiefs like Oreb and Zeeb; and all their rulers like Zebah and Zalmunna:

他们说，我们要得神的住处，作为自己的产业。
Who have said, Let us take for our heritage the resting-place of God.

我的神阿，求你叫他们像旋风的尘土，像风前的碎秸。
O my God, make them like the rolling dust; like dry stems before the wind.

火怎样焚烧树林，火焰怎样烧着山岭。
As fire burning a wood, and as a flame causing fire on the mountains,

求你也照样用狂风追赶他们，用暴雨恐吓他们。
So go after them with your strong wind, and let them be full of fear because of your storm.

愿你使他们满面羞耻，好叫他们寻求你耶和华的名。
Let their faces be full of shame; so that they may give honour to your name, O Lord.

愿他们永远羞愧惊惶。愿他们惭愧灭亡。
Let them be overcome and troubled for ever; let them be put to shame and come to destruction;

使他们知道惟独你名为耶和华的，是全地以上的至高者。
So that men may see that you only, whose name is Yahweh, are Most High over all the earth.

（可拉后裔的诗，交与伶长。用迦特乐器。）万军之耶和华阿，你的居所何等可爱。
<To the chief music-maker; put to the Gittith A Psalm. Of the sons of Korah.> How dear are your tents, O Lord of armies!

我羡慕渴想耶和华的院宇。我的心肠，我的肉体，向永生神呼吁（或作欢呼）。
The passion of my soul's desire is for the house of the Lord; my heart and my flesh are crying out for the living God.

万军之耶和华我的王，我的神阿，在你祭坛那里，麻雀为自己找着房屋。燕子为自己找着抱雏之窝。
The little birds have places for themselves, where they may put their young, even your altars, O Lord of armies, my King and my God.

如此住在你殿中的，便为有福。他们仍要赞美你。（细拉）
Happy are they whose resting-place is in your house: they will still be praising you. (Selah.)

靠你有力量心中想往锡安大道的，这人便为有福。
Happy is the man whose strength is in you; in whose heart are the highways to Zion.

他们经过流泪谷，叫这谷变为泉源之地。并有秋雨之福，盖满了全谷。
Going through the valley of balsam-trees, they make it a place of springs; it is clothed with blessings by the early rain.

他们行走，力上加力，各人到锡安朝见神。
They go from strength to strength; every one of them comes before God in Zion.

耶和华万军之神阿，求你听我的祷告。雅各的神阿，求你留心听。（细拉）
O Lord God of armies, let my prayer come to you: give ear, O God of Jacob. (Selah.)

神阿，你是我们的盾牌。求你垂顾观看你受膏者的面。
O God, let your eyes be on him who is our safe cover, and let your heart be turned to your king.

在你的院宇住一日，胜似在别处住千日。宁可在我神殿中看门，不愿住在恶人的帐棚里。
For a day in your house is better than a thousand. It is better to be a door-keeper in the house of my God, than to be living in the tents of sin.

因为耶和华神是日头，是盾牌，要赐下恩惠和荣耀。他未尝留下一样好处，不给那些行动正直的人。
The Lord God is our sun and our strength: the Lord will give grace and glory: he will not keep back any good thing from those whose ways are upright.

万军之耶和华阿，倚靠你的人，便为有福。
O Lord of armies, happy is the man whose hope is in you.

（可拉后裔的诗，交与伶长。）耶和华阿，你已经向你的地施恩，救回被掳的雅各。
<To the chief music-maker. A Psalm. Of the sons of Korah.> Lord, you were good to your land: changing the fate of Jacob.

你赦免了你百姓的罪孽，遮盖了他们一切的过犯。（细拉）
The wrongdoing of your people had forgiveness; all their sin had been covered. (Selah.)

你收转了所发的忿怒，和你猛烈的怒气。
You were no longer angry: you were turned from the heat of your wrath.

拯救我们的神阿，求你使我们回转，叫你的恼恨向我们止息。
Come back to us, O God of our salvation, and be angry with us no longer.

你要向我们发怒到永远吗？你要将你的怒气延留到万代吗？
Will you go on being angry with us for ever? will you keep your wrath against us through all the long generations?

你不再将我们救活，使你的百姓靠你欢喜吗？
Will you not give us life again, so that your people may be glad in you?

耶和华阿，求你使我们得见你的慈爱，又将你的救恩赐给我们。
Let us see your mercy, O Lord, and give us your salvation.

我要听神耶和华所说的话。因为他必应许将平安赐给他的百姓，他的圣民。他们却不可再转去妄行。
I will give ear to the voice of the Lord; for he will say words of peace to his people and to his saints; but let them not go back to their foolish ways.

他的救恩，诚然与敬畏他的人相近，叫荣耀住在我们的地上。
Truly, his salvation is near to his worshippers; so that glory may be in our land.

慈爱和诚实，彼此相遇。公义和平安，彼此相亲。
Mercy and faith have come together; righteousness and peace have given one another a kiss.

诚实从地而生，公义从天而现。
Faith comes up from the earth like a plant; righteousness is looking down from heaven.

耶和华必将好处赐给我们。我们的地，也要多出土产。
The Lord will give what is good; and our land will give its increase.

公义要行在他面前，叫他的脚踪，成为可走的路。
Righteousness will go before him, making a way for his footsteps.

（大卫的祈祷。）耶和华阿，求你侧耳应允我，因我是困苦穷乏的。
<A Prayer. Of David.> Let your ears be open to my voice, O Lord, and give me an answer; for I am poor and in need.

求你保存我的性命。因我是虔诚人。我的神阿，求你拯救这倚靠你的仆人。
Keep my soul, for I am true to you; O my God, give salvation to your servant, whose hope is in you.

主阿，求你怜悯我，因我终日求告你。
Have mercy on me, O Lord; for my cry goes up to you all the day.

主阿，求你使仆人心里欢喜。因为我的心仰望你。
Make glad the soul of your servant; for it is lifted up to you, O Lord.

主阿，你本为良善，乐意饶恕人，有丰盛的慈爱，赐给凡求告你的人。
You are good, O Lord, and full of forgiveness; your mercy is great to all who make their cry to you.

耶和华阿，求你留心听我的祷告，垂听我恳求的声音。
O Lord, give ear to my prayer; and take note of the sound of my requests.

我在患难之日要求告你。因为你必应允我。
In the day of my trouble I send up my cry to you; for you will give me an answer.

主阿，诸神之中，没有可比你的。你的作为也无可比。
There is no god like you, O Lord; there are no works like your works.

主阿，你所造的万民，都要来敬拜你。他们也要荣耀你的名。
Let all the nations whom you have made come and give worship to you, O Lord, giving glory to your name.

因你为大，且行奇妙的事。惟独你是神。
For you are great, and do great works of wonder; you only are God.

耶和华阿，求你将你的道指教我。我要照你的真理行。求你使我专心敬畏你的名。
Make your way clear to me, O Lord; I will go on my way in your faith: let my heart be glad in the fear of your name.

主我的神阿，我要一心称赞你。我要荣耀你的名，直到永远。
I will give you praise, O Lord my God, with all my heart; I will give glory to your name for ever.

因为你向我发的慈爱是大的。你救了我的灵魂，免入极深的阴间。
For your mercy to me is great; you have taken my soul up from the deep places of the underworld.

神阿，骄傲的人起来攻击我，又有一党强横的人寻索我的命。他们没有将你放在眼中。
O God, men of pride have come up against me, and the army of violent men would take my life; they have not put you before them.

主阿，你是有怜悯有恩典的神，不轻易发怒，并有丰盛的慈爱和诚实。
But you, O Lord, are a God full of pity and forgiveness, slow to get angry, great in mercy and wisdom.

求你向我转脸，怜恤我，将你的力量赐给仆人，救你婢女的儿子。
O be turned to me and have mercy on me: give your strength to your servant, and your salvation to the son of her who is your servant.

求你向我显出恩待我的凭据，叫恨我的人看见，便羞愧，因为你耶和华帮助我，安慰我。
Give me a sign for good; so that my haters may see it and be shamed; because you, Lord, have been my help and comfort.

（可拉后裔的诗歌。）耶和华所立的根基在圣山上。
<Of the sons of Korah. A Psalm. A Song.> This house is resting on the holy mountain.

他爱锡安的门，胜于爱雅各一切的住处。
The Lord has more love for the doors of Zion than for all the tents of Jacob.

神的城阿，有荣耀的事乃指着你说的。（细拉）
Noble things are said of you, O town of God. (Selah.)

我要提起拉哈伯，和巴比伦人是在认识我之中的，看哪，非利士，和推罗，并古实人，个个生在那里。
Rahab and Babylon will be named among those who have knowledge of me; see, Philistia and Tyre, with Ethiopia; this man had his birth there.

论到锡安必说，这一个那一个都生在其中。而且至高者必亲自坚立这城。
And of Zion it will be said, This or that man had his birth there; and the Most High will make her strong.

当耶和华记录万民的时候，他要点出这一个生在那里。（细拉）
The Lord will keep in mind, when he is writing the records of the people, that this man had his birth there. (Selah.)

歌唱的，跳舞的，都要说，我的泉源都在你里面。
The players on instruments will be there, and the dancers will say, All my springs are in you.

（可拉后裔的诗歌，就是以斯拉人希幔的训诲诗，交与伶长。调用麻哈拉利暗俄。）耶和华拯救我的神阿，我昼夜在你面前呼吁。
<A Song. A Psalm. Of the sons of Korah. To the chief music-maker; put to Mahalath Leannoth. Maschil. Of Heman the Ezrahite.> O Lord, God of my salvation, I have been crying to you for help by day and by night:

愿我的祷告达到你面前。求你侧耳听我的呼求。
Let my prayer come before you; give ear to my cry:

因为我心里满了患难，我的性命临近阴间。
For my soul is full of evils, and my life has come near to the underworld.

我算和下坑的人同列，如同无力的人一样。（无力或作没有帮助）
I am numbered among those who go down into the earth; I have become like a man for whom there is no help:

我被丢在死人中，好像被杀的人，躺在坟墓里。他们是你不再记念的，与你隔绝了。
My soul is among the dead, like those in the underworld, to whom you give no more thought; for they are cut off from your care.

你把我放在极深的坑里，在黑暗地方，在深处。
You have put me in the lowest deep, even in dark places.

你的忿怒重压我身。你用一切的波浪困住我。（细拉）
The weight of your wrath is crushing me, all your waves have overcome me. (Selah.)

你把我所认识的隔在远处，使我为他们所憎恶。我被拘困，不得出来。
You have sent my friends far away from me; you have made me a disgusting thing in their eyes: I am shut up, and not able to come out.

我的眼睛，因困苦而干瘪。耶和华阿，我天天求告你，向你举手。
My eyes are wasting away because of my trouble: Lord, my cry has gone up to you every day, my hands are stretched out to you.

你岂要行奇事给死人看吗？难道阴魂还能起来称赞你吗？（细拉）
Will you do works of wonder for the dead? will the shades come back to give you praise? (Selah.)

岂能在坟墓里述说你的慈爱吗？岂能在灭亡中述说你的信实吗？
Will the story of your mercy be given in the house of the dead? will news of your faith come to the place of destruction?

你的奇事，岂能在幽暗里被知道吗？你的公义，岂能在忘记之地被知道吗？
May there be knowledge of your wonders in the dark? or of your righteousness where memory is dead?

耶和华阿，我呼求你。我早晨的祷告要达到你面前。
But to you did I send up my cry, O Lord; in the morning my prayer came before you.

耶和华阿，你为何丢弃我。为何掩面不顾我。
Lord, why have you sent away my soul? why is your face covered from me?

我自幼受苦，几乎死亡。我受你的惊恐，甚至慌张。
I have been troubled and in fear of death from the time when I was young; your wrath is hard on me, and I have no strength.

你的烈怒漫过我身。你的惊吓，把我剪除。
The heat of your wrath has gone over me; I am broken by your cruel punishments.

这些终日如水环绕我，一齐都来围困我。
They are round me all the day like water; they have made a circle about me.

你把我的良朋密友隔在远处，使我所认识的人，进入黑暗里。
You have sent my friends and lovers far from me; I am gone from the memory of those who are dear to me.

（以斯拉人以探的训诲诗。）我要歌唱耶和华的慈爱，直到永远。我要用口将你的信实传与万代。
<Maschil. Of Ethan the Ezrahite.> My song will be of the mercies of the Lord for ever: with my mouth will I make his faith clear to all generations.

因我曾说，你的慈悲，必建立到永远。你的信实，必坚立在天上。
For you have said, Mercy will be made strong for ever; my faith will be unchanging in the heavens.

我与我所拣选的人立了约，向我的仆人大卫起了誓。
I have made an agreement with the man of my selection, I have made an oath to David my servant;

我要建立你的后裔，直到永远，要建立你的宝座，直到万代。
I will make your seed go on for ever, your kingdom will be strong through all generations. (Selah.)

耶和华阿，诸天要称赞你的奇事。在圣者的会中，要称赞你的信实。
In heaven let them give praise for your wonders, O Lord; and your unchanging faith among the saints.

在天空谁能比耶和华呢？神的众子中，谁能像耶和华呢？
For who is there in the heavens in comparison with the Lord? who is like the Lord among the sons of the gods?

他在圣者的会中，是大有威严的神，比一切在他四围的更可畏惧。
God is greatly to be feared among the saints, and to be honoured over all those who are about him.

耶和华万军之神阿，哪一个大能者象你耶和华？你的信实，是在你的四围。
O Lord God of armies, who is strong like you, O Jah? and your unchanging faith is round about you.

你管辖海的狂傲。波浪翻腾，你就使他平静了。
You have rule over the sea in storm; when its waves are troubled, you make them calm.

你打碎了拉哈伯似乎是已杀的人。你用有能的膀臂打散了你的仇敌。
Rahab was crushed by you like one wounded to death; with your strong arm you put to flight all your haters.

天属你，地也属你。世界和其中所充满的，都为你所建立。
Yours are the heavens, and the earth is yours; you have made the world, and everything which is in it.

南北为你所创造。他泊和黑门都因你的名欢呼。
You have made the north and the south; Tabor and Hermon are sounding with joy at your name.

你有大能的膀臂。你的手有力，你的右手也高举。
Yours is an arm of power; strong is your hand and high your right hand.

公义和公平，是你宝座的根基。慈爱和诚实，行在你前面。
The seat of your kingdom is resting on righteousness and right judging: mercy and good faith come before your face.

知道向你欢呼的，那民是有福的。耶和华阿，他们在你脸上的光里行走。
Happy are the people who have knowledge of the holy cry: the light of your face, O Lord, will be shining on their way.

他们因你的名终日欢乐，因你的公义得以高举。
In your name will they have joy all the day: in your righteousness will they be lifted up.

你是他们力量的荣耀。因为你喜悦我们，我们的角必被高举。
For you are the glory of their strength; in your pleasure will our horn be lifted up.

我们的盾牌属耶和华。我们的王属以色列的圣者。
For our breastplate is the Lord; and our king is the Holy One of Israel's.

当时你在异象中晓谕你的圣民，说，我已把救助之力，加在那有能者的身上。我高举那从民中所拣选的。
Then your voice came to your holy one in a vision, saying, I have put the crown on a strong one, lifting up one taken from among the people.

我寻得我的仆人大卫，用我的圣膏膏他。
I have made discovery of David my servant; I have put my holy oil on his head.

我的手必使他坚立。我的膀臂也必坚固他。
My hand will be his support; my arm will give him strength.

仇敌必不勒索他，凶恶之子，也不苦害他。
The deceit of those who are against him will not overcome him; he will not be troubled by the sons of evil.

我要在他面前打碎他的敌人，击杀那恨他的人。
I will have those who are against him broken before his face, and his haters will be crushed under my blows.

只是我的信实，和我的慈爱，要与他同在。因我的名，他的角必被高举。
But my faith and my mercy will be with him; and in my name will his horn be lifted up.

我要使他的左手伸到海上，右手伸到河上。
I will put his hand in the sea, and his right hand in the rivers.

他要称呼我说，你是我的父是我的神，是拯救我的磐石。
He will say to me, You are my father, my God, and the Rock of my salvation.

我也要立他为长子，为世上最高的君王。
And I will make him the first of my sons, most high over the kings of the earth.

我要为他存留我的慈爱，直到永远。我与他立的约，必要坚定。
I will keep my mercy for him for ever; my agreement with him will not be changed.

我也要使他的后裔，存到永远，使他的宝座，如天之久。
His seed will keep their place for ever; his kingdom will be eternal, like the heavens.

倘若他的子孙离弃我的律法，不照我的典章行。
If his children give up my law, and are not ruled by my decisions;

背弃我的律例，不遵守我的诫命。
If my rules are broken, and my orders are not kept;

我就要用杖责罚他们的过犯，用鞭责罚他们的罪孽。
Then I will send punishment on them for their sin; my rod will be the reward of their evil-doing.

只是我必不将我的慈爱，全然收回，也必不叫我的信实废弃。
But I will not take away my mercy from him, and will not be false to my faith.

我必不背弃我的约，也不改变我口中所出的。
I will be true to my agreement; the things which have gone out of my lips will not be changed.

我一次指着自己的圣洁起誓。我决不向大卫说谎。
I have made an oath once by my holy name, that I will not be false to David.

他的后裔要存到永远，他的宝座在我面前，如日之恒一般。
His seed will not come to an end for ever; the seat of his kingdom will be like the sun before me.

又如月亮永远坚立，如天上确实的见证。（细拉）
It will be fixed for ever like the moon; and the witness in heaven is true. (Selah.)

但你恼怒你的受膏者，就丢掉弃绝他。
But you have put him away in disgust; you have been angry with the king of your selection.

你厌恶了与仆人所立的约，将他的冠冕践踏于地。
You have made your agreement with your servant of no effect: you have had no respect for his crown, it has come down even to the earth.

你拆毁了他一切的篱笆。使他的保障，变为荒场。
All his walls are broken down; you have given his strong towers to destruction.

凡过路的人，都抢夺他。他成为邻邦的羞辱。
All those who come by take away his goods; he is laughed at by his neighbours.

你高举了他敌人的右手。你叫他一切的仇敌欢喜。
You have given power to the right hand of his haters; you have made glad all those who are against him.

你叫他的刀剑卷刃，叫他在争战之中站立不住。
His sword is turned back; you have not been his support in the fight.

你使他的光辉止息，将他的宝座推倒于地。
You have put an end to his glory: the seat of his kingdom has been levelled to the earth.

你减少他青年的日子。又使他蒙羞。（细拉）
You have made him old before his time; he is covered with shame. (Selah.)

耶和华阿，这要到几时呢？你要将自己隐藏到永远吗？你的忿怒如火焚烧，要到几时呢？
How long, O Lord, will you Keep yourself for ever from our eyes? how long will your wrath be burning like fire?

求你想念我的时候是何等的短少。你创造世人，要使他们归何等的虚空呢？（细拉）
See how short my time is; why have you made all men for no purpose?

谁能常活免死，救他的灵魂脱离阴间的权柄呢？（细拉）
What man now living will not see death? will he be able to keep back his soul from the underworld? (Selah.)

主阿，你从前凭你的信实向大卫立誓，要施行的慈爱在哪里呢？
Lord, where are your earlier mercies? where is the oath which you made to David in unchanging faith?

主阿，求你记念仆人们所受的羞辱，记念我怎样将一切强盛民的羞辱存在我怀里。
Keep in mind, O Lord, the shame of your servants, and how the bitter words of all the people have come into my heart;

耶和华阿，你的仇敌，用这羞辱，羞辱了你的仆人，羞辱了你受膏者的脚踪。
The bitter words of your haters, O Lord, shaming the footsteps of your king.

耶和华是应当称颂的，直到永远。阿们，阿们。
Let the Lord be praised for ever. So be it, So be it.

（神人摩西的祈祷。）主阿，你世世代代作我们的居所。
<A Prayer of Moses, the man of God.> Lord, you have been our resting-place in all generations.

诸山未曾生出，地与世界你未曾造成，从亘古到永远，你是神。
Before the mountains were made, before you had given birth to the earth and the world, before time was, and for ever, you are God.

你使人归于尘土，说，你们世人要归回。
You send man back to his dust; and say, Go back, you children of men.

在你看来，千年如已过的昨日，又如夜间的一更。
For to you a thousand years are no more than yesterday when it is past, and like a watch in the night.

你叫他们如水冲去。他们如睡一觉。早晨他们如生长的草。
...

早晨发芽生长，晚上割下枯干。
In the morning it is green; in the evening it is cut down, and becomes dry.

我们因你的怒气而消灭，因你的忿怒而惊惶。
We are burned up by the heat of your passion, and troubled by your wrath.

你将我们的罪孽摆在你面前，将我们的隐恶摆在你面光之中。
You have put our evil doings before you, our secret sins in the light of your face.

我们经过的日子，都在你震怒之下。我们度尽的年岁好像一声叹息。
For all our days have gone by in your wrath; our years come to an end like a breath.

我们一生的年日是七十岁。若是强壮可到八十岁。但其中所矜夸的，不过是劳苦愁烦。转眼成空，我们便如飞而去。
The measure of our life is seventy years; and if through strength it may be eighty years, its pride is only trouble and sorrow, for it comes to an end and we are quickly gone.

谁晓得你怒气的权势？谁按着你该受的敬畏晓得你的忿怒呢？
Who has knowledge of the power of your wrath, or who takes note of the weight of your passion?

求你指教我们怎样数算自己的日子，好叫我们得着智慧的心。
So give us knowledge of the number of our days, that we may get a heart of wisdom.

耶和华阿，我们要等到几时呢？求你转回，为你的仆人后悔。
Come back, O Lord; how long? let your purpose for your servants be changed.

求你使我们早早饱得你的慈爱，好叫我们一生一世欢呼喜乐。
In the morning give us your mercy in full measure; so that we may have joy and delight all our days.

求你照着你使我们受苦的日子，和我们遭难的年岁，叫我们喜乐。
Make us glad in reward for the days of our sorrow, and for the years in which we have seen evil.

愿你的作为向你仆人显现。愿你的荣耀向他们子孙显明。
Make your work clear to your servants, and your glory to their children.

愿主我们神的荣美，归于我们身上。愿你坚立我们手所作的工。我们手所作的工，愿你坚立。
Let the pleasure of the Lord our God be on us: O Lord, give strength to the work of our hands.

住在至高者隐密处的，必住在全能者的荫下。
Happy is he whose resting-place is in the secret of the Lord, and under the shade of the wings of the Most High;

我要论到耶和华说，他是我的避难所，是我的山寨，是我的神，是我所倚靠的。
Who says of the Lord, He is my safe place and my tower of strength: he is my God, in whom is my hope.

他必救你脱离捕鸟人的网罗，和毒害的瘟疫。
He will take you out of the bird-net, and keep you safe from wasting disease.

他必用自己的翎毛遮蔽你。你要投靠在他的翅膀底下。他的诚实，是大小的盾牌。
You will be covered by his feathers; under his wings you will be safe: his good faith will be your salvation.

你必不怕黑夜的惊骇，或是白日飞的箭。
You will have no fear of the evil things of the night, or of the arrow in flight by day,

也不怕黑夜行的瘟疫，或是午间灭人的毒病。
Or of the disease which takes men in the dark, or of the destruction which makes waste when the sun is high.

虽有千人仆倒在你旁边，万人仆倒在你右边，这灾却不得临近你。
You will see a thousand falling by your side, and ten thousand at your right hand; but it will not come near you.

你惟亲眼观看，见恶人遭报。
Only with your eyes will you see the reward of the evil-doers.

耶和华是我的避难所。你已将至高者当你的居所。
Because you have said, I am in the hands of the Lord, the Most High is my safe resting-place;

祸患必不临到你，灾害也不挨近你的帐棚。
No evil will come on you, and no disease will come near your tent.

因他要为你吩咐他的使者，在你行的一切道路上保护你。
For he will give you into the care of his angels to keep you wherever you go.

他们要用手托着你，免得你的脚碰在石头上。
In their hands they will keep you up, so that your foot may not be crushed against a stone.

你要踹在狮子和虺蛇的身上，践踏少壮狮子和大蛇。
You will put your foot on the lion and the snake; the young lion and the great snake will be crushed under your feet.

神说，因为他专心爱我，我就要搭救他。因为他知道我的名，我要把他安置在高处。
Because he has given me his love, I will take him out of danger: I will put him in a place of honour, because he has kept my name in his heart.

他若求告我，我就应允他。他在急难中，我要与他同在。我要搭救他，使他尊贵。
When his cry comes up to me, I will give him an answer: I will be with him in trouble; I will make him free from danger and give him honour.

我要使他足享长寿，将我的救恩显明给他。
With long life will he be rewarded; and I will let him see my salvation.

（安息日的诗歌。）称谢耶和华，歌颂你至高者的名。
<A Psalm. A Song for the Sabbath.> It is a good thing to give praise to the Lord, and to make melody to your name, O Most High;

用十弦的乐器和瑟，用琴弹幽雅的声音，早晨传扬你的慈爱，每夜传扬你的信实，这本为美事。
To make clear your mercy in the morning, and your unchanging faith every night;


On a ten-corded instrument, and on an instrument of music with a quiet sound.

因你耶和华借着你的作为，叫我高兴。我要因你手的工作欢呼。
For you, O Lord, have made me glad through your work; I will have joy in the works of your hands.

耶和华阿，你的工作何其大，你的心思极其深。
O Lord, how great are your works! and your thoughts are very deep.

畜类人不晓得，愚顽人也不明白。
A man without sense has no knowledge of this; and a foolish man may not take it in.

恶人茂盛如草，一切作孽之人发旺的时候，正是他们要灭亡，直到永远。
When the sinners come up like the grass, and all the workers of evil do well for themselves, it is so that their end may be eternal destruction.

惟你耶和华是至高，直到永远。
But you, O Lord, are on high for ever.

耶和华阿，你的仇敌都要灭亡，一切作孽的也要离散。
For see! your haters, O Lord, will be put to death; all the workers of evil will be put to flight;

你却高举了我的角，如野牛的角。我是被新油膏了的。
But my horn is lifted up like the horn of the ox: the best oil is flowing on my head.

我眼睛看见仇敌遭报，我耳朵听见那些起来攻击我的恶人受罚。
My eyes have seen trouble come on my haters; my ears have news of the fate of the evil-doers who have come up against me.

义人要发旺如棕树，生长如利巴嫩的香柏树。
The good man will be like a tall tree in his strength; his growth will be as the wide-stretching trees of Lebanon.

他们栽于耶和华的殿中，发旺在我们神的院里。
Those who are planted in the house of the Lord will come up tall and strong in his gardens.

他们年老的时候，仍要结果子。要满了汁浆而常发青。
They will give fruit even when they are old; they will be fertile and full of growth;

好显明耶和华是正直的，他是我的磐石，在他毫无不义。
For a sign that the Lord is upright; he is my Rock, there is no deceit in him.

耶和华作王。他以威严为衣穿上。耶和华以能力为衣，以能力束腰。世界就坚定，不得动摇。
The Lord is King; he is clothed with glory; the Lord is clothed with strength; power is the cord of his robe; the world is fixed, so that it may not be moved.

你的宝座从太初立定。你从亘古就有。
The seat of your power has been from the past; you are eternal.

耶和华阿，大水扬起，大水发声，波浪澎湃。
The rivers send up, O Lord, the rivers send up their voices; they send them up with a loud cry.

耶和华在高处大有能力，胜过诸水的响声，洋海的大浪。
The Lord in heaven is stronger than the noise of great waters, yes, he is stronger than the great waves of the sea.

耶和华阿，你的法度最的确。你的殿永称为圣，是合宜的。
Your witness is most certain; it is right for your house to be holy, O Lord, for ever.

耶和华阿，你是伸冤的神。伸冤的神阿，求你发出光来。
O God, in whose hands is punishment, O God of punishment, let your shining face be seen.

审判世界的主阿，求你挺身而立，使骄傲人受应得的报应。
Be lifted up, O judge of the earth; let their reward come to the men of pride.

耶和华阿，恶人夸胜要到几时呢？要到几时呢？
How long will sinners, O Lord, how long will sinners have joy over us?

他们絮絮叨叨，说傲慢的话。一切作孽的人，都自己夸张。
Words of pride come from their lips; all the workers of evil say great things of themselves.

耶和华阿，他们强压你的百姓，苦害你的产业。
Your people are crushed by them, O Lord, your heritage is troubled,

他们杀死寡妇和寄居的，又杀害孤儿。
They put to death the widow and the guest, they take the lives of children who have no father;

他们说，耶和华必不看见，雅各的神必不思念。
And they say, Jah will not see it, the God of Jacob will not give thought to it.

你们民间的畜类人当思想。你们愚顽人，到几时才有智慧呢？
Give your mind to my words, you who are without wisdom among the people; you foolish men, when will you be wise?

造耳朵的，难道自己不听见吗？造眼睛的，难道自己不看见吗？
Has he by whom your ears were planted no hearing? or is he blind by whom your eyes were formed?

管教列邦的，就是叫人得知识的，难道自己不惩治人吗？
He who is the judge of the nations, will he not give men the reward of their acts, even he who gives knowledge to man?

耶和华知道人的意念是虚妄的。
The Lord has knowledge of the thoughts of man, for they are only a breath.

耶和华阿，你所管教，用律法所教训的人，是有福的。
Happy is the man who is guided by you, O Jah, and to whom you give teaching out of your law;

你使他在遭难的日子，得享平安。惟有恶人陷在所挖的坑中。
So that you may give him rest from the days of evil, till a hole is made ready for the destruction of the sinners.

因为耶和华必不丢弃他的百姓，也不离弃他的产业。
The Lord will not give up his people, or take away his support from his heritage;

审判要转向公义。心里正直的，必都随从。
But decisions will again be made in righteousness; and they will be kept by all whose hearts are true.

谁肯为我起来攻击作恶的。谁肯为我站起抵挡作孽的。
Who will give me help against the sinners? and who will be my support against the workers of evil?

若不是耶和华帮助我，我就住在寂静之中了。
If the Lord had not been my helper, my soul would quickly have gone down into death.

我正说我失了脚，耶和华阿，那时你的慈爱扶助我。
If I say, My foot is slipping; your mercy, O Lord, is my support.

我心里多忧多疑，你安慰我，就使我欢乐。
Among all my troubled thoughts, your comforts are the delight of my soul.

那借着律例架弄残害，在位上行奸恶的，岂能与你相交吗？
What part with you has the seat of sin, which makes evil into a law?

他们大家聚集攻击义人，将无辜的人定为死罪。
They are banded together against the soul of the upright, to give decisions against those who have done no wrong.

但耶和华向来作了我的高台。我的神作了我投靠的磐石。
But the Lord is my safe resting-place; my God is the Rock where I am safe.

他叫他们的罪孽归到他们身上。他们正在行恶之中，他要剪除他们。耶和华我们的神要把他们剪除。
And he has made their evil designs come back on themselves, cutting them off in their sin; the Lord our God will put an end to them.

来阿，我们要向耶和华歌唱，向拯救我们的磐石欢呼。
O come, let us make songs to the Lord; sending up glad voices to the Rock of our salvation.

我们要来感谢他，用诗歌向他欢呼。
Let us come before his face with praises; and make melody with holy songs.

因耶和华为大神，为大王，超乎万神之上。
For the Lord is a great God, and a great King over all gods.

地的深处在他手中。山的高峰也属他。
The deep places of the earth are in his hand; and the tops of the mountains are his.

海洋属他。是他造的。旱地也是他手造成的。
The sea is his, and he made it; and the dry land was formed by his hands.

来阿，我们要屈身敬拜，在造我们的耶和华面前跪下。
O come, let us give worship, falling down on our knees before the Lord our Maker.

因为他是我们的神。我们是他草场的羊，是他手下的民。惟愿你们今天听他的话。
For he is our God; and we are the people to whom he gives food, and the sheep of his flock. Today, if you would only give ear to his voice!

你们不可硬着心，像当日在米利巴，就是在旷野的玛撒。
Let not your hearts be hard, as at Meribah, as in the day of Massah in the waste land;

那时你们的祖宗试我探我，并且观看我的作为。
When your fathers put me to the test and saw my power and my work.

四十年之久，我厌烦那世代，说，这是心里迷糊的百姓，竟不晓得我的作为。
For forty years I was angry with this generation, and said, They are a people whose hearts are turned away from me, for they have no knowledge of my ways;

所以我在怒中起誓，说，他们断不可进入我的安息。
And I made an oath in my wrath, that they might not come into my place of rest.

你们要向耶和华唱新歌。全地都要向耶和华歌唱。
O make a new song to the Lord; let all the earth make melody to the Lord.

要向耶和华歌唱，称颂他的名，天天传扬他的救恩。
Make songs to the Lord, blessing his name; give the good news of his salvation day by day.

在列邦中述说他的荣耀，在万民中述说他的奇事。
Make clear his glory to the nations, and his wonders to all the peoples.

因耶和华为大，当受极大的赞美。他在万神之上当受敬畏。
For the Lord is great, and greatly to be praised; he is more to be feared than all other gods.

外邦的神都属虚无。惟独耶和华创造诸天。
For all the gods of the nations are false gods; but the Lord made the heavens.

有尊荣和威严在他面前。有能力与华美在他圣所。
Honour and glory are before him: strong and fair is his holy place.

民中的万族阿，你们要将荣耀能力归给耶和华，都归给耶和华。
Give to the Lord, O you families of the peoples, give to the Lord glory and strength.

要将耶和华的名所当得的荣耀归给他，拿供物来进入他的院宇。
Give to the Lord the glory of his name; take with you an offering and come into his house.

当以圣洁的妆饰（的或作为），敬拜耶和华。全地要在他面前战抖。
O give worship to the Lord in holy robes; be in fear before him, all the earth.

人在列邦中要说，耶和华作王，世界就坚定，不得动摇。他要按公正审判众民。
Say among the nations, The Lord is King; yes, the world is ordered so that it may not be moved; he will be an upright judge of the peoples.

愿天欢喜，愿地快乐。愿海和其中所充满的澎湃。
Let the heavens have joy and the earth be glad; let the sea be thundering with all its waters;

愿田和其中所有的都欢乐。那时林中的树木，都要在耶和华面前欢呼。
Let the field be glad, and everything which is in it; yes, let all the trees of the wood be sounding with joy,

因为他来了。他来要审判全地。他要按公义审判世界，按他的信实审判万民。
Before the Lord, for he is come; he is come to be the judge of the earth; the earth will be judged in righteousness, and the peoples with unchanging faith.

耶和华作王。愿地快乐，愿众海岛欢喜。
The Lord is King, let the earth have joy; let all the sea-lands be glad.

密云和幽暗，在他的四围。公义和公平，是他宝座的根基。
Dark clouds are round him; his kingdom is based on righteousness and right judging.

有烈火在他前头行，烧灭他四围的敌人。
Fire goes before him, burning up all those who are against him round about.

他的闪电光照世界。大地看见便震动。
His bright flames give light to the world; the earth saw it with fear.

诸山见耶和华的面，就是全地之主的面，便消化如蜡。
The mountains became like wax at the coming of the Lord, at the coming of the Lord of all the earth.

诸天表明他的公义，万民看见他的荣耀。
The heavens gave out the news of his righteousness, and all the people saw his glory.

愿一切事奉雕刻的偶像，靠虚无之神自夸的，都蒙羞愧。万神哪，你们都当拜他。
Shamed be all those who give worship to images, and take pride in false gods; give him worship, all you gods.

耶和华阿，锡安听见你的判断，就欢喜，犹大的城邑（原文作女子），也都快乐。
Zion gave ear and was glad; and the daughters of Judah were full of joy, because of your decisions, O Lord.

因为你耶和华至高超乎全地。你被尊崇，远超万神之上。
For you, Lord, are most high over the earth; you are lifted up over all other gods.

你们爱耶和华的，都当恨恶罪恶。他保护圣民的性命，搭救他们脱离恶人的手。
You who are lovers of the Lord, be haters of evil; he keeps the souls of his saints; he takes them out of the hand of sinners.

散布亮光，是为义人。预备喜乐，是为正直人。
Light is shining on the lovers of righteousness, and for the upright in heart there is joy.

你们义人当靠耶和华欢喜，称谢他可记念的圣名。
Be glad in the Lord, you upright men; praising the memory of his holy name.

（一篇诗。）你们要向耶和华唱新歌。因为他行过奇妙的事。他的右手和圣臂，施行救恩。
<A Psalm.> O make a new song to the Lord, because he has done works of wonder; with his right hand, and with his holy arm, he has overcome.

耶和华发明了他的救恩，在列邦人眼前显出公义。
The Lord has given to all the knowledge of his salvation; he has made clear his righteousness in the eyes of the nations.

记念他向以色列家所发的慈爱，所凭的信实。地的四极，都看见我们神的救恩。
He has kept in mind his mercy and his unchanging faith to the house of Israel; all the ends of the earth have seen the salvation of our God.

全地都要向耶和华欢乐。要发起大声欢呼歌颂。
Let all the earth send out a glad cry to the Lord; sounding with a loud voice, and praising him with songs of joy.

要用琴歌颂耶和华，用琴和诗歌的声音歌颂他。
Make melody to the Lord with instruments of music; with a corded instrument and the voice of song.

用号和角声，在大君王耶和华面前欢呼。
With wind instruments and the sound of the horn, make a glad cry before the Lord, the King.

愿海和其中所充满的澎湃。世界和住在其间的，也要发声。
Let the sea be thundering, with all its waters; the world, and all who are living in it;

愿大水拍手。愿诸山在耶和华面前一同欢呼。
Let the streams make sounds of joy with their hands; let the mountains be glad together,

因为他来，要审判遍地。他要按公义审判世界，按公正审判万民。
Before the Lord, for he has come as judge of the earth; judging the world in righteousness, and giving true decisions for the peoples.

耶和华作王，万民当战抖。他坐在二基路伯上，地当动摇。
The Lord is King; let the peoples be in fear: his seat is on the winged ones; let the earth be moved.

耶和华在锡安为大。他超乎万民之上。
The Lord is great in Zion; he is high over all the nations.

他们当称赞他大而可畏的名。他本为圣。
Let them give praise to your name, for it is great and to be feared; holy is he.

王有能力喜爱公平，坚立公正，在雅各中施行公平和公义。
The king's power is used for righteousness; you give true decisions, judging rightly in the land of Jacob.

你们当尊崇耶和华我们的神，在他脚凳前下拜。他本为圣。
Give high honour to the Lord our God, worshipping at his feet; holy is he.

在他的祭司中有摩西和亚伦，在求告他名的人中有撒母耳，他们求告耶和华，他就应允他们。
Moses and Aaron among his priests, and Samuel among those who gave honour to his name; they made prayers to the Lord, and he gave answers to them.

他在云柱中对他们说话。他们遵守他的法度，和他所赐给他们的律例。
His voice came to them from the pillar of cloud; they kept his witness, and the law which he gave them.

耶和华我们的神阿，你应允他们。你是赦免他们的神，却按他们所行的报应他们。
You gave them an answer, O Lord our God; you took away their sin, though you gave them punishment for their wrongdoing.

你们要尊崇耶和华我们的神，在他的圣山下拜。因为耶和华我们的神本为圣。
Give high honour to the Lord our God, worshipping with your faces turned to his holy hill; for the Lord our God is holy.

（称谢诗。）普天下当向耶和华欢呼。
<A Psalm of Praise.> Make a glad sound to the Lord, all the earth.

你们当乐意事奉耶和华。当来向他歌唱。
Give worship to the Lord with joy; come before him with a song.

你们当晓得耶和华是神。我们是他造的，也是属他的。我们是他的民，也是他草场的羊。
Be certain that the Lord is God; it is he who has made us, and we are his; we are his people, and the sheep to whom he gives food.

当称谢进入他的门，当赞美进入他的院。当感谢他，称颂他的名。
Come into his doors with joy, and into his house with praise; give him honour, blessing his name.

因为耶和华本为善，他的慈爱，存到永远，他的信实，直到万代。
For the Lord is good, and his mercy is never-ending; his faith is unchanging through all generations.

（大卫的诗。）我要歌唱慈爱和公平。耶和华阿，我要向你歌颂。
<A Psalm. Of David.> I will make a song of mercy and righteousness; to you, O Lord, will I make melody.

我要用智慧行完全的道。你几时到我这里来呢？我要存完全的心，行在我家中。
I will do wisely in the way of righteousness: O when will you come to me? I will be walking in my house with a true heart.

邪僻的事，我都不摆在我眼前。悖逆人所做的事，我甚恨恶，不容沾在我身上。
I will not put any evil thing before my eyes; I am against all turning to one side; I will not have it near me.

弯曲的心思，我必远离。一切的恶人（或作恶事），我不认识。
The false heart I will send away from me: I will not have an evil-doer for a friend.

在暗中谗谤他邻居的，我必将他灭绝。眼目高傲，心里骄纵的，我必不容他。
I will put to death anyone who says evil of his neighbour secretly; the man with a high look and a heart of pride is disgusting to me.

我眼要看国中的诚实人，叫他们与我同住。行为完全的，他要伺候我。
My eyes will be on those of good faith in the land, so that they may be living in my house; he who is walking in the right way will be my servant.

行诡诈的，必不得住在我家里。说谎话的，必不得立在我眼前。
The worker of deceit will not come into my house; the false man will have no place before my eyes.

我每日早晨，要灭绝国中所有的恶人。好把一切作孽的，从耶和华的城里剪除。
Morning by morning will I put to death all the sinners in the land, so that all evil-doers may be cut off from Jerusalem.

（困苦人发昏的时候，在耶和华面前吐露苦情的祷告。）耶和华阿，求你听我的祷告，容我的呼求达到你面前。
<A Prayer of the man who is in trouble, when he is overcome, and puts his grief before the Lord.> Give ear to my prayer, O Lord, and let my cry come to you.

我在急难的日子，求你向我侧耳，不要向我掩面。我呼求的日子，求你快快应允我。
Let not your face be veiled from me in the day of my trouble; give ear to me, and let my cry be answered quickly.

因为，我的年日如烟云消灭，我的骨头，如火把烧着。
My days are wasted like smoke, and my bones are burned up as in a fire.

我的心被伤，如草枯干，甚至我忘记吃饭。
My heart is broken; it has become dry and dead like grass, so that I give no thought to food.

因我唉哼的声音，我的肉紧贴骨头。
Because of the voice of my sorrow, my flesh is wasted to the bone.

我如同旷野的鹈鹕。我好像荒场的？？鸟。
I am like a bird living by itself in the waste places; like the night-bird in a waste of sand.

我儆醒不睡。我像房顶上孤单的麻雀。
I keep watch like a bird by itself on the house-top.

我的仇敌终日辱骂我。向我猖狂的人指着我赌咒。
My haters say evil of me all day; those who are violent against me make use of my name as a curse.

我吃过炉灰，如同吃饭。我所喝的与眼泪搀杂。
I have had dust for bread and my drink has been mixed with weeping:

这都因你的恼恨和忿怒。你把我拾起来，又把我摔下去。
Because of your passion and your wrath, for I have been lifted up and then made low by you.

我的年日，如日影偏斜。我也如草枯干。
My days are like a shade which is stretched out; I am dry like the grass.

惟你耶和华必存到永远。你可记念的名，也存到万代。
But you, O Lord, are eternal; and your name will never come to an end.

你必起来怜恤锡安，因现在是可怜她的时候。日期已经到了。
You will again get up and have mercy on Zion: for the time has come for her to be comforted.

你的仆人原来喜悦她的石头，可怜她的尘土。
For your servants take pleasure in her stones, looking with love on her dust.

列国要敬畏耶和华的名。世上诸王都敬畏你的荣耀。
So the nations will give honour to the name of the Lord, and all the kings of the earth will be in fear of his glory:

因为耶和华建造了锡安，在他荣耀里显现。
When the Lord has put up the walls of Zion, and has been been in his glory;

他垂听穷人的祷告，并不藐视他们的祈求。
When he has given ear to the prayer of the poor, and has not put his request on one side.

这必为后代的人记下。将来受造的民，要赞美耶和华。
This will be put in writing for the coming generation, and the people of the future will give praise to the Lord.

因为他从至高的圣所垂看。耶和华从天向地观察。
For from his holy place the Lord has seen, looking down on the earth from heaven;

要垂听被囚之人的叹息。要释放将要死的人。
Hearing the cry of the prisoner, making free those for whom death is ordered;

使人在锡安传扬耶和华的名，在耶路撒冷传扬赞美他的话。
So that they may give out the name of the Lord in Zion, and his praise in Jerusalem;

就是在万民和列国聚会事奉耶和华的时候。
When the peoples are come together, and the kingdoms, to give worship to the Lord.

他使我的力量，中道衰弱，使我的年日短少。
He has taken my strength from me in the way; he has made short my days.

我说，我的神阿，不要使我中年去世。你的年数世世无穷。
I will say, O my God, take me not away before my time; your years go on through all generations:

你起初立了地的根基。天也是你手所造的。
In the past you put the earth on its base, and the heavens are the work of your hands.

天地都要灭没，你却要长存。天地都要如外衣渐渐旧了。你要将天地如里衣更换，天地就改变了。
They will come to an end, but you will still go on; they all will become old like a coat, and like a robe they will be changed:

惟有你永不改变。你的年数，没有穷尽。
But you are the unchanging One, and your years will have no end.

你仆人的子孙要长存。他们的后裔，要坚立在你面前。
The children of your servants will have a safe resting-place, and their seed will be ever before you.

（大卫的诗。）我的心哪，你要称颂耶和华。凡在我里面的，也要称颂他的圣名。
<Of David.> Give praise to the Lord, O my soul; let everything in me give praise to his holy name.

我的心哪，你要称颂耶和华，不可忘记他的一切恩惠。
Give praise to the Lord, O my soul; let not all his blessings go from your memory.

他赦免你的一切罪孽，医治你的一切疾病。
He has forgiveness for all your sins; he takes away all your diseases;

他救赎你的命脱离死亡，以仁爱和慈悲为你的冠冕。
He keeps back your life from destruction, crowning you with mercy and grace.

他用美物，使你所愿的得以知足，以致你如鹰返老还童。
He makes your mouth full of good things, so that your strength is made new again like the eagle's.

耶和华施行公义，为一切受屈的人伸冤。
The Lord gives decisions in righteousness for all who are in trouble.

他使摩西知道他的法则，叫以色列人晓得他的作为。
He gave knowledge of his way to Moses, and made his acts clear to the children of Israel.

耶和华有怜悯，有恩典，不轻易发怒，且有丰盛的慈爱。
The Lord is kind and full of pity, not quickly made angry, but ever ready to have mercy.

他不长久责备，也不永远怀怒。
His feeling will no longer be bitter; he will not keep his wrath for ever.

他没有按我们的罪过待我们，也没有照我们的罪孽报应我们。
He has not given us the punishment for our sins, or the reward of our wrongdoing.

天离地何等的高，他的慈爱向敬畏他的人，也是何等的大。
For as the heaven is high over the earth, so great is his mercy to his worshippers.

东离西有多远，他叫我们的过犯，离我们也有多远。
As far as the east is from the west, so far has he put our sins from us.

父亲怎样怜恤他的儿女，耶和华也怎样怜恤敬畏他的人。
As a father has pity on his children, so the Lord has pity on his worshippers.

因为他知道我们的本体，思念我们不过是尘土。
For he has knowledge of our feeble frame; he sees that we are only dust.

至于世人，他的年日如草一样。他发旺如野地的花。
As for man, his days are as grass: his beautiful growth is like the flower of the field.

经风一吹，便归无有。他的原处，也不再认识他。
The wind goes over it and it is gone; and its place sees it no longer.

但耶和华的慈爱，归于敬畏他的人，从亘古到永远。他的公义，也归于子子孙孙。
But the mercy of the Lord is eternal for his worshippers, and their children's children will see his righteousness;

就是那些遵守他的约，记念他的训词而遵行的人。
If they keep his agreement, and have his laws in mind to do them.

耶和华在天上立定宝座。他的权柄（原文作国）统管万有。
The Lord has made ready his high seat in the heavens; his kingdom is ruling over all.

听从他命令成全他旨意有大能的天使，都要称颂耶和华。
Give praise to the Lord, you his angels, who are great in strength, doing his orders, and waiting for his voice.

你们作他的诸军作他的仆役行他所喜悦的，都要称颂耶和华。
Give praise to the Lord, all you his armies; and you his servants who do his pleasure.

你们一切被他造的，在他所治理的各处，都要称颂耶和华。我的心哪，你要称颂耶和华。
Give praise to the Lord, all his works, in all places under his rule: give praise to the Lord, O my soul.

我的心哪，你要称颂耶和华。耶和华我的神阿，你为至大。你以尊荣威严为衣服。
Give praise to the Lord, O my soul. O Lord my God, you are very great; you are robed with honour and power.

披上亮光，如披外袍，铺张穹苍，如铺幔子。
You are clothed with light as with a robe; stretching out the heavens like a curtain:

在水中立楼阁的栋梁，用云彩为车辇，借着风的翅膀而行。
The arch of your house is based on the waters; you make the clouds your carriage; you go on the wings of the wind:

以风为使者，以火焰为仆役。
He makes winds his angels, and flames of fire his servants.

将地立在根基上，使地永不动摇。
He has made the earth strong on its bases, so that it may not be moved for ever and ever;

你用深水遮盖地面，犹如衣裳。诸水高过山岭。
Covering it with the sea as with a robe: the waters were high over the mountains;

你的斥责一发，水便奔逃。你的雷声一发，水便奔流。
At the voice of your word they went in flight; at the sound of your thunder they went away in fear;

（诸山升上，诸谷沉下（或作随山上翻，随谷下流）），归你为它所安定之地
The mountains came up and the valleys went down into the place which you had made ready for them.

你定了界限，使水不能过去，不再转回遮盖地面。
You made a limit over which they might not go, so that the earth would never again be covered by them.

耶和华使泉源涌在山谷，流在山间。
You sent the springs into the valleys; they are flowing between the hills.

使野地的走兽有水喝，野驴得解其渴。
They give drink to every beast of the field; the mountain asses come to them for water.

天上的飞鸟在水旁住宿，在树枝上啼叫。
The birds of the air have their resting-places by them, and make their song among the branches.

他从楼阁中浇灌山岭。因他作为的功效，地就丰足。
He sends down rain from his store-houses on the hills: the earth is full of the fruit of his works.

他使草生长，给六畜吃。使菜蔬发长，供给人用。使人从地里能得食物。
He makes the grass come up for the cattle, and plants for the use of man; so that bread may come out of the earth;

又得酒能悦人心，得油能润人面，得粮能养人心。
And wine to make glad the heart of man, and oil to make his face shining, and bread giving strength to his heart.

佳美的树木，就是利巴嫩的香柏树，是耶和华所栽种的，都满了汁浆。
The trees of the Lord are full of growth, the cedars of Lebanon of his planting;

雀鸟在其上搭窝。至于鹤，松树是它的房屋。
Where the birds have their resting-places; as for the stork, the tall trees are her house.

高山为野山羊的住所。岩石为沙番的藏处。
The high hills are a safe place for the mountain goats, and the rocks for the small beasts.

你安置月亮为定节令。日头自知沉落。
He made the moon for a sign of the divisions of the year; teaching the sun the time of its going down.

你造黑暗为夜，林中的百兽就都爬出来。
When you make it dark, it is night, when all the beasts of the woods come quietly out of their secret places.

少壮狮子吼叫，要抓食，向神寻求食物。
The young lions go thundering after their food; searching for their meat from God.

日头一出，兽便躲避，卧在洞里。
The sun comes up, and they come together, and go back to their secret places to take their rest.

人出去做工，劳碌直到晚上。
Man goes out to his work, and to his business, till the evening.

耶和华阿，你所造的何其多，都是你用智慧造成的。遍地满了你的丰富。
O Lord, how great is the number of your works! in wisdom you have made them all; the earth is full of the things you have made.

那里有海，又大又广。其中有无数的动物。大小活物都有。
There is the great, wide sea, where there are living things, great and small, more than may be numbered.

那里有船行走。有你所造的鳄鱼游泳在其中。
There go the ships; there is that great beast, which you have made as a plaything.

这都仰望你按时给它食物。
All of them are waiting for you, to give them their food in its time.

你给它们，它们便拾起来；你张手，它们饱得美食。
They take what you give them; they are full of the good things which come from your open hand.

你掩面，它们便惊惶。你收回它们的气，它们就死亡，归于尘土。
If your face is veiled, they are troubled; when you take away their breath, they come to an end, and go back to the dust.

你发出你的灵，它们便受造。你使地面更换为新。
If you send out your spirit, they are given life; you make new the face of the earth.

愿耶和华的荣耀存到永远。愿耶和华喜悦自己所造的。
Let the glory of the Lord be for ever; let the Lord have joy in his works:

他看地，地便震动。他摸山，山就冒烟。
At whose look the earth is shaking; at whose touch the mountains send out smoke.

我要一生向耶和华唱诗。我还活的时候，要向我神歌颂。
I will make songs to the Lord all my life; I will make melody to my God while I have my being.

愿他以我的默念为甘甜。我要因耶和华欢喜。
Let my thoughts be sweet to him: I will be glad in the Lord.

愿罪人从世上消灭。愿恶人归于无有。我的心哪，要称颂耶和华。你们要赞美耶和华。（原文作哈利路亚下同）
Let sinners be cut off from the earth, and let all evil-doers come to an end. Give praise to the Lord, O my soul. Give praise to the Lord.

你们要称谢耶和华，求告他的名，在万民中传扬他的作为。
O give praise to the Lord; give honour to his name, talking of his doings among the peoples.

要向他唱诗歌颂，谈论他一切奇妙的作为。
Let your voice be sounding in songs and melody; let all your thoughts be of the wonder of his works.

要以他的圣名夸耀。寻求耶和华的人，心中应当欢喜。
Have glory in his holy name; let the hearts of those who are searching after the Lord be glad.

要寻求耶和华与他的能力，时常寻求他的面。
Let your search be for the Lord and for his strength; let your hearts ever be turned to him.

他仆人亚伯拉罕的后裔，他所拣选雅各的子孙哪，你们要记念他奇妙的作为和他的奇事，并他口中的判语。
Keep in mind the great works which he has done; his wonders, and the decisions of his mouth;


O you seed of Abraham, his servant, you children of Jacob, his loved ones.

他是耶和华我们的神。全地都有他的判断。
He is the Lord our God: he is judge of all the earth.

他记念他的约，直到永远，他所吩咐的话，直到千代。
He has kept his agreement in mind for ever, the word which he gave for a thousand generations;

就是与亚伯拉罕所立的约，向以撒所起的誓。
The agreement which he made with Abraham, and his oath to Isaac;

他又将这约向雅各定为律例，向以色列定为永远的约，
And he gave it to Jacob for a law, and to Israel for an eternal agreement;

说，我必将迦南地赐给你，作你产业的分。
Saying, To you will I give the land of Canaan, the measured line of your heritage:

当时，他们人丁有限，数目稀少，并且在那地为寄居的。
When they were still small in number, and strange in the land;

他们从这邦游到那邦，从这国行到那国。
When they went about from one nation to another, and from one kingdom to another people.

他不容什么人欺负他们，为他们的缘故责备君王，
He would not let anyone do them wrong; he even kept back kings because of them,

说，不可难为我受膏的人，也不可恶待我的先知。
Saying, Put not your hand on those who have been marked with my holy oil, and do my prophets no wrong.

他命饥荒降在那地上，将所倚靠的粮食全行断绝。
And he took away all food from the land, so that the people were without bread.

在他们以先打发一个人去。约瑟被卖为奴仆。
He sent a man before them, even Joseph, who was given as a servant for a price:

人用脚镣伤他的脚，他被铁链捆拘。
His feet were fixed in chains; his neck was put in iron bands;

耶和华的话试炼他，直等到他所说的应验了。
Till the time when his word came true; he was tested by the word of the Lord.

王打发人把他解开，就是治理众民的，把他释放。
The king sent men to take off his chains; even the ruler of the people, who let him go free.

立他作王家之主，掌管他一切所有的。
He made him lord of his house, and ruler over everything he had;

使他随意捆绑他的臣宰，将智慧教导他的长老。
To give his chiefs teaching at his pleasure, and so that his law-givers might get wisdom from him.

以色列也到了埃及，雅各在含地寄居。
Then Israel came into Egypt, and Jacob was living in the land of Ham.

耶和华使他的百姓生养众多，使他们比敌人强盛。
And his people were greatly increased, and became stronger than those who were against them.

使敌人的心转去恨他的百姓，并用诡计待他的仆人。
Their hearts were turned to hate against his people, so that they made secret designs against them.

他打发他的仆人摩西，和他所拣选的亚伦。
He sent Moses, his servant, and Aaron, the man of his selection.

在敌人中间显他的神迹，在含地显他的奇事。
He let his signs be seen among the people, and his wonders in the land of Ham.

他命黑暗，就有黑暗。没有违背他话的。
He sent black night and made it dark; and they did not go against his word.

他叫埃及的水变为血，叫他们的鱼死了。
At his word their waters were turned to blood, and he sent death on all their fish.

在他们的地上，以及王宫的内室，青蛙多多滋生。
Their land was full of frogs, even in the rooms of the king.

他说一声，苍蝇就成群而来，并有虱子进入他们四境。
He gave the word, and there came the dog-fly, and insects over all the land.

他给他们降下冰雹为雨，在他们的地上降下火焰。
He gave them ice for rain, and flaming fire in their land.

他也击打他们的葡萄树和无花果树，毁坏他们境内的树木。
He gave their vines and their fig-trees to destruction, and the trees of their land were broken down.

他说一声，就有蝗虫蚂蚱上来，不计其数，
At his word the locusts came, and young locusts more than might be numbered,

吃尽了他们地上各样的菜蔬，和田地的出产。
And put an end to all the plants of their land, taking all the fruit of the earth for food.

他又击杀他们国内一切的长子，就是他们强壮时头生的。
He put to death the first child of every family in the land, the first-fruits of their strength.

他领自己的百姓带银子金子出来。他支派中没有一个软弱的。
He took his people out with silver and gold: there was not one feeble person among them.

他们出来的时候，埃及人便欢喜。原来埃及人惧怕他们。
Egypt was glad when they went; for the fear of them had come down on them.

他铺张云彩当遮盖，夜间使火光照。
A cloud was stretched over them for a cover; and he sent fire to give light in the night.

他们一求，他就使鹌鹑飞来，并用天上的粮食，叫他们饱足。
At the people's request he sent birds, and gave them the bread of heaven for food.

他打开磐石，水就涌出。在干旱之处，水流成河。
His hand made the rock open, and the waters came streaming out; they went down through the dry places like a river.

这都因他记念他的圣言，和他的仆人亚伯拉罕。
For he kept in mind his holy word, and Abraham, his servant.

他带领百姓欢乐而出，带领选民欢呼前往。
And he took his people out with joy, the men of his selection with glad cries:

他将列国的地赐给他们，他们便承受众民劳碌得来的。
And gave them the lands of the nations; and they took the work of the peoples for a heritage;

好使他们遵他的律例，守他的律法。你们要赞美耶和华。
So that they might keep his orders, and be true to his laws. Give praise to the Lord.

你们要赞美耶和华。要称谢耶和华，因他本为善。他的慈爱永远长存。
Let the Lord be praised. O give praise to the Lord, for he is good: for his mercy is unchanging for ever.

谁能传说耶和华的大能，谁能表明他一切的美德。
Who is able to give an account of the great acts of the Lord, or to make clear all his praise?

凡遵守公平，常行公义的，这人便为有福。
Happy are they whose decisions are upright, and he who does righteousness at all times.

耶和华阿，你用恩惠待你的百姓，求你也用这恩惠记念我，开你的救恩眷顾我，
Keep me in mind, O Lord, when you are good to your people; O let your salvation come to me;

使我见你选民的福，乐你国民的乐，与你的产业一同夸耀。
So that I may see the well-being of the people of your selection, and have a part in the joy of your nation, and take pride in your heritage.

我们与我们的祖宗一同犯罪。我们作了孽，行了恶。
We are sinners like our fathers, we have done wrong, our acts are evil.

我们的祖宗在埃及不明白你的奇事，不记念你丰盛的慈爱，反倒在红海行了悖逆。
Our fathers did not give thought to your wonders in Egypt; they did not keep in memory the great number of your mercies, but gave you cause for wrath at the sea, even at the Red Sea.

然而，他因自己的名拯救他们，为要彰显他的大能。
But he was their saviour because of his name, so that men might see his great power.

并且斥责红海，海便干了；他带领他们经过深处，如同经过旷野。
By his word the Red Sea was made dry: and he took them through the deep waters as through the waste land.

他拯救他们脱离恨他们人的手，从仇敌手中救赎他们。
And he took them safely out of the hands of their haters, and kept them from the attacks of those who were against them.

水淹没他们的敌人，没有一个存留。
And the waters went over their haters; all of them came to an end.

那时，他们才信了他的话，歌唱赞美他。
Then they had faith in his words; they gave him songs of praise.

等不多时，他们就忘了他的作为，不仰望他的指教，
But their memory of his works was short; not waiting to be guided by him,

反倒在旷野大起欲心，在荒地试探神。
They gave way to their evil desires in the waste land, and put God to the test in the dry places.

他将他们所求的赐给他们，却使他们的心灵软弱。
And he gave them their request, but sent a wasting disease into their souls.

他们又在营中嫉妒摩西，和耶和华的圣者亚伦。
They were full of envy against Moses among the tents, and against Aaron, the holy one of the Lord.

地裂开，吞下大坍，掩盖亚比兰一党的人。
The earth opening put an end to Dathan, covering up Abiram and his band.

有火在他们的党中发起，有火焰烧毁了恶人。
And a fire was lighted among their tents; the sinners were burned up by the flames.

他们在何烈山造了牛犊，叩拜铸成的像。
They made a young ox in Horeb, and gave worship to an image of gold.

如此将他们荣耀的主，换为吃草之牛的像。
And their glory was changed into the image of an ox, whose food is grass.

忘了神他们的救主。他曾在埃及行大事。
They had no memory of God their saviour, who had done great things in Egypt;

在含地行奇事，在红海行可畏的事。
Works of wonder in the land of Ham, and things of fear by the Red Sea.

所以，他说要灭绝他们。若非有他所拣选的摩西站在当中（原文作破口），使他的忿怒转消，恐怕他就灭绝他们。
And he was purposing to put an end to them if Moses, his special servant, had not gone up before him, between him and his people, turning back his wrath, to keep them from destruction.

他们又藐视那美地，不信他的话，
They were disgusted with the good land; they had no belief in his word;

在自己帐棚内发怨言，不听耶和华的声音。
Talking against him secretly in their tents, they did not give ear to the voice of the Lord.

所以，他对他们起誓，必叫他们倒在旷野，
So he made an oath against them, to put an end to them in the waste land:

叫他们的后裔倒在列国之中，分散在各地。
That their children might be mixed among the nations, and sent away into other lands.

他们又与巴力毗珥连合，且吃了祭死神（或作人）的物。
And they were joined to Baal-peor, and took part in the offerings to the dead.

他们这样行，惹耶和华发怒，便有瘟疫流行在他们中间。
So they made him angry by their behaviour; and he sent disease on them.

那时，非尼哈站起，刑罚恶人，瘟疫这才止息。
Then Phinehas got up, and made prayer for them; and the disease went no farther.

那就算为他的义，世世代代，直到永远。
And all the generations coming after him kept the memory of his righteousness for ever.

他们在米利巴水又叫耶和华发怒，甚至摩西也受了亏损。
They made God angry again at the waters of Meribah, so that Moses was troubled because of them;

是因他们惹动他的灵，摩西（原文作他）用嘴说了急躁的话。
For they made his spirit bitter, and he said unwise things.

他们不照耶和华所吩咐的灭绝外邦人，
They did not put an end to the peoples, as the Lord had said;

反与他们混杂相合，学习他们的行为，
But they were joined to the nations, learning their works.

事奉他们的偶像，这就成了自己的网罗。
And they gave worship to images; which were a danger to them:

把自己的儿女祭祀鬼魔，
They even made offerings of their sons and their daughters to evil spirits,

流无辜人的血，就是自己儿女的血，把他们祭祀迦南的偶像，那地就被血污秽了。
And gave the blood of their sons and their daughters who had done no wrong, offering them to the images of Canaan; and the land was made unclean with blood.

这样，他们被自己所做的污秽了，在行为上犯了邪淫。
So they became unclean through their works, going after their evil desires.

所以，耶和华的怒气，向他的百姓发作，憎恶他的产业。
Then the wrath of the Lord was burning against his people, and he was angry with his heritage.

将他们交在外邦人的手里；恨他们的人就辖制他们。
And he gave them into the hands of the nations; and they were ruled by their haters.

他们的仇敌也欺压他们，他们就伏在敌人手下。
By them they were crushed, and made low under their hands.

他屡次搭救他们，他们却设谋背逆，因自己的罪孽降为卑下。
Again and again he made them free; but their hearts were turned against his purpose, and they were overcome by their sins.

然而，他听见他们哀告的时候，就眷顾他们的急难。
But when their cry came to his ears, he had pity on their trouble:

为他们记念他的约，照他丰盛的慈爱后悔。
And kept in mind his agreement with them, and in his great mercy gave them forgiveness.

他也使他们在凡掳掠他们的人面前蒙怜恤。
He put pity into the hearts of those who made them prisoners.

耶和华我们的神阿，求你拯救我们，从外邦中招聚我们，我们好称赞你的圣名，以赞美你为夸胜。
Be our saviour, O Lord our God, and let us come back together from among the nations, so that we may give honour to your holy name, and have glory in your praise.

耶和华以色列的神是应当称颂的，从亘古直到永远。愿众民都说，阿们。你们要赞美耶和华。
Praise be to the Lord God of Israel for ever and for ever; and let all the people say, So be it. Give praise to the Lord.

你们要称谢耶和华，因他本为善。他的慈爱，永远长存。
O give praise to the Lord, for he is good: for his mercy is unchanging for ever.

愿耶和华的赎民说这话，就是他从敌人手中所救赎的，
Let those whose cause the Lord has taken up say so, his people whom he has taken out of the hands of their haters;

从各地，从东从西，从南从北，所招聚来的。
Making them come together out of all the lands, from the east and from the west, from the north and from the south.

他们在旷野荒地漂流，寻不见可住的城邑。
They were wandering in the waste places; they saw no way to a resting-place.

又饥又渴，心里发昏。
Their souls became feeble for need of food and drink.

于是，他们在苦难中哀求耶和华，他从他们的祸患中搭救他们。
Then they sent up their cry to the Lord in their sorrow, and he gave them salvation out of all their troubles;

又领他们行走直路，使他们往可居住的城邑。
Guiding them in the right way, so that they might come into the town of their resting-place.

但愿人因耶和华的慈爱和他向人所行的奇事都称赞他。
Let men give praise to the Lord for his mercy, and for the wonders which he does for the children of men!

因他使心里渴慕的人，得以知足，使心里饥饿的人，得饱美物。
He gives its desire to the unresting soul, so that it is full of good things.

那些坐在黑暗中死荫里的人，被困苦和铁链捆锁，
Those who were in the dark, in the black night, in chains of sorrow and iron;

是因他们违背神的话语，藐视至高者的旨意。
Because they went against the words of God, and gave no thought to the laws of the Most High:

所以，他用劳苦治服他们的心。他们仆倒，无人扶助。
So that he made their hearts weighted down with grief; they were falling, and had no helper.

于是，他们在苦难中哀求耶和华，他从他们的祸患中拯救他们。
Then they sent up their cry to the Lord in their sorrow, and he gave them salvation out of all their troubles.

他从黑暗中，和死荫里，领他们出来，折断他们的绑索。
He took them out of the dark and the black night, and all their chains were broken.

但愿人因耶和华的慈爱，和他向人所行的奇事都称赞他。
Let men give praise to the Lord for his mercy, and for the wonders which he does for the children of men!

因为他打破了铜门，砍断了铁闩。
The doors of brass are broken by his arm, and the bands of iron are cut in two.

愚妄人因自己的过犯，和自己的罪孽便受苦楚。
Foolish men, because of their sins, and because of their wrongdoing, are troubled;

他们心里厌恶各样的食物，就临近死门。
They are disgusted by all food, and they come near to the doors of death.

于是，他们在苦难中哀求耶和华，他从他们的祸患中拯救他们。
Then they send up their cry to the Lord in their sorrow, and he gives them salvation out of all their troubles.

他发命医治他们，救他们脱离死亡。
He sent his word and made them well, and kept them safe from the underworld.

但愿人因耶和华的慈爱，和他向人所行的奇事都称赞他。
Let men give praise to the Lord for his mercy, and for the wonders which he does for the children of men!

愿他们以感谢为祭献给他，欢呼述说他的作为。
Let them make offerings of praise, giving news of his works with cries of joy.

在海上坐船，在大水中经理事务的。
Those who go down to the sea in ships, who do business in the great waters;

他们看见耶和华的作为，并他在深水中的奇事。
They see the works of the Lord, and his wonders in the deep.

因他一吩咐，狂风就起来，海中的波浪也扬起。
For at his word comes up the storm-wind, lifting high the waves.

他们上到天空，下到海底，他们的心因患难便消化。
The sailors go up to heaven, and down into the deep; their souls are wasted because of their trouble.

他们摇摇幌幌。东倒西歪，好像醉酒的人。他们的智慧无法可施。
They are turned here and there, rolling like a man who is full of wine; and all their wisdom comes to nothing.

于是，他们在苦难中哀求耶和华，他从他们的祸患中领出他们来。
Then they send up their cry to the Lord in their sorrow, and he gives them salvation out of all their troubles.

他使狂风止息，波浪就平静。
He makes the storm into a calm, so that the waves are at peace.

风息浪静，他们便欢喜。他就引他们到所愿去的海口。
Then they are glad, because the sea is quiet, and he takes them to the harbour of their desire.

但愿人因耶和华的慈爱，和他向人所行的奇事都称赞他。
Let men give praise to the Lord for his mercy, and for the wonders which he does for the children of men!

愿他们在民的会中尊崇他，在长老的位上赞美他。
Let them give glory to him in the meeting of the people, and praise among the chiefs.

他使江河变为旷野，叫水泉变为干渴之地。
He makes rivers into waste places, and springs of water into a dry land;

使肥地变为碱地。这都因其间居民的罪恶。
He makes a fertile country into a salt waste, because of the sins of those who are living there.

他使旷野变为水潭，叫旱地变为水泉。
He makes a waste land into a place of water, and a dry land into water-springs.

他使饥饿的人住在那里，好建造可住的城邑。
And there he gives the poor a resting-place, so that they may make themselves a town;

又种田地，栽葡萄园，得享所出的土产。
And put seed in the fields and make vine-gardens, to give them fruit.

他又赐福给他们，叫他们生养众多。也不叫他们的牲畜减少。
He gives them his blessing so that they are increased greatly, and their cattle do not become less.

他们又因暴虐，患难，愁苦，就减少且卑下。
And when they are made low, and crushed by trouble and sorrow,

他使君王蒙羞被辱，使他们在荒废无路之地漂流。
He puts an end to the pride of kings, and sends them wandering in the waste lands where there is no way.

他却将穷乏人安置在高处，脱离苦难，使他的家属多如羊群。
But he puts the poor man on high from his troubles, and gives him families like a flock.

正直人看见，就欢喜。罪孽之辈，必塞口无言。
The upright see it and are glad: the mouth of the sinner is stopped.

凡有智慧的，必在这些事上留心，也必思想耶和华的慈爱。
Let the wise give thought to these things, and see the mercies of the Lord.

（大卫的诗歌。）神阿，我心坚定。我口（原文作荣耀）要唱诗歌颂。
<A Song. A Psalm. Of David.> O God, my heart is fixed; I will make songs and melody, even with my glory.

琴瑟阿，你们当醒起。我自己要极早醒起。
Give out your sounds, O corded instruments: the dawn will be awaking with my song.

耶和华阿，我要在万民中称谢你，在列邦中歌颂你。
I will give you praise, O Lord, among the peoples; I will make melody to you among the nations.

因为，你的慈爱，大过诸天；你的诚实，达到穹苍。
For your mercy is higher than the heavens: and your unchanging faith than the clouds.

神阿，愿你崇高过于诸天。愿你的荣耀，高过全地。
Be lifted up, O God, higher than the heavens; let your glory be over all the earth.

求你应允我们，用右手拯救我们，好叫你所亲爱的人得救。
Let your right hand be stretched out for salvation, and give me an answer, so that your loved ones may be safe from danger.

神已经指着他的圣洁说（说或作应许我），我要欢乐。我要分开示剑，丈量疏割谷。
This is the word of the holy God: I will be glad; I will make Shechem a heritage, measuring out the valley of Succoth.

基列是我的。玛拿西是我的。以法莲是护卫我头的。犹大是我的杖。
Gilead is mine; Manasseh is mine; Ephraim is the strength of my head; Judah is my law-giver;

摩押是我的沐浴盆。我要向以东抛鞋。我必因胜非利士呼喊。
Moab is my washpot; on Edom is the resting-place of my shoe; over Philistia will I send out a glad cry.

谁能领我进坚固城。谁能引我到以东地。
Who will take me into the strong town? who will be my guide into Edom?

神阿，你不是丢弃了我们吗？神阿，你不和我们的军兵同去吗？
Have you not sent us away from you, O God? and you go not out with our armies.

求你帮助我们攻击敌人，因为人的帮助是枉然的。
Give us help in our trouble; for there is no help in man.

我们倚靠神，才得施展大能，因为践踏我们敌人的就是他。
With God we will do great things; for by him will our haters be crushed underfoot.

（大卫的诗，交与伶长。）我所赞美的神阿，求你不要闭口不言。
<To the chief music-maker. Of David. A Psalm.> God of my praise, let my prayer be answered;

因为恶人的嘴，和诡诈人的口，已经张开攻击我。他们用撒谎的舌头对我说话。
For the mouth of the sinner is open against me in deceit: his tongue has said false things against me.

他们围绕我，说怨恨的话，又无故地攻打我。
Words of hate are round about me; they have made war against me without cause.

他们与我为敌以报我爱。但我专心祈祷。
For my love they give me back hate; but I have given myself to prayer.

他们向我以恶报善，以恨报爱。
They have put on me evil for good; hate in exchange for my love.

愿你派一个恶人辖制他，派一个对头站在他右边。
Put an evil man over him; and let one be placed at his right hand to say evil of him.

他受审判的时候，愿他出来担当罪名。愿他的祈祷反成为罪。
When he is judged, let the decision go against him; and may his prayer become sin.

愿他的年日短少。愿别人得他的职分。
Let his life be short; let another take his position of authority.

愿他的儿女为孤儿，他的妻子为寡妇。
Let his children have no father, and his wife be made a widow.

愿他的儿女漂流讨饭，从他们荒凉之处出来求食。
Let his children be wanderers, looking to others for their food; let them be sent away from the company of their friends.

愿强暴的债主牢笼他一切所有的。愿外人抢他劳碌得来的。
Let his creditor take all his goods; and let others have the profit of his work.

愿无人向他延绵施恩。愿无人可怜他的孤儿。
Let no man have pity on him, or give help to his children when he is dead.

愿他的后人断绝，名字被涂抹，不传于下代。
Let his seed be cut off; in the coming generation let their name go out of memory.

愿他祖宗的罪孽被耶和华记念。愿他母亲的罪过不被涂抹。
Let the Lord keep in mind the wrongdoing of his fathers; and may the sin of his mother have no forgiveness.

愿这些罪常在耶和华面前，使他的名号断绝于世。
Let them be ever before the eyes of the Lord, so that the memory of them may be cut off from the earth.

因为他不想施恩，却逼迫困苦穷乏的，和伤心的人，要把他们治死。
Because he had no mercy, but was cruel to the low and the poor, designing the death of the broken-hearted.

他爱咒骂，咒骂就临到他。他不喜爱福乐，福乐就与他远离。
As he took pleasure in cursing, so let it come on him; and as he had no delight in blessing, let it be far from him.

他拿咒骂当衣服穿上。这咒骂就如水进他里面，像油入他的骨头。
He put on cursing like a robe, and it has come into his body like water, and into his bones like oil.

愿这咒骂当他遮身的衣服，当他常束的腰带。
Let it be to him as a robe which he puts on, let it be like a band which is round him at all times.

这就是我对头，和用恶言议论我的人，从耶和华那里所受的报应。
Let this be the reward given to my haters from the Lord, and to those who say evil of my soul.

主耶和华阿，求你为你的名恩待我。因你的慈爱美好，求你搭救我。
But, O Lord God, give me your help, because of your name; take me out of danger, because your mercy is good.

因为我困苦穷乏，内心受伤。
For I am poor and in need, and my heart is wounded in me.

我如日影渐渐偏斜而去。我如蝗虫被抖出来。
I am gone like the shade when it is stretched out: I am forced out of my place like a locust.

我因禁食，膝骨软弱；我身上的肉也渐渐瘦了。
My knees are feeble for need of food; there is no fat on my bones.

我受他们的羞辱。他们看见我，便摇头。
As for me, they make sport of me; shaking their heads when they see me.

耶和华我的神阿，求你帮助我，照你的慈爱拯救我。
Give me help, O Lord my God; in your mercy be my saviour;

使他们知道这是你的手，是你耶和华所行的事。
So that they may see that it is the work of your hand; that you, Lord, have done it.

任凭他们咒骂。惟愿你赐福。他们几时起来就必蒙羞，你的仆人却要欢喜。
They may give curses but you give blessing; when they come up against me, put them to shame; but let your servant be glad.

愿我的对头，披戴羞辱。愿他们以自己的羞愧为外袍遮身。
Let my haters be clothed with shame, covering themselves with shame as with a robe.

我要用口极力称谢耶和华。我要在众人中间赞美他。
I will give the Lord great praise with my mouth; yes, I will give praise to him among all the people.

因为他必站在穷乏人的右边，要救他脱离审判他灵魂的人。
For he is ever at the right hand of the poor, to take him out of the hands of those who go after his soul.

（大卫的诗。）耶和华对我主说，你坐在我的右边，等我使你仇敌作你的脚凳。
<A Psalm. Of David.> The Lord said to my lord, Be seated at my right hand, till I put all those who are against you under your feet.

耶和华必使你从锡安伸出能力的杖来。你要在你仇敌中掌权。
The Lord will send out the rod of your strength from Zion; be king over your haters.

当你掌权的日子（或作行军的日子），你的民要以圣洁的妆饰为衣（或作以圣洁为妆饰），甘心牺牲自己。你的民多如清晨的甘露（或作你少年时光耀如清晨的甘露）。
Your people give themselves gladly in the day of your power; like the dew of the morning on the holy mountains is the army of your young men.

耶和华起了誓，决不后悔，说，你是照着麦基洗德的等次，永远为祭司。
The Lord has made an oath, and will not take it back. You are a priest for ever, after the order of Melchizedek.

在你右边的主，当他发怒的日子，必打伤列王。
In the day of his wrath kings will be wounded by the Lord at your right hand.

他要在列邦中刑罚恶人，尸首就遍满各处。他要在许多国中打破仇敌的头
He will be judge among the nations, the valleys will be full of dead bodies; the head over a great country will be wounded by him.

他要喝路旁的河水，因此必抬起头来。
He will take of the stream by the way; so his head will be lifted up.
