你们要赞美耶和华。我要在正直人的大会中，并公会中，一心称谢耶和华。
Let the Lord be praised. I will give praise to the Lord with all my heart, among the upright, and in the meeting of the people.

耶和华的作为本为大。凡喜爱的都必考察。
The works of the Lord are great, searched out by all those who have delight in them.

他所行的是尊荣和威严。他的公义存到永远。
His work is full of honour and glory; and his righteousness is unchanging for ever.

他行了奇事，使人记念。耶和华有恩惠，有怜悯。
Certain for ever is the memory of his wonders: the Lord is full of pity and mercy.

他赐粮食给敬畏他的人。他必永远记念他的约。
He has given food to his worshippers; he will keep his agreement in mind for ever.

他向百姓显出大能的作为，把外邦的地赐给他们为业。
He has made clear to his people the power of his works, giving them the heritage of the nations.

他手所行的，是诚实公平。他的训词都是确实的。
The works of his hands are faith and righteousness; all his laws are unchanging.

是永永远远坚定的，是按诚实正直设立的。
They are fixed for ever and ever, they are done in faith and righteousness.

他向百姓施行救赎，命定他的约，直到永远。他的名圣而可畏。
He has sent salvation to his people; he has given his word for ever: holy is his name and greatly to be feared.

敬畏耶和华是智慧得开端。凡遵行。他命令的，是聪明人。耶和华是永远当赞美的。
The fear of the Lord is the best part of wisdom: all those who keep his laws are wise: his praise is eternal.

你们要赞美耶和华。敬畏耶和华，甚喜爱他命令的，这人便为有福。
Let the Lord be praised. Happy is the man who gives honour to the Lord, and has great delight in his laws.

他的后裔在世必强盛。正直人的后代，必要蒙福。
His seed will be strong on the earth; blessings will be on the generation of the upright.

他家中有货物，有钱财。他的公义存到永远。
A store of wealth will be in his house, and his righteousness will be for ever.

正直人在黑暗中，有光向他发现。他有恩惠，有怜悯，有公义。
For the upright there is a light shining in the dark; he is full of grace and pity.

施恩与人，借贷与人的，这人事情顺利。他被审判的时候，要诉明自己的冤。
All is well for the man who is kind and gives freely to others; he will make good his cause when he is judged.

他永不动摇。义人被记念，直到永远。
He will not ever be moved; the memory of the upright will be living for ever.

他必不怕凶恶的信息。他心坚定，倚靠耶和华。
He will have no fear of evil news; his heart is fixed, for his hope is in the Lord.

他心确定，总不惧怕，直到他看见敌人遭报。
His heart is resting safely, he will have no fear, till he sees trouble come on his haters.

他施舍钱财，周济贫穷。他的仁义存到永远。他的角必被高举，大有荣耀。
He has given with open hands to the poor; his righteousness is for ever; his horn will be lifted up with honour.

恶人看见便恼恨。必咬牙而消化。恶人的心愿，要归灭绝。
The sinner will see it with grief; he will be wasted away with envy; the desire of the evil-doers will come to nothing.

你们要赞美耶和华。耶和华的仆人哪，你们要赞美，赞美耶和华的名。
Let the Lord be praised. O you servants of the Lord, give praise to the name of the Lord.

耶和华的名，是应当称颂的，从今时直到永远。
Let blessing be on the name of the Lord, from this time and for ever.

从日出之地，到日落之处，耶和华的名是应当赞美的。
From the coming up of the sun to its going down, the Lord's name is to be praised.

耶和华超乎万民之上。他的荣耀高过诸天。
The Lord is high over all nations, and his glory is higher than the heavens.

谁像耶和华我们的神呢？他坐在至高之处，
Who is like the Lord our God, who is seated on high,

自己谦卑，观看天上地下的事。
Looking down on the heavens, and on the earth?

他从灰尘里抬举贫寒人，从粪堆中提拔穷乏人。
He takes the poor man out of the dust, lifting him up from his low position;

使他们与王子同坐，就是与本国的王子同坐。
To give him a place among the rulers, even with the rulers of his people.

他使不能生育的妇人安居家中，为多子的乐母。你们要赞美耶和华。
He gives the unfertile woman a family, making her a happy mother of children. Give praise to the Lord.

以色列出了埃及，雅各家离开说异言之民。
When Israel came out of Egypt, the children of Jacob from a people whose language was strange to them;

那时，犹大为主的圣所，以色列为他所治理的国度。
Judah became his holy place, and Israel his kingdom.

沧海看见就奔逃。约旦河也倒流。
The sea saw it, and went in flight; Jordan was turned back.

大山踊跃，如公羊。小山跳舞，如羊羔。
The mountains were jumping like goats, and the little hills like lambs.

沧海阿，你为何奔逃。约旦哪，你为何倒流。
What was wrong with you, O sea, that you went in flight? O Jordan, that you were turned back?

大山哪，你为何踊跃，如公羊。小山哪，你为何跳舞，如羊羔。
You mountains, why were you jumping like goats, and you little hills like lambs?

大地阿，你因见主的面，就是雅各神的面，便要震动。
Be troubled, O earth, before the Lord, before the God of Jacob;

他叫磐石变为水池，叫坚石变为泉源。
Who made the rock into a water-spring, and the hard stone into a fountain.

耶和华阿，荣耀不要归与我们，不要归与我们。要因你的慈爱和诚实归在你的名下。
Not to us, O Lord, not to us, but to your name let glory be given, because of your mercy and your unchanging faith.

为何容外邦人说，他们的神在哪里呢？
Why may the nations say, Where is now their God?

然而，我们的神在天上。都随自己的意旨行事。
But our God is in heaven: he has done whatever was pleasing to him.

他们的偶像，是金的，银的，是人手所造的。
Their images are silver and gold, the work of men's hands.

有口却不能言，有眼却不能看。
They have mouths, but no voice; they have eyes, but they see not;

有耳却不能听。有鼻却不能闻。
They have ears, but no hearing; they have noses, but no sense of smell;

有手却不能摸。有脚却不能走。有喉咙也不能出声。
They have hands without feeling, and feet without power of walking; and no sound comes from their throat.

造他的要和他一样。凡靠他的也要如此。
Those who make them are like them; and so is everyone who puts his faith in them.

以色列阿，你要倚靠耶和华。他是你的帮助，和你的盾牌。
O Israel, have faith in the Lord: he is their help and their breastplate.

亚伦家阿，你们要倚靠耶和华。他是你们的帮助，和你们的盾牌。
O house of Aaron, have faith in the Lord: he is their help and their breastplate.

你们敬畏耶和华的，要倚靠耶和华。他是你们的帮助，和你们的盾牌。
You worshippers of the Lord, have faith in the Lord: he is their help and their breastplate.

耶和华向来眷念我们。他还要赐福给我们，要赐福给以色列的家，赐福给亚伦的家。
The Lord has kept us in mind and will give us his blessing; he will send blessings on the house of Israel and on the house of Aaron.

凡敬畏耶和华的，无论大小，主必赐福给他。
He will send blessings on the worshippers of the Lord, on the small and on the great.

愿耶和华叫你们和你们的子孙，日见加增。
May the Lord give you and your children still greater increase.

你们蒙了造天地之耶和华的福。
May you have the blessing of the Lord, who made heaven and earth.

天，是耶和华的天。地，他却给了世人。
The heavens are the Lord's; but the earth he has given to the children of men.

死人不能赞美耶和华。下到寂静中的也都不能。
The dead do not give praise to the Lord; or those who go down to the underworld.

但我们要称颂耶和华，从今时直到永远。你们要赞美耶和华。
But we will give praise to the Lord now and for ever. Praise be to the Lord.

我爱耶和华，因为他听了我的声音，和我的恳求。
I have given my love to the Lord, because he has given ear to the voice of my cry and my prayer.

他既向我侧耳，我一生要求告他。
He has let my request come before him, and I will make my prayer to him all my days.

死亡的绳索缠绕我，阴间的痛苦抓住我。我遭遇患难愁苦。
The nets of death were round me, and the pains of the underworld had me in their grip; I was full of trouble and sorrow.

那时，我便求告耶和华的名，说，耶和华阿，求你救我的灵魂。
Then I made my prayer to the Lord, saying, O Lord, take my soul out of trouble.

耶和华有恩惠，有公义。我们的神以怜悯为怀。
The Lord is full of grace and righteousness; truly, he is a God of mercy.

耶和华保护愚人。我落到卑微的地步，他救了我。
The Lord keeps the simple; I was made low, and he was my saviour.

我的心哪，你要仍归安乐，因为耶和华用厚恩待你。
Come back to your rest, O my soul; for the Lord has given you your reward.

主阿，你救我的命，免了死亡，救我的眼，免了流泪，救我的脚，免了跌倒。
You have taken my soul from the power of death, keeping my eyes from weeping, and my feet from falling.

我要在耶和华面前，行活人之路。
I will go before the Lord in the land of the living.

我因信，所以如此说话。我受了极大的困苦。
I still had faith, though I said, I am in great trouble;

我曾急促地说，人都是说谎的。
Though I said in my fear, All men are false.

我拿什么报答耶和华向我所赐的一切厚恩。
What may I give to the Lord for all the good things which he has done for me?

我要举起救恩的杯，称扬耶和华的名。
I will take the cup of salvation, and give praise to the name of the Lord.

我要在他众民面前向耶和华还我的愿。
I will make the offering of my oath to the Lord, even before all his people.

在耶和华眼中，看圣民之死，极为宝贵。
Dear in the eyes of the Lord is the death of his saints.

耶和华阿，我真是你的仆人。我是你的仆人，是你婢女的儿子。你已经解开我的绑索。
O Lord, truly I am your servant; I am your servant, the son of her who is your servant; by you have my cords been broken.

我要以感谢为祭献给你，又要求告耶和华的名。
I will give an offering of praise to you, and make my prayer in the name of the Lord.

我要在他众民面前，在耶和华殿的院内，在耶路撒冷当中，向耶和华还我的愿。你们要赞美耶和华。
I will make the offerings of my oath, even before all his people;


In the Lord's house, even in Jerusalem. Praise be to the Lord.

万国阿，你们都当赞美耶和华。万民哪，你们都当颂赞他。
Let all the nations give praise to the Lord: let all the people give him praise.

因为他向我们大施慈爱。耶和华的诚实存到永远。你们要赞美耶和华。
For great is his mercy to us, and his faith is unchanging for ever. Praise be to the Lord.

你们要称谢耶和华，因他本为善。他的慈爱永远长存。
O give praise to the Lord, for he is good: for his mercy is unchanging for ever.

愿以色列说，他的慈爱永远长存。
Let Israel now say, that his mercy is unchanging for ever.

愿亚伦的家说，他的慈爱永远长存。
Let the house of Aaron now say, that his mercy is unchanging for ever.

愿敬畏耶和华的说，他的慈爱永远长存。
Let all worshippers of the Lord now say, that his mercy is unchanging for ever.

我在急难中求告耶和华，他就应允我，把我安置在宽阔之地。
I made my prayer to the Lord in my trouble: and the Lord gave me an answer, and put me in a wide place.

有耶和华帮助我。我必不惧怕。人能把我怎么样呢？
The Lord is on my side; I will have no fear: what is man able to do to me?

在那帮助我的人中，有耶和华帮助我，所以我要看见那恨我的人遭报。
The Lord is my great helper: I will see my desire against my haters.

投靠耶和华，强似倚赖人。
It is better to have faith in the Lord than to put one's hope in man.

投靠耶和华，强似倚赖王子。
It is better to have faith in the Lord than to put one's hope in rulers.

万民围绕我。我靠耶和华的名，必剿灭他们。
All the nations have come round me; but in the name of the Lord I will have them cut down.

他们环绕我，围困我。我靠耶和华的名，必剿灭他们。
They are round me, yes, they are all about me; but in the name of the Lord I will have them cut down.

他们如同蜂子围绕我，好像烧荆棘的火，必被熄灭。我靠耶和华的名，必剿灭他们。
They are round me like bees; but they are put out like a fire among thorns; for in the name of the Lord I will have them cut down.

你推我，要叫我跌倒，但耶和华帮助了我。
I have been hard pushed by you, so that I might have a fall: but the Lord was my helper.

耶和华是我的力量，是我的诗歌。他也成了我的拯救。
The Lord is my strength and my song; he has become my salvation.

在义人的帐棚里，有欢呼拯救的声音。耶和华的右手施展大能。
The sound of joy and salvation is in the tents of the upright; the right hand of the Lord does works of power.

耶和华的右手高举。耶和华的右手施展大能。
The right hand of the Lord is lifted up; the right hand of the Lord does works of power.

我必不至死，仍要存活，并要传扬耶和华的作为。
Life and not death will be my part, and I will give out the story of the works of the Lord.

耶和华虽严严地惩治我，却未曾将我交于死亡。
The hand of Jah has been hard on me; but he has not given me up to death.

给我敞开义门。我要进去称谢耶和华。
Let the doors of righteousness be open to me; I will go in and give praise to the Lord.

这是耶和华的门。义人要进去。
This is the door of the Lord's house; the workers of righteousness will go in through it.

我要称谢你，因为你已经应允我，又成了我的拯救。
I will give you praise, for you have given me an answer, and have become my salvation.

匠人所弃的石头，已成了房角的头块石头。
The stone which the builders put on one side has become the chief stone of the building.

这是耶和华所做的，在我们眼中看为希奇。
This is the Lord's doing; it is a wonder in our eyes.

这是耶和华所定的日子。我们在其中要高兴欢喜。
This is the day which the Lord has made; we will be full of joy and delight in it.

耶和华阿，求你拯救。耶和华阿，求你使我们亨通。
Send salvation now, O Lord; Lord, send us your blessing.

奉耶和华名来的，是应当称颂的。我们从耶和华的殿中，为你们祝福。
A blessing be on him who comes in the name of the Lord; we give you blessing from the house of the Lord.

耶和华是神。他光照了我们。理当用绳索把祭牲拴住，牵到坛角那里。
The Lord is God, and he has given us light; let the holy dance be ordered with branches, even up to the horns of the altar.

你是我的神，我要称谢你。你是我的神，我要尊崇你。
You are my God, and I will give you praise; my God, and I will give honour to your name.

你们要称谢耶和华，因他本为善。他的慈爱永远长存。
O give praise to the Lord, for he is good: for his mercy is unchanging for ever.

行为完全，遵行耶和华律法的，这人便为有福。
<ALEPH> Happy are they who are without sin in their ways, walking in the law of the Lord.

遵守他的法度，一心寻求他的，这人便为有福。
Happy are they who keep his unchanging word, searching after him with all their heart.

这人不做非义的事，但遵行他的道。
They do no evil; they go in his ways.

耶和华阿，你曾将你的训词吩咐我们，为要我们殷勤遵守。
You have put your orders into our hearts, so that we might keep them with care.

但愿我行事坚定，得以遵守你的律例。
If only my ways were ordered so that I might keep your rules!

我看重你的一切命令，就不至于羞愧。
Then I would not be put to shame, as long as I have respect for all your teaching.

我学了你公义的判语，就要以正直的心称谢你。
I will give you praise with an upright heart in learning your right decisions.

我必守你的律例。求你总不要丢弃我。
I will keep your rules: O give me not up completely.

少年人用什么洁净他的行为呢？是要遵行你的话。
<BETH> How may a young man make his way clean? by guiding it after your word.

我一心寻求了你。求你不要叫我偏离你的命令。
I have made search for you with all my heart: O let me not go wandering far from your teaching.

我将你的话藏在心里，免得我得罪你。
I have kept your sayings secretly in my heart, so that I might do no sin against you.

耶和华阿，你是应当称颂的。求你将你的律例教训我。
Praise be to you, O Lord: give me knowledge of your rules.

我用嘴唇传扬你口中的一切典章。
With my lips have I made clear all the decisions of your mouth.

我喜悦你的法度，如同喜悦一切的财物。
I have taken as much delight in the way of your unchanging word, as in all wealth.

我要默想你的训词，看重你的道路。
I will give thought to your orders, and have respect for your ways.

我要在你的律例中自乐。我不忘记你的话。
I will have delight in your rules; I will not let your word go out of my mind.

求你用厚恩待你的仆人，使我存活。我就遵守你的话。
<GIMEL> Give me, your servant, the reward of life, so that I may keep your word;

求你开我的眼睛，使我看出你律法中的奇妙。
Let my eyes be open to see the wonders of your law.

我是在地上作寄居的。求你不要向我隐瞒你的命令。
I am living in a strange land: do not let your teachings be kept secret from me.

我时常切慕你的典章，甚至心碎。
My soul is broken with desire for your decisions at all times.

受咒诅偏离你命令的骄傲人，你已经责备他们。
Your hand has been against the men of pride, a curse is on those who go wandering out of your way.

求你除掉我所受的羞辱和藐视。因我遵守你的法度。
Take away from me shame and bitter words; for I have kept your unchanging word in my heart.

虽有首领坐着妄论我。你仆人却思想你的律例。
Rulers make evil designs against me; but your servant gives thought to your rules.

你的法度，是我所喜乐的，是我的谋士。
Your unchanging word is my delight, and the guide of my footsteps.

我的性命几乎归于尘土。求你照你的话，将我救活。
<DALETH> My soul is joined to the dust: O give me life, in keeping with your word.

我述说我所行的，你应允了我。求你将你的律例教训我。
I put the record of my ways before you, and you gave me an answer: O give me knowledge of your rules.

求你使我明白你的训词，我就思想你的奇事。
Make the way of your orders clear to me; then my thoughts will be ever on your wonders.

我的心因愁苦而消化。求你照你的话使我坚立。
My soul is wasted with sorrow; give me strength again in keeping with your word

求你使我离开奸诈的道，开恩将你的律法赐给我。
Take from me every false way; and in mercy give me your law.

我拣选了忠信的道，将你的典章摆在我面前。
I have taken the way of faith: I have kept your decisions before me.

我持守你的法度。耶和华阿，求你不要叫我羞愧。
I have been true to your unchanging word; O Lord, do not put me to shame.

你开广我心的时候，我就往你命令的道上直奔。
I will go quickly in the way of your teaching, because you have given me a free heart.

耶和华阿，求你将你的律例指教我，我必遵守到底。
<HE> O Lord, let me see the way of your rules, and I will keep it to the end.

求你赐我悟性，我便遵守你的律法。且要一心遵守。
Give me wisdom, so that I may keep your law; going after it with all my heart.

求你叫我遵行你的命令。因为这是我所喜乐的。
Make me go in the way of your teachings; for they are my delight.

求你使我的心，趋向你的法度，不趋向非义之财。
Let my heart be turned to your unchanging word, and not to evil desire.

求你叫我转眼不看虚假，又叫我在你的道中生活。
Let my eyes be turned away from what is false; give me life in your ways.

你向敬畏你的人所应许的话，求你向仆人坚定。
Give effect to your word to your servant, in whose heart is the fear of you.

求你使我所怕的羞辱远离我，因你的典章本为美。
Take away the shame which is my fear; for your decisions are good.

我羡慕你的训词。求你使我在你的公义上生活。
See how great is my desire for your orders: give me life in your righteousness.

耶和华阿，愿你照你的话，使你的慈爱，就是你的救恩，临到我身上。
<VAU> Let your mercies come to me, O Lord, even your salvation, as you have said.

我就有话回答那羞辱我的。因我倚靠你的话。
So that I may have an answer for the man who would put me to shame; for I have faith in your word.

求你叫真理的话，总不离开我口。因我仰望你的典章。
Take not your true word quite out of my mouth; for I have put my hope in your decisions.

我要常守你的律法，直到永永远远。
So that I may keep your law for ever and ever;

我要自由而行（或作我要行在宽阔之地）。因我素来考究你的训词。
So that my way may be in a wide place: because my search has been for your orders.

我也要在君王面前，论说你的法度，并不至于羞愧。
So that I may give knowledge of your unchanging word before kings, and not be put to shame.

我要在你的命令中自乐。这命令素来是我所爱的。
And so that I may take delight in your teachings, to which I have given my love.

我又要遵行（原文作举手）你的命令。这命令素来是我所爱的。我也要思想你的律例。
And so that my hands may be stretched out to you; and I will give thought to your rules.

求你记念向你仆人所应许的话，叫我有盼望。
<ZAIN> Keep in mind your word to your servant, for on it has my hope been fixed.

这话将我救活了。我在患难中，因此得安慰。
This is my comfort in my trouble; that your sayings have given me life.

骄傲的人甚侮慢我。我却未曾偏离你的律法。
The men of pride have made great sport of me; but I have not been turned from your law.

耶和华阿，我记念你从古以来的典章，就得了安慰。
I have kept the memory of your decisions from times past, O Lord; and they have been my comfort.

我见恶人离弃你的律法，就怒气发作，犹如火烧。
I am burning with wrath, because of the sinners who have given up your law.

我在世寄居，素来以你的律例为诗歌。
Your rules have been melodies to me, while I have been living in strange lands.

耶和华阿，我夜间记念你的名，遵守你的律法。
I have given thought to your name in the night, O Lord, and have kept your law.

我所以如此，是因我守你的训词。
This has been true of me, that I have kept your orders in my heart.

耶和华是我的福分。我曾说，我要遵守你的言语。
<CHETH> The Lord is my heritage: I have said that I would be ruled by your words.

我一心求过你的恩。愿你照你的话怜悯我。
I have given my mind to do your pleasure with all my heart; have mercy on me, as you have said.

我思想我所行的道，就转步归向你的法度。
I gave thought to my steps, and my feet were turned into the way of your unchanging word.

我急忙遵守你的命令，并不迟延。
I was quick to do your orders, and let no time be wasted.

恶人的绳索缠绕我。我却没有忘记你的律法。
The cords of evil-doers are round me; but I have kept in mind your law.

我因你公义的典章，半夜必起来称谢你。
In the middle of the night I will get up to give you praise, because of all your right decisions.

凡敬畏你，守你训词的人，我都与他作伴。
I keep company with all your worshippers, and those who have your orders in their memory.

耶和华阿，你的慈爱遍满大地。求你将你的律例教训我。
The earth, O Lord, is full of your mercy: give me knowledge of your rules.

耶和华阿，你向来是照你的话善待仆人。
<TETH> You have done good to your servant, O Lord, in keeping with your word.

求你将精明和知识赐给我。因我信了你的命令。
Give me knowledge and good sense; for I have put my faith in your teachings.

我未受苦以先，走迷了路，现在却遵守你的话。
Before I was in trouble I went out of the way; but now I keep your word.

你本为善，所行的也善。求你将你的律例教训我。
You are good, and your works are good; give me knowledge of your rules.

骄傲人编造谎言攻击我。我却要一心守你的训词。
The men of pride have said false things about me; but I will keep your orders in my heart.

他们心蒙脂油。我却喜爱你的律法。
Their hearts are shut up with fat; but my delight is in your law.

我受苦是与我有益，为要使我学习你的律例。
It is good for me to have been through trouble; so that I might come to the knowledge of your rules.

你口中的训言（或作律法），与我有益，胜于千万的金银。
The law of your mouth is better to me than thousands of gold and silver.

你的手制造我，建立我。求你赐我悟性，可以学习你的命令。
<JOD> Your hands have made me, and given me form: give me wisdom, so that I may have knowledge of your teaching.

敬畏你的人见我，就要欢喜。因我仰望你的话。
Your worshippers will see me and be glad; because my hope has been in your word.

耶和华阿，我知道你的判语是公义的。你使我受苦，是以诚实待我。
I have seen, O Lord, that your decisions are right, and that in unchanging faith you have sent trouble on me.

求你照着应许仆人的话，以慈爱安慰我。
Let your mercy now be my comfort, as you have said to your servant.

愿你的慈悲临到我，使我存活。因你的律法是我所喜爱的。
Let your gentle mercies come to me, so that I may have life; for your law is my delight.

愿骄傲人蒙羞。因为他们无理地倾覆我。但我要思想你的训词。
Let the men of pride be shamed; because they have falsely given decision against me; but I will give thought to your orders.

愿敬畏你的人归向我，他们就知道你的法度。
Let your worshippers be turned to me, and those who have knowledge of your words.

愿我的心在你的律例上完全，使我不至蒙羞。
Let all my heart be given to your orders, so that I may not be put to shame.

我心渴想你的救恩，仰望你的应许。
<CAPH> My soul is wasted with desire for your salvation: but I have hope in your word.

我因盼望你的应许，眼睛失明，说，你何时安慰我。
My eyes are full of weariness with searching for your word, saying, When will you give me comfort?

我好像烟薰的皮袋。却不忘记你的律例。
For I have become like a wine-skin black with smoke; but I still keep the memory of your rules.

你仆人的年日有多少呢？你几时向逼迫我的人施行审判呢？
How short is the life of your servant! when will you give your decision against those who are attacking me?

不从你律法的骄傲人，为我掘了坑。
The men of pride, who are turned away from your law, have put nets for me.

你的命令尽都诚实。他们无理地逼迫我，求你帮助我。
All your teachings are certain; they go after me with evil design; give me your help.

他们几乎把我从世上灭绝，但我没有离弃你的训词。
They had almost put an end to me on earth; but I did not give up your orders.

求你照你的慈爱将我救活。我就遵守你口中的法度。
Give me life in your mercy; so that I may be ruled by the unchanging word of your mouth.

耶和华阿，你的话安定在天，直到永远。
<LAMED> For ever, O Lord, your word is fixed in heaven.

你的诚实存到万代。你坚定了地，地就长存。
Your faith is unchanging from generation to generation: you have put the earth in its place, and it is not moved.

天地照你的安排，存到今日。万物都是你的仆役。
They are ruled this day by your decisions; for all things are your servants.

我若不是喜爱你的律法，早就在苦难中灭绝了。
If your law had not been my delight, my troubles would have put an end to me.

我永不忘记你的训词。因你用这训词将我救活了。
I will ever keep your orders in mind; for in them I have life.

我是属你的，求你救我，因我寻求了你的训词。
I am yours, O be my saviour; for my desire has been for your rules.

恶人等待我，要灭绝我，我却要揣摩你的法度。
The sinners have been waiting for me to give me up to destruction; but I will give all my mind to your unchanging word.

我看万事尽都有限。惟有你的命令，极其宽广。
I have seen that nothing on earth is complete; but your teaching is very wide.

我何等爱慕你的律法，终日不住地思想。
<MEM> O what love I have for your law! I give thought to it all the day.

你的命令常存在我心里，使我比仇敌有智慧。
Your teaching has made me wiser than my haters: for it is mine for ever.

我比我的师傅更通达。因我思想你的法度。
I have more knowledge than all my teachers, because I give thought to your unchanging word.

我比年老的更明白，因我守了你的训词。
I have more wisdom than the old, because I have kept your orders.

我禁止我脚走一切的邪路，为要遵守你的话。
I have kept back my feet from all evil ways, so that I might be true to your word.

我没有偏离你的典章，因为你教训了我。
My heart has not been turned away from your decisions; for you have been my teacher.

你的言语，在我上膛何等甘美。在我口中比蜜更甜。
How sweet are your sayings to my taste! truly, they are sweeter than honey in my mouth!

我借着你的训词，得以明白。所以我恨一切的假道。
Through your orders I get wisdom; for this reason I am a hater of every false way.

你的话是我脚前的灯，是我路上的光。
<NUN> Your word is a light for my feet, ever shining on my way.

你公义的典章，我曾起誓遵守，我必按誓而行。
I have made an oath and kept it, to be guided by your upright decisions.

我甚是受苦。耶和华阿，求你照你的话将我救活。
I am greatly troubled, O Lord, give me life in keeping with your word.

耶和华阿，求你悦纳我口中的赞美为供物，又将你的典章教训我。
Take, O Lord, the free offerings of my mouth, and give me knowledge of your decisions.

我的性命常在危险之中，我却不忘记你的律法。
My soul is ever in danger; but I still keep the memory of your law.

恶人为我设下网罗。我却没有偏离你的训词。
Sinners have put a net to take me; but I was true to your orders.

我以你的法度为永远的产业。因这是我心中所喜爱的。
I have taken your unchanging word as an eternal heritage; for it is the joy of my heart.

我的心专向你的律例，永远遵行，一直到底。
My heart is ever ready to keep your rules, even to the end.

心怀二意的人，为我所恨。但你的律法，为我所爱。
<SAMECH> I am a hater of men of doubting mind; but I am a lover of your law.

你是我藏身之处，又是我的盾牌。我甚仰望你的话语。
You are my secret place and my breastplate against danger; my hope is in your word.

作恶的人哪，你们离开我吧，我好遵守我神的命令。
Go far from me, you evil-doers; so that I may keep the teachings of my God.

求你照你的话扶持我，使我存活，也不叫我因失望而害羞。
Be my support as you have said, and give me life; let not my hope be turned to shame.

求你扶持我，我便得救，时常看重你的律例。
Let me not be moved, and I will be safe, and ever take delight in your rules.

凡偏离你律例的人，你都轻弃他们。因为他们的诡诈必归虚空。
You have overcome all those who are wandering from your rules; for all their thoughts are false.

凡地上的恶人，你除掉他，好像除掉渣滓。因此我爱你的法度。
All the sinners of the earth are like waste metal in your eyes; and for this cause I give my love to your unchanging word.

我因惧怕你，肉就发抖。我也怕你的判语。
My flesh is moved for fear of you; I give honour to your decisions.

我行过公平和公义。求你不要撇下我给欺压我的人。
<AIN> I have done what is good and right: you will not give me into the hands of those who are working against me.

求你为仆人作保，使我得好处。不容骄傲人欺压我。
Take your servant's interests into your keeping; let me not be crushed by the men of pride.

我因盼望你的救恩，和你公义的话，眼睛失明。
My eyes are wasted with desire for your salvation, and for the word of your righteousness.

求你照你的慈爱待仆人，将你的律例教训我。
Be good to your servant in your mercy, and give me teaching in your rules.

我是你的仆人。求你赐我悟性，使我得知你的法度。
I am your servant; give me wisdom, so that I may have knowledge of your unchanging word.

这是耶和华降罚的时候，因人废了你的律法。
It is time, O Lord, for you to let your work be seen; for they have made your law without effect.

所以，我爱你的命令胜于金子，更胜于精金。
For this reason I have greater love far your teachings than for gold, even for shining gold.

你一切的训词，在万事上我都以为正直。我却恨恶一切假道。
Because of it I keep straight in all things by your orders; and I am a hater of every false way.

你的法度奇妙，所以我一心谨守。
<PE> Your unchanging word is full of wonder; for this reason my soul keeps it.

你的言语一解开，就发出亮光，使愚人通达。
The opening of your words gives light; it gives good sense to the simple.

我张口而气喘。因我切慕你的命令。
My mouth was open wide, waiting with great desire for your teachings.

求你转向我，怜悯我，好象你素常待那些爱你名的人。
Let your eyes be turned to me, and have mercy on me, as it is right for you to do to those who are lovers of your name.

求你用你的话，使我脚步稳当，不许什么罪孽辖制我。
Let my steps be guided by your word; and let not sin have control over me.

求你救我脱离人的欺压。我要遵守你的训词。
Make me free from the cruel rule of man; then I will keep your orders.

求你用脸光照仆人。又将你的律例教训我。
Let your servant see the shining of your face; give me knowledge of your rules.

我的眼泪下流成河，因为他们不守你的律法。
Rivers of water are flowing from my eyes, because men do not keep your law.

耶和华阿，你是公义的，你的判语也是正直的。
<TZADE> O Lord, great is your righteousness, and upright are your decisions.

你所命定的法度，是凭公义和至诚。
You have given your unchanging word in righteousness, and it is for ever.

我心焦急，如同火烧，因我敌人忘记你的言语。
My passion has overcome me; because my haters are turned away from your words.

你的话极其精炼。所以你的仆人喜爱。
Your word is of tested value; and it is dear to your servant.

我微小，被人藐视。却不忘记你的训词。
I am small and of no account; but I keep your orders in mind.

你的公义永远长存。你的律法尽都真实。
Your righteousness is an unchanging righteousness, and your law is certain.

我遭遇患难愁苦。你的命令却是我所喜爱的。
Pain and trouble have overcome me: but your teachings are my delight.

你的法度永远是公义的。求你赐我悟性，我就活了。
The righteousness of your unchanging word is eternal; give me wisdom so that I may have life.

耶和华阿，我一心呼吁你。求你应允我，我必谨守你的律例。
<KOPH> I have made my prayer with all my heart; give answer to me, O Lord: I will keep your rules.

我向你呼吁，求你救我。我要遵守你的法度。
My cry has gone up to you; take me out of trouble, and I will be guided by your unchanging word.

我趁天未亮呼求。我仰望了你的言语。
Before the sun is up, my cry for help comes to your ear; my hope is in your words.

我趁夜更未换，将眼睁开，为要思想你的话语。
In the night watches I am awake, so that I may give thought to your saying.

求你照你的慈爱听我的声音。耶和华阿，求你照你的典章，将我救活。
Let my voice come to you, in your mercy; O Lord, by your decisions give me life.

追求奸恶的人临近了。他们远离你的律法。
Those who have evil designs against me come near; they are far from your law.

耶和华阿，你与我相近。你一切的命令尽都真实。
You are near, O Lord; and all your teachings are true.

我因学你的法度，久已知道是你永远立定的。
I have long had knowledge that your unchanging word is for ever.

求你看顾我的苦难，搭救我，因我不忘记你的律法。
<RESH> O see my trouble, and be my saviour; for I keep your law in my mind,

求你为我辨屈，救赎我，照你的话将我救活。
Undertake my cause, and come to my help, give me life, as you have said.

救恩远离恶人。因为他们不寻求你的律例。
Salvation is far from evil-doers; for they have made no search for your rules.

耶和华阿，你的慈悲本为大。求你照你的典章将我救活。
Great is the number of your mercies, O Lord; give me life in keeping with your decisions.

逼迫我的，抵挡我的，很多，我却没有偏离你的法度。
Great is the number of those who are against me; but I have not been turned away from your unchanging word.

我看见奸恶的人，就甚憎恶，因为他们不遵守你的话。
I saw with hate those who were untrue to you; for they did not keep your saying.

你看我怎样爱你的训词。耶和华阿，求你照你的慈爱将我救活。
See how great is my love for your orders: give me life, O Lord, in keeping with your mercy.

你话的总纲是真实。你一切公义的典章是永远长存。
Your word is true from the first; and your upright decision is unchanging for ever.

首领无故地逼迫我。但我的心畏惧你的言语。
<SHIN> Rulers have been cruel to me without cause; but I have the fear of your word in my heart.

我喜爱你的话，好像人得了许多掳物。
I am delighted by your saying, like a man who makes discovery of great wealth.

谎话是我所恨恶所憎嫌的。惟你的律法，是我所爱的。
I am full of hate and disgust for false words; but I am a lover of your law.

我因你公义的典章，一天七次赞美你。
Seven times a day do I give you praise, because of your upright decisions.

爱你律法的人，有大平安。什么都不能使他们绊脚。
Great peace have lovers of your law; they have no cause for falling.

耶和华阿，我仰望了你的救恩，遵行了你的命令。
Lord, my hope has been in your salvation; and I have kept your teachings.

我心里守了你的法度。这法度我甚喜爱。
My soul has kept your unchanging word; great is my love for it.

我遵守了你的训词和法度。因我一切所行的，都在你面前。
I have been ruled by your orders; for all my ways are before you.

耶和华阿，愿我的呼吁达到你面前，照你的话赐我悟性。
<TAU> Let my cry come before you, O Lord; give me wisdom in keeping with your word.

愿我的恳求达到你面前，照你的话搭救我。
Let my prayer come before you; take me out of trouble, as you have said.

愿我的嘴发出赞美的话。因为你将律例教训我。
Let my lips be flowing with praise, because you have given me knowledge of your rules.

愿我的舌头歌唱你的话。因你一切的命令尽都公义。
Let my tongue make songs in praise of your word; for all your teachings are righteousness.

愿你用手帮助我。因我拣选了你的训词。
Let your hand be near for my help; for I have given my heart to your orders.

耶和华阿，我切慕你的救恩。你的律法也是我所喜爱的。
All my desire has been for your salvation, O Lord; and your law is my delight.

愿我的性命存活，得以赞美你。愿你的典章帮助我。
Give life to my soul so that it may give you praise; and let your decisions be my support.

我如亡羊走迷了路。求你寻找仆人。因我不忘记你的命令。
I have gone out of the way like a wandering sheep; make search for your servant; for I keep your teachings ever in mind.

（上行（或作登阶。下同）之诗。）我在急难中求告耶和华，他就应允我。
<A Song of the going up.> In my trouble my cry went up to the Lord, and he gave me an answer.

耶和华阿，求你救我脱离说谎的嘴唇，和诡诈的舌头。
O Lord, be the saviour of my soul from false lips, and from the tongue of deceit.

诡诈的舌头阿，要给你什么呢？要拿什么加给你呢？
What punishment will he give you? what more will he do to you, you false tongue?

就是勇士的利箭，和罗腾木的炭火（罗腾小树名松类）。
Sharp arrows of the strong, and burning fire.

我寄居在米设，住在基达帐棚之中，有祸了。
Sorrow is mine because I am strange in Meshech, and living in the tents of Kedar.

我与那恨恶和睦的人，许久同住。
My soul has long been living with the haters of peace.

我愿和睦。但我发言，他们就要争战。
I am for peace: but when I say so, they are for war.

（上行之诗。）我要向山举目。我的帮助从何而来。
<A Song of the going up.> My eyes are lifted up to the hills: O where will my help come from?

我的帮助从造天地的耶和华而来。
Your help comes from the Lord, who made heaven and earth.

他必不叫你的脚摇动。保护你的必不打盹。
May he not let your foot be moved: no need of sleep has he who keeps you.

保护以色列的，也不打盹，也不睡觉。
See, the eyes of Israel's keeper will not be shut in sleep.

保护你的是耶和华。耶和华在你右边荫庇你。
The Lord is your keeper; the Lord is your shade on your right hand.

白日太阳必不伤你，夜间月亮必不害你。
You will not be touched by the sun in the day, or by the moon at night.

耶和华要保护你，免受一切的灾害。他要保护你的性命。
The Lord will keep you safe from all evil; he will take care of your soul.

你出你入耶和华要保护你，从今时直到永远。
The Lord will keep watch over your going out and your coming in, from this time and for ever.

（大卫上行之诗。）人对我说，我们往耶和华的殿去，我就欢喜。
<A Song of the going up. Of David.> I was glad because they said to me, We will go into the house of the Lord.

耶路撒冷阿，我们的脚站在你的门内。
At last our feet were inside your doors, O Jerusalem.

耶路撒冷被建造，如同连络整齐的一座城。
O Jerusalem, you are like a town which is well joined together;

众支派，就是耶和华的支派，上那里去，按以色列的常例（或作作以色列的证据）称赞耶和华的名。
To which the tribes went up, even the tribes of the Lord, for a witness to Israel, to give praise to the name of the Lord.

因为在那里设立审判的宝座，就是大卫家的宝座。
For there seats for the judges were placed, even the rulers' seats of the line of David.

你们要为耶路撒冷求平安。耶路撒冷阿，爱你的人必然兴旺。
O make prayers for the peace of Jerusalem; may they whose love is given to you do well.

愿你城中平安，愿你宫内兴旺。
May peace be inside your walls, and wealth in your noble houses.

因我弟兄和同伴的缘故，我要说，愿平安在你中间。
Because of my brothers and friends, I will now say, Let peace be with you.

因耶和华我们神殿的缘故，我要为你求福。
Because of the house of the Lord our God, I will be working for your good.

（上行之诗。）坐在天上的主阿，我向你举目。
<A Song of the going up.> To you my eyes are lifted up, even to you whose seat is in the heavens.

看哪，仆人的眼睛怎样望主人的手，使女的眼睛怎样望主母的手，我们的眼睛也照样望耶和华我们的神，直到他怜悯我们。
See! as the eyes of servants are turned to the hands of their masters, and the eyes of a servant-girl to her owner, so our eyes are waiting for the Lord our God, till he has mercy on us.

耶和华阿，求你怜悯我们，怜悯我们。因为我们被藐视，已到极处。
Have mercy on us, O Lord, have mercy on us: for all men are looking down on us.

我们被那些安逸人的讥诮，和骄傲人的藐视，已到极处。
For long enough have men of pride made sport of our soul.

（大卫上行之诗。）以色列人要说，若不是耶和华帮助我们，
<A Song of the going up. Of David.> If it had not been the Lord who was on our side (let Israel now say);

若不是耶和华帮助我们，当人起来攻击我们，
If it had not been the Lord who was on our side, when men came up against us;

向我们发怒的时候，就把我们活活地吞了。
They would have made a meal of us while still living, in the heat of their wrath against us:

那时，波涛必漫过我们，河水必淹没我们。
We would have been covered by the waters; the streams would have gone over our soul;

狂傲的水必淹没我们。
Yes, the waters of pride would have gone over our soul.

耶和华是应当称颂的。他没有把我们当野食交给他们吞吃（原文作牙齿）。
Praise be to the Lord, who has not let us be wounded by their teeth.

我们好像雀鸟，从捕鸟人的网罗里逃脱。网罗破裂，我们逃脱了。
Our soul has gone free like a bird out of the net of those who would take her: the net is broken, and we are free.

我们得帮助，是在乎倚靠造天地之耶和华的名。
Our help is in the name of the Lord, the maker of heaven and earth.

（上行之诗。）倚靠耶和华的人，好像锡安山，永不动摇。
<A Song of the going up.> Those whose hope is in the Lord are like the mountain of Zion, which may not be moved, but keeps its place for ever.

众山怎样围绕耶路撒冷，耶和华也照样围绕他的百姓，从今时直到永远。
As the mountains are round about Jerusalem, so the Lord is round about his people, from this time and for ever.

恶人的杖不常落在义人的分上，免得义人伸手作恶。
For the rod of sinners will not be resting on the heritage of the upright; so that the upright may not put out their hands to evil.

耶和华阿，求你善待那些为善，和心里正直的人。
Do good, O Lord, to those who are good, and to those who are upright in heart.

至于那偏行弯曲道路的人，耶和华必使他和作恶的人一同出去受刑。愿平安归于以色列。
But as for such as are turned out of the straight way, the Lord will take them away with the workers of evil. Let peace be on Israel.

（上行之诗。）当耶和华将那些被掳的带回锡安的时候，我们好像做梦的人。
<A Song of the going up.> When the Lord made a change in Zion's fate, we were like men in a dream.

我们满口喜笑，满舌欢呼的时候，外邦中就有人说，耶和华为他们行了大事。
Then our mouths were full of laughing, and our tongues gave a glad cry; they said among the nations, The Lord has done great things for them.

耶和华果然为我们行了大事，我们就欢喜。
The Lord has done great things for us; because of which we are glad.

耶和华阿，求你使我们被掳的人归回，好像南地的河水复流。
Let our fate be changed, O Lord, like the streams in the South.

流泪撒种的，必欢呼收割。
Those who put in seed with weeping will get in the grain with cries of joy.

那带种流泪出去的，必要欢欢乐乐地带禾捆回来。
Though a man may go out weeping, taking his vessel of seed with him; he will come again in joy, with the corded stems of grain in his arms.

（所罗门上行之诗。）若不是耶和华建造房屋，建造的人就枉然劳力。若不是耶和华看守城池，看守的人就枉然儆醒。
<A Song of the going up. Of Solomon.> If the Lord is not helping the builders, then the building of a house is to no purpose: if the Lord does not keep the town, the watchman keeps his watch for nothing.

你们清晨早起，夜晚安歇，吃劳碌得来的饭，本是枉然。惟有耶和华所亲爱的，必叫他安然睡觉。
It is of no use for you to get up early, and to go late to your rest, with the bread of sorrow for your food; for the Lord gives to his loved ones in sleep.

儿女是耶和华所赐的产业。所怀的胎是他所给的赏赐。
See, sons are a heritage from the Lord; the fruit of the body is his reward.

少年时所生的儿女，好像勇士手中的箭。
Like arrows in the hand of a man of war, are the children of the young.

箭袋充满的人便为有福。他们在城门口和仇敌说话的时候，必不至于羞愧。
Happy is the man who has a good store of them; he will not be put to shame, but his cause will be supported by them against his haters.

（上行之诗。）凡敬畏耶和华，遵行他道的人便为有福。
<A Song of the going up.> Happy is the worshipper of the Lord, who is walking in his ways.

你要吃劳碌得来的。你要享福，事情顺利。
You will have the fruit of the work of your hands: happy will you be, and all will be well for you.

你妻子在你的内室，好像多结果子的葡萄树。你儿女围绕你的桌子，好像橄榄栽子。
Your wife will be like a fertile vine in the inmost parts of your house: your children will be like olive plants round your table.

看哪，敬畏耶和华的人，必要这样蒙福。
See! this is the blessing of the worshipper of the Lord.

愿耶和华从锡安赐福给你。愿你一生一世，看见耶路撒冷的好处。
May the Lord send you blessing out of Zion: may you see the good of Jerusalem all the days of your life.

愿你看见你儿女的儿女。愿平安归于以色列。
May you see your children's children. Peace be on Israel.

（上行之诗。）以色列当说，从我幼年以来，敌人屡次苦害我，
<A Song of the going up.> Great have been my troubles from the time when I was young (let Israel now say);

从我幼年以来，敌人屡次苦害我，却没有胜了我。
Great have been my troubles from the time when I was young, but my troubles have not overcome me.

如同扶犁的在我背上扶犁而耕，耕的犁沟甚长。
The ploughmen were ploughing on my back; long were the wounds they made.

耶和华是公义的。他砍断了恶人的绳索。
The Lord is true: the cords of the evil-doers are broken in two.

愿恨恶锡安的，都蒙羞退后。
Let all the haters of Zion be shamed and turned back.

愿他们像房顶上的草，未长成而枯干。
Let them be like the grass on the house-tops, which is dry before it comes to full growth.

收割的不够一把，捆禾的也不满怀。
He who gets in the grain has no use for it; and they do not make bands of it for the grain-stems.

过路的也不说，愿耶和华所赐的福，归与你们。我们奉耶和华的名，给你们祝福。
And those who go by do not say, The blessing of the Lord be on you; we give you blessing in the name of the Lord.

（上行之诗。）耶和华阿，我从深处向你求告。
<A Song of the going up.> Out of the deep have I sent up my cry to you, O Lord.

主阿，求你听我的声音。愿你侧耳听我恳求的声音。
Lord, let my voice come before you: let your ears be awake to the voice of my prayer.

主耶和华阿，你若究察罪孽，谁能站得住呢？
O Jah, if you took note of every sin, who would go free?

但在你有赦免之恩，要叫人敬畏你。
But there is forgiveness with you, so that you may be feared.

我等候耶和华，我的心等候。我也仰望他的话。
I am waiting for the Lord, my soul is waiting for him, and my hope is in his word.

我的心等候主，胜于守夜的，等候天亮，胜于守夜的，等候天亮。
My soul is watching for the Lord more than those who are watching for the morning; yes, more than the watchers for the morning.

以色列阿，你当仰望耶和华。因他有慈爱，有丰盛的救恩。
O Israel, have hope in the Lord; for with the Lord is mercy and full salvation.

他必救赎以色列脱离一切的罪孽。
And he will make Israel free from all his sins.

（大卫上行之诗。）耶和华阿，我的心不狂傲，我的眼不高大。重大和测不透的事，我也不敢行。
<A Song of the going up. Of David.> Lord, there is no pride in my heart and my eyes are not lifted up; and I have not taken part in great undertakings, or in things over-hard for me.

我的心平稳安静，好像断过奶的孩子在他母亲的怀中。我的心在我里面真像断过奶的孩子。
See, I have made my soul calm and quiet, like a child on its mother's breast; my soul is like a child on its mother's breast.

以色列阿，你当仰望耶和华，从今时直到永远。
O Israel, have hope in the Lord, from this time and for ever.

（上行之诗。）耶和华阿，求你记念大卫所受的一切苦难。
<A Song of the going up.> Lord, give thought to David, and to all his troubles;

他怎样向耶和华起誓，向雅各的大能者许愿，
How he made an oath to the Lord, and gave his word to the great God of Jacob, saying,

说，我必不进我的帐幕，也不上我的床榻。
Truly, I will not come into my house, or go to my bed,

我不容我的眼睛睡觉，也不容我的眼目打盹。
I will not give sleep to my eyes, or rest to my eyeballs,

直等我为耶和华寻得所在，为雅各的大能者寻得居所。
Till I have got a place for the Lord, a resting-place for the great God of Jacob.

我们听说约柜在以法他，我们在基列耶琳就寻见了。
We had news of it at Ephrathah: we came to it in the fields of the wood.

我们要进他的居所，在他脚凳前下拜。
Let us go into his tent; let us give worship at his feet.

耶和华阿，求你兴起，和你有能力的约柜同入安息之所。
Come back, O Lord, to your resting-place; you and the ark of your strength.

愿你的祭司披上公义。愿你的圣民欢呼。
Let your priests be clothed with righteousness; and let your saints give cries of joy.

求你因你仆人大卫的缘故，不要厌弃你的受膏者。
Because of your servant David, do not give up your king.

耶和华向大卫，凭诚实起了誓，必不反覆，说，我要使你所生的坐在你的宝座上。
The Lord gave a true oath to David, which he will not take back, saying, I will give your kingdom to the fruit of your body.

你的众子若守我的约，和我所教训他们的法度，他们的子孙，必永远坐在你的宝座上。
If your children keep my word, and the teachings which I will give them, their children will be rulers of your kingdom for ever.

因为耶和华拣选了锡安，愿意当作自己的居所，
For the Lord's heart is on Zion, desiring it for his resting-place.

说，这是我永远安息之所。我要住在这里，因为是我所愿意的。
This is my rest for ever: here will I ever be; for this is my desire.

我要使其中的粮食丰满，使其中的穷人饱足。
My blessing will be on her food; and her poor will be full of bread.

我要使祭司披上救恩，圣民大声欢呼。
Her priests will be clothed with salvation; and her saints will give cries of joy.

我要叫大卫的角，在那里发生。我为我的受膏者，预备明灯。
There I will make the horn of David fertile: I have made ready a light for my king.

我要使他的仇敌披上羞耻。但他的冠冕，要在头上发光。
His haters will be clothed with shame; but I will make his crown shining.

（大卫上行之诗。）看哪，弟兄和睦同居，是何等的善，何等的美。
<A Song of the going up. Of David.> See how good and how pleasing it is for brothers to be living together in harmony!

这好比那贵重的油，浇在亚伦的头上，流到胡须，又流到他的衣襟。
It is like oil of great price on the head, flowing down over the face, even Aaron's face: coming down to the edge of his robe;

又好比黑门的甘露，降在锡安山。因为在那里有耶和华所命定的福，就是永远的生命。
Like the dew of Hermon, which comes down on the mountains of Zion: for there the Lord gave orders for the blessing, even life for ever.

（上行之诗。）耶和华的仆人，夜间站在耶和华殿中的，你们当称颂耶和华。
<A Song of the going up.> Give praise to the Lord, all you servants of the Lord, who take your places in the house of the Lord by night.

你们当向圣所举手，称颂耶和华。
Give praise to the Lord, lifting up your hands in his holy place.

愿造天地的耶和华，从锡安赐福给你们。
May the Lord, who made heaven and earth, send you blessing out of Zion,

你们要赞美耶和华。你们要赞美耶和华的名。耶和华的仆人站在耶和华殿中，站在我们神殿院中的，你们要赞美他。
Let the Lord be praised. O you servants of the Lord, give praise to the name of the Lord.


You who are in the house of the Lord, and in the open spaces of the house of our God,

你们要赞美耶和华。耶和华本为善。要歌颂他的名，因为这是美好的。
Give praise to Jah, for he is good: make melody to his name, for it is pleasing.

耶和华拣选雅各归自己，拣选以色列特作自己的子民。
For the Lord has taken Jacob for himself, and Israel for his property.

原来我知道耶和华为大，也知道我们的主超乎万神之上。
I know that the Lord is great, and that our Lord is greater than all other gods.

耶和华在天上，在地下，在海中，在一切的深处，都随自己的意旨而行。
The Lord has done whatever was pleasing to him, in heaven, and on the earth, in the seas and in all the deep waters.

他使云雾从地极上腾，造电随雨而闪，从府库中带出风来。
He makes the mists go up from the ends of the earth; he makes thunder-flames for the rain; he sends out the winds from his store-houses.

他将埃及头生的，连人带牲畜都击杀了。
He put to death the first-fruits of Egypt, of man and of beast.

埃及阿，他施行神迹奇事，在你当中，在法老和他一切臣仆身上。
He sent signs and wonders among you, O Egypt, on Pharaoh, and on all his servants.

他击杀许多的民，又杀戮大能的王，
He overcame great nations, and put strong kings to death;

就是亚摩利王西宏，和巴珊王噩，并迦南一切的国王，
Sihon, king of the Amorites, and Og, king of Bashan, and all the kingdoms of Canaan;

将他们的地，赏赐他的百姓以色列为业。
And gave their land for a heritage, even for a heritage to Israel his people.

耶和华阿，你的名存到永远。耶和华阿，你可记念的名存到万代。
O Lord, your name is eternal; and the memory of you will have no end.

耶和华要为他的百姓伸冤，为他的仆人后悔。
For the Lord will be judge of his people's cause; his feelings will be changed to his servants.

外邦的偶像是金的，银的，是人手所造的。
The images of the nations are silver and gold, the work of men's hands.

有口却不能言，有眼却不能看，
They have mouths, but no voice, they have eyes, but they do not see;

有耳却不能听，口中也没有气息。
They have ears, but no hearing; and there is no breath in their mouths.

造他的要和他一样，凡靠他的也要如此。
Those who make them are like them; and so is everyone who puts his hope in them.

以色列家阿，你们要称颂耶和华。亚伦家阿，你们要称颂耶和华。
Give praise to the Lord, O children of Israel: give praise to the Lord, O sons of Aaron:

利未家阿，你们要称颂耶和华。你们敬畏耶和华的，要称颂耶和华。
Give praise to the Lord, O sons of Levi: let all the worshippers of the Lord give him praise.

住在耶路撒冷的耶和华，该从锡安受称颂。你们要赞美耶和华。
Praise be to the Lord out of Zion, even to the Lord whose house is in Jerusalem, Let the Lord be praised.

你们要称谢耶和华，因他本为善。他的慈爱永远长存。
O give praise to the Lord, for he is good: for his mercy is unchanging for ever.

你们要称谢万神之神，因他的慈爱永远长存。
O give praise to the God of gods: for his mercy is unchanging for ever.

你们要称谢万主之主，因他的慈爱永远长存。
O give praise to the Lord of lords: for his mercy is unchanging for ever.

称谢那独行大奇事的，因他的慈爱永远长存。
To him who only does great wonders: for his mercy is unchanging for ever.

称谢那用智慧造天的，因他的慈爱永远长存。
To him who by wisdom made the heavens: for his mercy is unchanging for ever.

称谢那铺地在水以上的，因他的慈爱永远长存。
To him by whom the earth was stretched out over the waters: for his mercy is unchanging for ever.

称谢那造成大光的，因他的慈爱永远长存。
To him who made great lights: for his mercy is unchanging for ever.

他造日头管白昼，因他的慈爱永远长存。
The sun to have rule by day: for his mercy is unchanging for ever.

他造月亮星宿管黑夜，因他的慈爱永远长存。
The moon and the stars to have rule by night: for his mercy is unchanging for ever.

称谢那击杀埃及人之长子的，因他的慈爱永远长存。
To him who put to death the first-fruits of Egypt: for his mercy is unchanging for ever:

他领以色列人从他们中间出来，因他的慈爱永远长存。
And took out Israel from among them: for his mercy is unchanging for ever:

他施展大能的手和伸出来的膀臂，因他的慈爱永远长存。
With a strong hand and an outstretched arm: for his mercy is unchanging for ever.

称谢那分裂红海的，因他的慈爱永远长存。
To him who made a way through the Red Sea: for his mercy is unchanging for ever:

他领以色列从其中经过，因他的慈爱永远长存。
And let Israel go through it: for his mercy is unchanging for ever:

却把法老和他的军兵推翻在红海里，因他的慈爱永远长存。
By him Pharaoh and his army were overturned in the Red Sea: for his mercy is unchanging for ever.

称谢那引导自己的民行走旷野的，因他的慈爱永远长存。
To him who took his people through the waste land: for his mercy is unchanging for ever.

称谢那击杀大君王的，因他的慈爱永远长存。
To him who overcame great kings: for his mercy is unchanging for ever:

他杀戮有名的君王，因他的慈爱永远长存。
And put noble kings to death: for his mercy is unchanging for ever:

就是杀戮亚摩利王西宏，因他的慈爱永远长存。
Sihon, king of the Amorites: for his mercy is unchanging for ever:

又杀巴珊王噩，因他的慈爱永远长存。
And Og, king of Bashan: for his mercy is unchanging for ever:

他将他们的地赐他的百姓为业，因他的慈爱永远长存。
And gave their land to his people for a heritage: for his mercy is unchanging for ever.

就是赐他的仆人以色列为业，因他的慈爱永远长存。
Even a heritage for his servant Israel: for his mercy is unchanging for ever.

他顾念我们在卑微的地步，因他的慈爱永远长存。
Who kept us in mind when we were in trouble: for his mercy is unchanging for ever.

他救拔我们脱离敌人，因他的慈爱永远长存。
And has taken us out of the hands of our haters: for his mercy is unchanging for ever.

他赐粮食给凡有血气的，因他的慈爱永远长存。
Who gives food to all flesh: for his mercy is unchanging for ever.

你们要称谢天上的神，因他的慈爱永远长存。
O give praise to the God of heaven: for his mercy is unchanging for ever.

我们曾在巴比伦的河边坐下，一追想锡安就哭了。
By the rivers of Babylon we were seated, weeping at the memory of Zion,

我们把琴挂在那里的柳树上。
Hanging our instruments of music on the trees by the waterside.

因为在那里，掳掠我们的要我们唱歌，抢夺我们的，要我们作乐，说，给我们唱一首锡安歌吧。
For there those who had taken us prisoners made request for a song; and those who had taken away all we had gave us orders to be glad, saying, Give us one of the songs of Zion.

我们怎能在外邦唱耶和华的歌呢？
How may we give the Lord's song in a strange land?

耶路撒冷阿，我若忘记你，情愿我的右手忘记技巧。
If I keep not your memory, O Jerusalem, let not my right hand keep the memory of its art.

我若不记念你，若不看耶路撒冷过于我所最喜乐的，情愿我的舌头贴于上膛。
If I let you go out of my thoughts, and if I do not put Jerusalem before my greatest joy, let my tongue be fixed to the roof of my mouth.

耶路撒冷遭难的日子，以东人说，拆毁，拆毁，直拆到根基。耶和华阿求你记念这仇。
O Lord, keep in mind against the children of Edom the day of Jerusalem; how they said, Let it be uncovered, uncovered even to its base.

将要被灭的巴比伦城阿（城原文作女子），报复你象你待我们的，那人便为有福。
O daughter of Babylon, whose fate is destruction; happy is the man who does to you what you have done to us.

拿你的婴孩摔在磐石上的，那人便为有福。
Happy is the man who takes your little ones, crushing them against the rocks.

（大卫的诗。）我要一心称谢你，在诸神面前歌颂你。
<Of David.> I will give you praise with all my heart: I will make melody to you before the gods.

我要向你的圣殿下拜，为你的慈爱和诚实称赞你的名。因你使你的话显为大，过于你所应许的（或作超乎你的名声）。
I will give worship before your holy Temple, praising your name for your mercy and for your unchanging faith: for you have made your word greater than all your name.

我呼求的日子，你就应允我，鼓励我，使我心里有能力。
When my cry came to your ears you gave me an answer, and made me great with strength in my soul.

耶和华阿，地上的君王，都要称谢你，因他们听见了你口中的言语。
All the kings of the earth will give you praise, O Lord, when the words of your mouth come to their ears.

他们要歌颂耶和华的作为，因耶和华大有荣耀。
They will make songs about the ways of the Lord; for great is the glory of the Lord.

耶和华虽高，仍看顾低微的人。他却从远处看出骄傲的人。
Though the Lord is high, he sees those who are low; and he has knowledge from far off of those who are lifted up.

我虽行在患难中，你必将我救活。我的仇敌发怒，你必伸手抵挡他们。你的右手也必救我。
Even when trouble is round me, you will give me life; your hand will be stretched out against the wrath of my haters, and your right hand will be my salvation.

耶和华必成全关乎我的事。耶和华阿，你的慈爱永远长存。求你不要离弃你手所造的。
The Lord will make all things complete for me: O Lord, your mercy is eternal; do not give up the works of your hands.

（大卫的诗，交与伶长。）耶和华阿，你已经鉴察我，认识我。
<To the chief music-maker. A Psalm. Of David.> O Lord, you have knowledge of me, searching out all my secrets.

我坐下，我起来，你都晓得。你从远处知道我的意念。
You have knowledge when I am seated and when I get up, you see my thoughts from far away.

我行路，我躺卧，你都细察，你也深知我一切所行的。
You keep watch over my steps and my sleep, and have knowledge of all my ways.

耶和华阿，我舌头上的话，你没有一句不知道的。
For there is not a word on my tongue which is not clear to you, O Lord.

你在我前后环绕我，按手在我身上。
I am shut in by you on every side, and you have put your hand on me.

这样的知识奇妙，是我不能测的。至高，是我不能及的。
Such knowledge is a wonder greater than my powers; it is so high that I may not come near it.

我往那里去躲避你的灵。我往那里逃躲避你的面。
Where may I go from your spirit? how may I go in flight from you?

我若升到天上，你在那里。我若在阴间下榻，你也在那里。
If I go up to heaven, you are there: or if I make my bed in the underworld, you are there.

我若展开清晨的翅膀，飞到海极居住。
If I take the wings of the morning, and go to the farthest parts of the sea;

就是在那里，你的手必引导我，你的右手，也必扶持我。
Even there will I be guided by your hand, and your right hand will keep me.

我若说，黑暗必定遮蔽我，我周围的亮光必成为黑夜。
If I say, Only let me be covered by the dark, and the light about me be night;

黑暗也不能遮蔽我使你不见，黑夜却如白昼发亮。黑暗和光明，在你看都是一样。
Even the dark is not dark to you; the night is as bright as the day: for dark and light are the same to you.

我的肺腑是你所造的。我在母腹中，你已覆庇我。
My flesh was made by you, and my parts joined together in my mother's body.

我要称谢你，因我受造，奇妙可畏。你的作为奇妙，这是我心深知道的。
I will give you praise, for I am strangely and delicately formed; your works are great wonders, and of this my soul is fully conscious.

我在暗中受造，在地的深处被联络。那时，我的形体并不向你隐藏。
My frame was not unseen by you when I was made secretly, and strangely formed in the lowest parts of the earth.

我未成形的体质，你的眼早已看见了。你所定的日子，我尚未度一日（或作我被造的肢体尚未有其一），你都写在你的册上了。
Your eyes saw my unformed substance; in your book all my days were recorded, even those which were purposed before they had come into being.

神阿，你的意念向我何等宝贵。其数何等众多。
How dear are your thoughts to me, O God! how great is the number of them!

我若数点，比海沙更多。我睡醒的时候，仍和你同在。
If I made up their number, it would be more than the grains of sand; when I am awake, I am still with you.

神阿，你必要杀戮恶人。所以，你们好流人血的，离开我去吧。
If only you would put the sinners to death, O God; go far from me, you men of blood.

因为他们说恶言顶撞你。你的仇敌也妄称你的名。
For they go against you with evil designs, and your haters make sport of your name.

耶和华阿，恨恶你的，我岂不恨恶他们吗？攻击你的，我岂不憎嫌他们吗？
Are not your haters hated by me, O Lord? are not those who are lifted up against you a cause of grief to me?

我切切地恨恶他们，以他们为仇敌。
My hate for them is complete; my thoughts of them are as if they were making war on me.

神阿，求你鉴察我，知道我的心思，试炼我，知道我的意念。
O God, let the secrets of my heart be uncovered, and let my wandering thoughts be tested:

看在我里面有什么恶行没有，引导我走永生的道路。
See if there is any way of sorrow in me, and be my guide in the eternal way.

（大卫的诗，交与伶长。）耶和华阿，求你拯救我脱离凶恶的人，保护我脱离强暴的人。
<To the chief music-maker. A Psalm. Of David.> O Lord, take me out of the power of the evil man; keep me safe from the violent man:

他们心中图谋奸恶，常常聚集要争战。
For their hearts are full of evil designs; and they are ever making ready causes of war.

他们使舌头尖利如蛇，嘴里有虺蛇的毒气。（细拉）
Their tongues are sharp like the tongue of a snake; the poison of snakes is under their lips. (Selah.)

耶和华阿，求你拯救我脱离恶人的手，保护我脱离强暴的人。他们图谋推我跌倒。
O Lord, take me out of the hands of sinners; keep me safe from the violent man: for they are designing my downfall.

骄傲人为我暗设网罗和绳索。他们在路旁铺下网，设下圈套。（细拉）
The men of pride have put secret cords for my feet; stretching nets in my way, so that they may take me with their tricks. (Selah.)

我曾对耶和华说，你是我的神。耶和华阿，求你留心听我恳求的声音。
I have said to the Lord, You are my God: give ear, O Lord, to the voice of my prayer.

主耶和华，我救恩的力量阿，在争战的日子，你遮蔽了我的头。
O Lord God, the strength of my salvation, you have been a cover over my head in the day of the fight.

耶和华阿，求你不要遂恶人的心愿。不要成就他们的计谋，恐怕他们自高。（细拉）
O Lord, give not the wrongdoer his desire; give him no help in his evil designs, or he may be uplifted in pride. (Selah.)

至于那些昂首围困我的人，愿他们嘴唇的奸恶陷害（原文作遮蔽）自己。
As for those who come round me, let their heads be covered by the evil of their lips.

愿火炭落在他们身上。愿他们被丢在火中，抛在深坑里，不能再起来。
Let burning flames come down on them: let them be put into the fire, and into deep waters, so that they may not get up again.

说恶言的人，在地上必坚立不住。祸患必猎取强暴的人，将他打倒。
Let not a man of evil tongue be safe on earth: let destruction overtake the violent man with blow on blow.

我知道耶和华必为困苦人伸冤，必为穷乏人辨屈。
I am certain that the Lord will take care of the cause of the poor, and of the rights of those who are troubled.

义人必要称赞你的名。正直人必住在你面前。
Truly, the upright will give praise to your name: the holy will have a place in your house.

（大卫的诗。）耶和华阿，我曾求告你，求你快快临到我这里。我求告你的时候，愿你留心听我的声音。
<A Psalm. Of David.> Lord, I have made my cry to you; come to me quickly; give ear to my voice, when it goes up to you.

愿我的祷告，如香陈列在你面前。愿我举手祈求，如献晚祭。
Let my prayer be ordered before you like a sweet smell; and let the lifting up of my hands be like the evening offering.

耶和华阿，求你禁止我的口，把守我的嘴。
O Lord, keep a watch over my mouth; keep the door of my lips.

求你不叫我的心，偏向邪恶，以致我和作孽的人同行恶事。也不叫我吃他们的美食。
Keep my heart from desiring any evil thing, or from taking part in the sins of the evil-doers with men who do wrong: and let me have no part in their good things.

任凭义人击打我，这算为仁慈。任凭他责备我，这算为头上的膏油。我的头不要躲闪。正在他们行恶的时候，我仍要祈祷。
Let the upright give me punishment; and let the god-fearing man put me in the right way; but I will not let the oil of sinners come on my head: when they do evil I will give myself to prayer.

他们的审判官，被扔在岩下。众人要听我的话，因为这话甘甜。
When destruction comes to their judges by the side of the rock, they will give ear to my words, for they are sweet.

我们的骨头散在墓旁，好像人耕田，刨地的土块。
Our bones are broken up at the mouth of the underworld, as the earth is broken by the plough.

主耶和华阿，我的眼目仰望你。我投靠你，求你不要将我撇得孤苦。
But my eyes are turned to you, O Lord God: my hope is in you; let not my soul be given up to death.

求你保护我脱离恶人为我设的网罗，和作孽之人的圈套。
Keep me from the net which they have put down for me, and from the designs of the workers of evil.

愿恶人落在自己的网里，我却得以逃脱。
Let the sinners be taken in the nets which they themselves have put down, while I go free.

（大卫在洞里作的训诲诗，乃是祈祷。）我发声哀告耶和华，发声恳求耶和华。
<Maschil. Of David. A prayer when he was in the hole of the rock.> The sound of my cry went up to the Lord; with my voice I made my prayer for grace to the Lord.

我在他面前吐露我的苦情，陈说我的患难。
I put all my sorrows before him; and made clear to him all my trouble.

我的灵在我里面发昏的时候，你知道我的道路。在我行的路上，敌人为我暗设网罗。
When my spirit is overcome, your eyes are on my goings; nets have been secretly placed in the way in which I go.

求你向我右边观看，因为没有人认识我。我无处避难，也没有人眷顾我。
Looking to my right side, I saw no man who was my friend: I had no safe place; no one had any care for my soul.

耶和华阿，我曾向你哀求。我说，你是我的避难所。在活人之地，你是我的福分。
I have made my cry to you, O Lord; I have said, You are my safe place, and my heritage in the land of the living.

求你侧耳听我的呼求，因我落到极卑之地。求你救我脱离逼迫我的人，因为他们比我强盛。
Give ear to my cry, for I am made very low: take me out of the hands of my haters, for they are stronger than I.

求你领我出离被囚之地，我好称赞你的名。义人必环绕我，因为你是用厚恩待我。
Take my soul out of prison, so that I may give praise to your name: the upright will give praise because of me; for you have given me a full reward.

（大卫的诗。）耶和华阿，求你听我的祷告，留心听我的恳求，凭你的信实和公义应允我。
<A Psalm. Of David.> Let my prayer come to you, O Lord; give ear to my requests for your grace; keep faith with me, and give me an answer in your righteousness;

求你不要审问仆人。因为在你面前，凡活着的人，没有一个是义的。
Let not your servant come before you to be judged; for no man living is upright in your eyes.

原来仇敌逼迫我，将我打倒在地，使我住在幽暗之处，像死了许久的人一样。
The evil man has gone after my soul; my life is crushed down to the earth: he has put me in the dark, like those who have long been dead.

所以，我的灵在我里面发昏。我的心在我里面凄惨。
Because of this my spirit is overcome; and my heart is full of fear.

我追想古时之日，思想你的一切作为，默念你手的工作。
I keep in mind the early days of the past, giving thought to all your acts, even to the work of your hands.

我向你举手。我的心渴想你，如干旱之地盼雨一样。（细拉）
My hands are stretched out to you: my soul is turned to you, like a land in need of water. (Selah.)

耶和华阿，求你速速应允我。我心神耗尽。不要向我掩面，免得我像那些下坑的人一样。
Be quick in answering me, O Lord, for the strength of my spirit is gone: let me see your face, so that I may not be like those who go down into the underworld.

求你使我清晨得听你慈爱之言，因我倚靠你。求你使我知道当行的路，因我的心仰望你。
Let the story of your mercy come to me in the morning, for my hope is in you: give me knowledge of the way in which I am to go; for my soul is lifted up to you.

耶和华阿，求你救我脱离我的仇敌。我往你那里藏身。
O Lord, take me out of the hands of my haters; my soul is waiting for you.

求你指教我遵行你的旨意，因你是我的神。你的灵本为善。求你引我到平坦之地。
Give me teaching so that I may do your pleasure; for you are my God: let your good Spirit be my guide into the land of righteousness.

耶和华阿，求你为你的名将我救活。凭你的公义，将我从患难中领出来。
Give me life, O Lord, because of your name; in your righteousness take my soul out of trouble.

凭你的慈爱剪除我的仇敌，灭绝一切苦待我的人，因我是你的仆人。
And in your mercy put an end to my haters, and send destruction on all those who are against my soul; for I am your servant.

（大卫的诗。）耶和华我的磐石，是应当称颂的。他教导我的手争战，教导我的指头打仗。
<A Psalm. Of David.> Praise be to the God of my strength, teaching my hands the use of the sword, and my fingers the art of fighting:

他是我慈爱的主，我的山寨，我的高台，我的救主，我的盾牌，是我所投靠的。他使我的百姓服在我以下。
He is my strength, and my Rock; my high tower, and my saviour; my keeper and my hope: he gives me authority over my people.

耶和华阿，人算什么，你竟认识他。世人算什么，你竟顾念他。
Lord, what is man, that you keep him in mind? or the son of man that you take him into account?

人好像一口气。他的年日，如同影儿快快过去。
Man is like a breath: his life is like a shade which is quickly gone.

耶和华阿，求你使天下垂，亲自降临，摸山，山就冒烟。
Come down, O Lord, from your heavens: at your touch let the mountains give out smoke.

求你发出闪电，使他们四散，射出你的箭，使他们扰乱。
With your storm-flames send them in flight: send out your arrows for their destruction.

求你从上伸手救拔我，救我出离大水，救我脱离外邦人的手。
Put out your hand from on high; make me free, take me safely out of the great waters, and out of the hands of strange men;

他们的口说谎话。他们的右手起假誓。
In whose mouths are false words, and whose right hand is a right hand of deceit.

神阿，我要向你唱新歌，用十弦瑟向你歌颂。
I will make a new song to you, O God; I will make melody to you on an instrument of ten cords.

你是那拯救君王的。你是那救仆人大卫脱离害命之刀的。
It is God who gives salvation to kings; and who kept his servant David from the wounding sword.

求你救拔我，救我脱离外邦人的手。他们的口说谎话。他们的右手起假誓。
Make me free, and take me out of the hands of strange men, in whose mouths are false words, and whose right hand is a right hand of deceit.

我们的儿子，从幼年好像树栽子长大。我们的女儿如同殿角石，是按建宫的样式凿成的。
Our sons are like tall young plants; and our daughters like the shining stones of a king's house;

我们的仓盈满，能出各样的粮食。我们的羊，在田间孳生千万。
Our store-houses are full of all good things; and our sheep give birth to thousands and ten thousands in our fields.

我们的牛驮着满驮，没有人闯进来抢夺，也没有人出去争战。我们的街市上，也没有哭号的声音。
Our oxen are well weighted down; our cows give birth safely; there is no going out, and there is no cry of sorrow in our open places.

遇见这光景的百姓，便为有福。有耶和华为他们的神，这百姓便为有福。
Happy is the nation whose ways are so ordered: yes, happy is the nation whose God is the Lord.

（大卫的赞美诗。）我的神我的王阿，我要尊崇你。我要永永远远称颂你的名。
<A Song of praise. Of David.> Let me give glory to you, O God, my King; and blessing to your name for ever and ever.

我要天天称颂你，也要永永远远赞美你的名。
Every day will I give you blessing, praising your name for ever and ever.

耶和华本为大，该受大赞美。其大无法测度。
Great is the Lord, and greatly to be praised; his power may never be searched out.

这代要对那代颂赞你的作为，也要传扬你的大能。
One generation after another will give praise to your great acts, and make clear the operation of your strength.

我要默念你威严的尊荣，和你奇妙的作为。
My thoughts will be of the honour and glory of your rule, and of the wonder of your works.

人要传说你可畏之事的能力。我也要传扬你的大德。
Men will be talking of the power and fear of your acts; I will give word of your glory.

他们记念你的大恩，就要传出来，并要歌唱你的公义。
Their sayings will be full of the memory of all your mercy, and they will make songs of your righteousness.

耶和华有恩惠，有怜悯，不轻易发怒，大有慈爱。
The Lord is full of grace and pity; not quickly angry, but great in mercy.

耶和华善待万民，他的慈悲，覆庇他一切所造的。
The Lord is good to all men; and his mercies are over all his works.

耶和华阿，你一切所造，的都要称谢你。你的圣民也要称颂你，
All the works of your hands give praise to you, O Lord; and your saints give you blessing.

传说你国的荣耀，谈论你的大能，
Their words will be of the glory of your kingdom, and their talk of your strength;

好叫世人知道你大能的作为，并你国度威严的荣耀。
So that the sons of men may have knowledge of his acts of power, and of the great glory of his kingdom.

你的国是永远的国，你执掌的权柄，存到万代。
Your kingdom is an eternal kingdom, and your rule is through all generations.

凡跌倒的，耶和华将他们扶持。凡被压下的，将他们扶起。
The Lord is the support of all who are crushed, and the lifter up of all who are bent down.

万民都举目仰望你。你随时给他们食物。
The eyes of all men are waiting for you; and you give them their food in its time.

你张手，使有生气的都随愿饱足。
By the opening of your hand, every living thing has its desire in full measure.

耶和华在他一切所行的，无不公义。在他一切所作的，都有慈爱。
The Lord is upright in all his ways, and kind in all his works.

凡求告耶和华的，就是诚心求告他的，耶和华便与他们相近。
The Lord is near all those who give honour to his name; even to all who give honour to him with true hearts.

敬畏他的，他必成就他们的心愿。也必听他们的呼求，拯救他们。
To his worshippers, he will give their desire; their cry comes to his ears, and he gives them salvation.

耶和华保护一切爱他的人，却要灭绝一切的恶人。
The Lord will keep all his worshippers from danger; but he will send destruction on all sinners.

我的口要说出赞美耶和华的话。惟愿凡有血气的，都永永远远称颂他的圣名。
My mouth will give praise to the Lord; let all flesh be blessing his holy name for ever and ever.

你们要赞美耶和华。我的心哪，你要赞美耶和华。
Let the Lord be praised. Give praise to the Lord, O my soul.

我一生要赞美耶和华。我还活的时候要歌颂我的神。
While I have breath I will give praise to the Lord: I will make melody to my God while I have my being.

你们不要倚靠君王，不要倚靠世人。他一点不能帮助。
Put not your faith in rulers, or in the son of man, in whom there is no salvation.

他的气一断，就归回尘土。他所打算的，当日就消灭了。
Man's breath goes out, he is turned back again to dust; in that day all his purposes come to an end.

以雅各的神为帮助，仰望耶和华他神的，这人便为有福。
Happy is the man who has the God of Jacob for his help, whose hope is in the Lord his God:

耶和华造天，地，海，和其中的万物。他守诚实，直到永远。
Who made heaven and earth, the sea, and all things in them; who keeps faith for ever:

他为受屈的伸冤，赐食物与饥饿的。耶和华释放被囚的。
Who gives their rights to those who are crushed down; and gives food to those who are in need of it: the Lord makes the prisoners free;

耶和华开了瞎子的眼睛。耶和华扶起被压下的人。耶和华喜爱义人。
The Lord makes open the eyes of the blind; the Lord is the lifter up of those who are bent down; the Lord is a lover of the upright;

耶和华保护寄居的，扶持孤儿和寡妇，却使恶人的道路弯曲。
The Lord takes care of those who are in a strange land; he gives help to the widow and to the child who has no father; but he sends destruction on the way of sinners.

耶和华要作王，直到永远。锡安哪，你的神要作王，直到万代。你们要赞美耶和华。
The Lord will be King for ever; your God, O Zion, will be King through all generations. Praise be to the Lord.

你们要赞美耶和华，因歌颂我们的神为善为美。赞美的话是合宜的。
Give praise to the Lord; for it is good to make melody to our God; praise is pleasing and beautiful.

耶和华建造耶路撒冷，聚集以色列中被赶散的人。
The Lord is building up Jerusalem; he makes all the outlaws of Israel come together.

他医好伤心的人，裹好他们的伤处。
He makes the broken-hearted well, and puts oil on their wounds.

他数点星宿的数目，一一称它的名。
He sees the number of the stars; he gives them all their names.

我们的主为大，最有能力。他的智慧无法测度。
Great is our Lord, and great his power; there is no limit to his wisdom.

耶和华扶持谦卑人，将恶人倾覆于地。
The Lord gives help to the poor in spirit; but he sends sinners down in shame.

你们要以感谢向耶和华歌唱，用琴向我们的神歌颂。
Make songs of praise to the Lord; make melody to our God with instruments of music.

他用云遮天，为地降雨，使草生长在山上。
By his hand the heaven is covered with clouds and rain is stored up for the earth; he makes the grass tall on the mountains.

他赐食给走兽，和啼叫的小乌鸦。
He gives food to every beast, and to the young ravens in answer to their cry.

他不喜悦马的力大，不喜爱人的腿快。
He has no delight in the strength of a horse; he takes no pleasure in the legs of a man.

耶和华喜爱敬畏他和盼望他慈爱的人。
The Lord takes pleasure in his worshippers, and in those whose hope is in his mercy.

耶路撒冷阿，你要颂赞耶和华。锡安哪，你要赞美你的神。
Give praise to the Lord, O Jerusalem; give praise to your God, O Zion.

因为他坚固了你的门闩，赐福给你中间的儿女。
He has made strong the iron bands of your doors; he has sent blessings on your children inside your walls.

他使你境内平安。用上好的麦子使你满足。
He gives peace in all your land, making your stores full of fat grain.

他发命在地。他的话颁行最快。
He sends out his orders to the earth; his word goes out quickly.

他降雪如羊毛，撒霜如炉灰。
He gives snow like wool; he sends out ice-drops like dust.

他掷下冰雹如碎渣。他发出寒冷，谁能当得起呢？
He sends down ice like raindrops: water is made hard by his cold.

他一出令，这些就都消化。他使风刮起，水便流动。
At the outgoing of his word, the ice is turned to water; when he sends out his wind, there is a flowing of waters.

他将他的道指示雅各，将他的律例典章指示以色列。
He makes his word clear to Jacob, teaching Israel his laws and his decisions.

别国他都没有这样待过。至于他的典章，他们向来没有知道。你们要赞美耶和华。
He has not done these things for any other nation: and as for his laws, they have no knowledge of them. Let the Lord be praised.

你们要赞美耶和华，从天上赞美耶和华，在高处赞美他。
Give praise to the Lord. Let the Lord be praised from the heavens: give him praise in the skies.

他的众使者都要赞美他。他的诸军都要赞美他。
Give praise to him, all you his angels: give praise to him, all his armies.

日头月亮，你们要赞美他。放光的星宿，你们都要赞美他。
Give praise to him, you sun and moon: give praise to him, all you stars of light.

天上的天，和天上的水，你们都要赞美他。
Give praise to him, you highest heavens, and you waters which are over the heavens.

愿这些都赞美耶和华的名。因他一吩咐便都造成。
Let them give praise to the name of the Lord: for he gave the order, and they were made.

他将这些立定，直到永永远远。他定了命，不能废去（废去或作越过）。
He has put them in their places for ever; he has given them their limits which may not be broken.

所有在地上的，大鱼和一切深洋，
Give praise to the Lord from the earth, you great sea-beasts, and deep places:

火与冰雹，雪和雾气，成就他命的狂风，
Fire and rain of ice, snow and mists; storm-wind, doing his word:

大山和小山，结果的树木，和一切香柏树，
Mountains and all hills; fruit-trees and all trees of the mountains:

野兽和一切牲畜，昆虫和飞鸟，
Beasts and all cattle; insects and winged birds:

世上的君王和万民，首领和世上一切审判官，
Kings of the earth, and all peoples; rulers and all judges of the earth:

少年人和处女，老年人和孩童，都当赞美耶和华。
Young men and virgins; old men and children:

愿这些都赞美耶和华的名。因为独有他的名被尊崇。他的荣耀在天地之上。
Let them give glory to the name of the Lord: for his name only is to be praised: his kingdom is over the earth and the heaven.

他将他百姓的角高举，因此他（因此他或作他使）一切圣民以色列人，就是与他相近的百姓，都赞美他。你们要赞美耶和华。
He has put on high the horn of his people, for the praise of all his saints; even the children of Israel, a people which is near to him. Let the Lord be praised.

你们要赞美耶和华，向耶和华唱新歌，在圣民的会中赞美他。
Let the Lord be praised. Make a new song to the Lord, let his praise be in the meeting of his saints.

愿以色列因造他的主欢喜。愿锡安的民，因他们的王快乐。
Let Israel have joy in his maker; let the children of Zion be glad in their King.

愿他们跳舞赞美他的名，击鼓弹琴歌颂他。
Let them give praise to his name in the dance: let them make melody to him with instruments of brass and corded instruments of music.

因为耶和华喜爱他的百姓。他要用救恩当作谦卑人的妆饰。
For the Lord has pleasure in his people: he gives the poor in spirit a crown of salvation.

愿圣民因所得的荣耀高兴。愿他们在床上欢呼。
Let the saints have joy and glory: let them give cries of joy on their beds.

愿他们口中称赞神为高，手里有两刃的刀。
Let the high praises of God be in their mouths, and a two-edged sword in their hands;

为要报复列邦，刑罚万民。
To give the nations the reward of their sins, and the peoples their punishment;

要用链子捆他们的君王，用铁镣锁他们的大臣。
To put their kings in chains, and their rulers in bands of iron;

要在他们身上施行所记录的审判。他的圣民都有这荣耀。你们要赞美耶和华。
To give them the punishment which is in the holy writings: this honour is given to all his saints. Praise be to the Lord.

你们要赞美耶和华，在神的圣所赞美他，在他显能力的穹苍赞美他。
Let the Lord be praised. Give praise to God in his holy place: give him praise in the heaven of his power.

要因他大能的作为赞美他，按着他极美的大德赞美他。
Give him praise for his acts of power: give him praise in the measure of his great strength.

要用角声赞美他，鼓瑟弹琴赞美他。
Give him praise with the sound of the horn: give him praise with corded instruments of music.

击鼓跳舞赞美他，用丝弦的乐器，和箫的声音赞美他。
Give him praise with instruments of brass and in the dance: give him praise with horns and corded instruments.

用大响的钹赞美他，用高声的钹赞美他。
Give him praise with the loud brass: give him praise with the high-sounding brass.

凡有气息的，都要赞美耶和华。你们要赞美耶和华。
Let everything which has breath give praise to the Lord. Let the Lord be praised.uts oil on their wounds.

他数点星宿的数目，一一称它的名。
He sees the number of the stars; he gives them all their names.

我们的主为大，最有能力。他的智慧无法测度。
Great is our Lord, and great his power; there is no limit to his wisdom.

耶和华扶持谦卑人，将恶人倾覆于地。
The Lord gives help to the poor in spirit; but he sends sinners down in shame.

你们要以感谢向耶和华歌唱，用琴向我们的神歌颂。
Make songs of praise to the Lord; make melody to our God with instruments of music.

他用云遮天，为地降雨，使草生长在山上。
By his hand the heaven is covered with clouds and rain is stored up for the earth; he makes the grass tall on the mountains.

他赐食给走兽，和啼叫的小乌鸦。
He gives food to every beast, and to the young ravens in answer to their cry.

他不喜悦马的力大，不喜爱人的腿快。
He has no delight in the strength of a horse; he takes no pleasure in the legs of a man.

耶和华喜爱敬畏他和盼望他慈爱的人。
The Lord takes pleasure in his worshippers, and in those whose hope is in his mercy.

耶路撒冷阿，你要颂赞耶和华。锡安哪，你要赞美你的神。
Give praise to the Lord, O Jerusalem; give praise to your God, O Zion.

因为他坚固了你的门闩，赐福给你中间的儿女。
He has made strong the iron bands of your doors; he has sent blessings on your children inside your walls.

他使你境内平安。用上好的麦子使你满足。
He gives peace in all your land, making your stores full of fat grain.

他发命在地。他的话颁行最快。
He sends out his orders to the earth; his word goes out quickly.

他降雪如羊毛，撒霜如炉灰。
He gives snow like wool; he sends out ice-drops like dust.

他掷下冰雹如碎渣。他发出寒冷，谁能当得起呢？
He sends down ice like raindrops: water is made hard by his cold.

他一出令，这些就都消化。他使风刮起，水便流动。
At the outgoing of his word, the ice is turned to water; when he sends out his wind, there is a flowing of waters.

他将他的道指示雅各，将他的律例典章指示以色列。
He makes his word clear to Jacob, teaching Israel his laws and his decisions.

别国他都没有这样待过。至于他的典章，他们向来没有知道。你们要赞美耶和华。
He has not done these things for any other nation: and as for his laws, they have no knowledge of them. Let the Lord be praised.

你们要赞美耶和华，从天上赞美耶和华，在高处赞美他。
Give praise to the Lord. Let the Lord be praised from the heavens: give him praise in the skies.

他的众使者都要赞美他。他的诸军都要赞美他。
Give praise to him, all you his angels: give praise to him, all his armies.

日头月亮，你们要赞美他。放光的星宿，你们都要赞美他。
Give praise to him, you sun and moon: give praise to him, all you stars of light.

天上的天，和天上的水，你们都要赞美他。
Give praise to him, you highest heavens, and you waters which are over the heavens.

愿这些都赞美耶和华的名。因他一吩咐便都造成。
Let them give praise to the name of the Lord: for he gave the order, and they were made.

他将这些立定，直到永永远远。他定了命，不能废去（废去或作越过）。
He has put them in their places for ever; he has given them their limits which may not be broken.

所有在地上的，大鱼和一切深洋，
Give praise to the Lord from the earth, you great sea-beasts, and deep places:

火与冰雹，雪和雾气，成就他命的狂风，
Fire and rain of ice, snow and mists; storm-wind, doing his word:

大山和小山，结果的树木，和一切香柏树，
Mountains and all hills; fruit-trees and all trees of the mountains:

野兽和一切牲畜，昆虫和飞鸟，
Beasts and all cattle; insects and winged birds:

世上的君王和万民，首领和世上一切审判官，
Kings of the earth, and all peoples; rulers and all judges of the earth:

少年人和处女，老年人和孩童，都当赞美耶和华。
Young men and virgins; old men and children:

愿这些都赞美耶和华的名。因为独有他的名被尊崇。他的荣耀在天地之上。
Let them give glory to the name of the Lord: for his name only is to be praised: his kingdom is over the earth and the heaven.

他将他百姓的角高举，因此他（因此他或作他使）一切圣民以色列人，就是与他相近的百姓，都赞美他。你们要赞美耶和华。
He has put on high the horn of his people, for the praise of all his saints; even the children of Israel, a people which is near to him. Let the Lord be praised.

你们要赞美耶和华，向耶和华唱新歌，在圣民的会中赞美他。
Let the Lord be praised. Make a new song to the Lord, let his praise be in the meeting of his saints.

愿以色列因造他的主欢喜。愿锡安的民，因他们的王快乐。
Let Israel have joy in his maker; let the children of Zion be glad in their King.

愿他们跳舞赞美他的名，击鼓弹琴歌颂他。
Let them give praise to his name in the dance: let them make melody to him with instruments of brass and corded instruments of music.

因为耶和华喜爱他的百姓。他要用救恩当作谦卑人的妆饰。
For the Lord has pleasure in his people: he gives the poor in spirit a crown of salvation.

愿圣民因所得的荣耀高兴。愿他们在床上欢呼。
Let the saints have joy and glory: let them give cries of joy on their beds.

愿他们口中称赞神为高，手里有两刃的刀。
Let the high praises of God be in their mouths, and a two-edged sword in their hands;

为要报复列邦，刑罚万民。
To give the nations the reward of their sins, and the peoples their punishment;

要用链子捆他们的君王，用铁镣锁他们的大臣。
To put their kings in chains, and their rulers in bands of iron;

要在他们身上施行所记录的审判。他的圣民都有这荣耀。你们要赞美耶和华。
To give them the punishment which is in the holy writings: this honour is given to all his saints. Praise be to the Lord.

你们要赞美耶和华，在神的圣所赞美他，在他显能力的穹苍赞美他。
Let the Lord be praised. Give praise to God in his holy place: give him praise in the heaven of his power.

要因他大能的作为赞美他，按着他极美的大德赞美他。
Give him praise for his acts of power: give him praise in the measure of his great strength.

要用角声赞美他，鼓瑟弹琴赞美他。
Give him praise with the sound of the horn: give him praise with corded instruments of music.

击鼓跳舞赞美他，用丝弦的乐器，和箫的声音赞美他。
Give him praise with instruments of brass and in the dance: give him praise with horns and corded instruments.

用大响的钹赞美他，用高声的钹赞美他。
Give him praise with the loud brass: give him praise with the high-sounding brass.

凡有气息的，都要赞美耶和华。你们要赞美耶和华。
Let everything which has breath give praise to the Lord. Let the Lord be praised.
